# Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Potema must be stopped.** | |

| Reward: | Leveled gold, [Shield of Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield_of_Solitude "Skyrim:Shield of Solitude") |

The Wolf Queen, awakened

## Quick Walkthrough

1. After receiving the letter from the courier, speak to [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard").
2. Speak to [Styrr](/wiki/Skyrim:Styrr "Skyrim:Styrr").
3. Fight through the underground tunnels.
4. Defeat [Queen Potema and Potema's Remains](/wiki/Skyrim:Queen_Potema "Skyrim:Queen Potema").
5. Retrieve [Potema's Skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Potema%27s_Skull "Skyrim:Potema's Skull") from the throne.
6. Give the remains to Styrr.
7. Return to Falk.

### The Unbound

After you complete [The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf"), you soon discover that your battle with Potema is not over. Once you have leveled up after interrupting the binding ritual, a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") will approach you outside of Solitude with a [letter from Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Letter from Falk Firebeard"). The letter warns you of an impending threat and requests that you return to Solitude. When you get there, Falk will inform you that Potema has indeed escaped. He asks you to speak with Styrr, a priest of [Arkay](/wiki/Lore:Arkay "Lore:Arkay"), as he can provide you with more guidance on how to secure the threat.

### The Wolf Queen and You

Styrr is located in Solitude's [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)"). You should probably ask him exactly what you are getting yourself into with Potema. Potema is the granddaughter of [Uriel Septim II](/wiki/Lore:Uriel_Septim_II "Lore:Uriel Septim II"), and former Queen of Solitude, and was quite intent on becoming Empress. A formidable necromancer, she had raised armies of dead led by [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") to help her. Since she had not achieved her corporeal form during the summoning, she has fled to a place of the dead, her Catacombs. Because you were present at Potema's summoning, there is now a strange connection between the two of you, and it must be you that deals with her. To keep Potema from returning fully, you must find her remains and bring them to Styrr to be sanctified. To assist you, Styrr gives you the key to the catacombs, and the spell [Turn Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Turn_Undead_(spell) "Skyrim:Turn Undead (spell)").

### The Wolf's Den

*"You've arrived at last."*

The entrance to the catacombs is in the [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines"). When you arrive in the temple, go to the back, past the pews, and on your left will be some stairs going down. Take the stairs, and you will be confronted with a locked iron gate, which can only be unlocked using the key Styrr gave you. Through here you will see the hole one of Potema's servants created into Potema's Catacombs. The dungeon is filled with Potema's minions: leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and vampires. The dungeon itself is very linear, and proceeding through it is a fairly simple endeavor.

Upon entering, the voice of Potema calls to you: *"You've arrived at last. The hero/heroine who prevented me from being bound returns to my fold. I have much to thank you for, little one. When you die I will raise you and you can take your place by my side."* The iron gate that previously barred your path is opened once Potema finishes speaking. Proceed forward until you reach a room at the bottom of a set of stairs with purple flammable liquid on the floor. There is a table in the center of this room, with a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Surfeit of Thieves](/wiki/Skyrim:Surfeit_of_Thieves "Skyrim:Surfeit of Thieves")*.

A draugr rising from the water.

You will eventually reach what seems like a dead end, but there is a lever to open the path forward. Activate the lever, and the stone wall in front of you will start to revolve. Waiting will reveal that there is a door opening barred by an iron bar gate cut out in the rotating wall. If you throw the lever at just the right moment, you can stop the revolving wheel as the gate is opening.

### Potema's Refuge

Walking forward will bring you to a room with three additional revolving-stone doorways and three corresponding levers. Activating the first lever in line will stop and start the first revolving door, etc. Stop all three doors when the entrance is open to you, and walk forward. These rotating doors may slip over time so it's a one way trip past this point (or you can keep them spinning and run through carefully).

You will come to a room with a "sleeping" draugr in a throne near the back of the room and an accompanying vampire. The vampire will approach you and speak before attacking: *"You've come far, mortal. No doubt you seek to enter Potema's Sanctum. I can see to that. We'll need plenty of fresh corpses to rebuild her army, you see."* The draugr will now rise from the throne. The key to Potema's Sanctum is found on the body of the vampire (another copy of the key is found on the armrest of the draugr's throne). Loot it to avoid picking the master lock to Potema's Sanctum, which is the final area of the dungeon.

*"No doubt you seek to enter Potema's Sanctum."*

### Potema's Sanctum

*"Serve me in death."*

Proceeding forward will bring you to a room full of dead draugr, a dead vampire and a locked iron gate. Potema's voice will speak out to you: *"Not much further. Come, little thing. Serve me in death."* The iron gate will then unlock, and Potema will reanimate the vampire and two of the draugr in the room. Defeat them, then continue. In the hallway before the final encounter, there are two [resist shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Shock "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Shock") potions on the shelf near the door. Take them; you will need them to protect yourself against Potema. You will eventually come to a room with a floating spirit and tombs scattered around the perimeter and center of the room. This is the boss fight.

### Defeating Potema

*"You've come far, mortal, but can you stand against my inner council? Let's see!"*

Again, you will hear Potema's voice: *"You've come far, mortal, but can you stand against my inner council? Let's see!"* She will radiate bolts of electricity and rotate the bolts, dealing shock damage to those the bolts of electricity hit. It is advisable to consume potions which give you Resist Shock - such as those in the antechamber. During the fight, she will mock you, *"Don't applaud yourself too soon, worm!"* and spur on her minions, *"Rip the eyes from his/her head!"*. Arrows will not affect Potema, but magic will. Potema will also release draugr from their tombs to attack you. Some of the draugr are warlocks and can summon [frost atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Frost Atronach") to join the fight. After each wave of defeated draugr, Potema will reanimate some of them, and will release more draugr, as well. Each wave of draugr you defeat will make Potema weaker. Keep killing the draugr, and the spirit of Potema will eventually recede into the locked room opposite where you came in.

Follow the spirit of Potema, and Potema's Ghostly Remains will appear, ready to fight you. The apparition respawns and has to be defeated several times. It can also resurrect the draugr you just killed in the last room so watch for attacks from behind. After defeating the apparition, you will see that there is a seat with a skull on it. This skull is Potema's Remains. Take Potema's Skull, and loot the chest. Inside the chest is the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") [*Legend of Krately House*](/wiki/Skyrim:Legend_of_Krately_House "Skyrim:Legend of Krately House"). Exit the room.

Potema's Remains at her throne.

### The Unholy Remains

There are only two more enemies between you and the exit at this point, two draugr, one higher level than the other. They are found seated in facing alcoves with a short pillar in the middle of the hall between them. On the pillar is a helmet or some other piece of loot. If you take this bait, the draugr awaken and attack you. You can ignore them and walk past (the object on the pillar is usually low-level), or deal with them individually. A short distance after this, you pass through a door and emerge on a mountain overlooking a docked ship in Solitude. There is an unlocked chest with random loot to your immediate left as you emerge onto the mountain ledge and a random potion to the right of the chest and a random helmet on the rock above. Travel to Solitude and go to the Hall of the Dead. There, speak with Styrr and he will gratefully accept the remains. He goes off to bless the remains, and all there is left to do now is to report to Falk Firebeard. Returning the remains will count as [assisting the people of Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Haafingar "Skyrim:Thane of Haafingar").

### The Shield of Solitude

Travel to the Blue Palace and speak to Falk, where he will speak on behalf of the jarl in expressing his gratitude. Your reward is gold and the [Shield of Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield_of_Solitude "Skyrim:Shield of Solitude"). The quest concludes here.

After the release of the Anniversary Edition and with the [Bone Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Wolf "Skyrim:Bone Wolf") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, you will receive another [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Bolgeir_Bearclaw "Skyrim:Letter from Bolgeir Bearclaw") by courier once this quest has been completed. Reading this letter will trigger the next quest, [Let Sleeping Wolves Lie](/wiki/Skyrim:Let_Sleeping_Wolves_Lie "Skyrim:Let Sleeping Wolves Lie").

## Notes

- The [Shield of Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield_of_Solitude "Skyrim:Shield of Solitude") that is received as reward for this quest has a unique Resist Magic enchantment that can be learned through disenchantment, and can be stacked with the regular Resist Magic in double enchantments to create a single item with 45% magic resistance.
- Reading Falk's note will not trigger a quest in your Journal, and no quest marker will appear, until you speak to him. However, reading the note is still a requisite for even being able to speak to him about the quest.

## Bugs

- In order to receive the [Letter from Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Letter from Falk Firebeard"), you must gain a level after completing [The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf"). Leveling must happen away from Solitude. If you have already reached level 81, the only way to acquire the letter and activate this quest is to steal it from Falk.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, addresses this issue. The patch introduces a new feature removing the level limit, allowing potentially unlimited level-ups.
  -  This issue has been addressed by the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"); version 1.3.1 alters the requirement to simply changing locations (i.e. leaving the Palace) after 7 in-game days. Use `show USLEEPMS06StartDay` and ensure it is lower than "Days Passed" statistic.

- The courier will occasionally not appear at all to deliver the [Letter from Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Letter from Falk Firebeard"), regardless of how long you wait. If this occurs, complete any other action which could cause the courier to appear (for example, a different quest), and the courier will deliver the note then instead, alongside the note for the other quest. You might notice a delay in the speech when this occurs, just allow a minute or so for the conversation to time out, and the note should appear in your inventory. **?**

- Falk Firebeard has the Letter from Falk Firebeard in his inventory from the start of the game. It can be pickpocketed but is then unable to be dropped as it is tagged as a quest item.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.

- The Letter from Falk Firebeard may not always be removed from your inventory at the conclusion of the quest and will remain behind as an unremovable quest item. **?**
  -  Use the console command `player.removeitem D91D1 1` to remove the letter.

- Backing out of conversation with Styrr too early can block quest progress.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.5, fixes this bug.

- When fighting Potema's three waves of summoned draugr, all three waves may not spawn, leaving the quest stuck.
  - Reloading from a previous save prior to entering the room is the only way to correct the issue.

- After defeating Potema's inner council, the door to Potema's throne might not open.
  -  Use the console command `TCL` to no-clip through the door. You will skip the Potema battle but you can complete the quest.

- The room with the draugr may not load properly. The draugr waves will load, but the room is missing visual assets. The room may be very dark and filled with green mist. Potema's lightning attack does not function. The final door may also be missing.
  - Exiting the zone and re-entering should load the room assets properly. Potema will load and activate, and the final door will load. Any draugr previously killed will remain dead.

- One of the draugr may get knocked through the non-door to Potema's Remains, or be teleported there on loading a save, making it impossible to kill it and leaving the quest stuck (you can tell by the red icon on your compass behind the door). **?**
  - Try conjuring a creature on the other side of the door by facing the door up close and casting the spell.
  -  Use the console command `TCL` to no-clip through the door and defeat the draugr.

- If you have reanimated any of the draugr in the room, Potema's spirit will not recede through the locked door, nor will the door be opened until this very last draugr has also crumbled to the ground. **?**

- The bar on the door after you collect Potema's Remains may be unresponsive even though the door behind it opens.
  - Backtrack through Potema's Sanctum and enter Potema's Refuge. Then re-enter Potema's Sanctum again. The bar should now operate normally.

- Potema's Skull may not be "active", making it impossible to pick it up and complete the quest.
  - Save and reload. The skull should be near where Potema's remains have fallen (or where it would have rolled from the throne).
  - Using the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout on the skull may fix this.

- When you take Potema's Skull, the quest marker will point you back the way you came, not through the door behind her throne.

- Sometimes after defeating Potema's summoned draugr in the first room where she is encountered, her ghostly remains will not appear to fight you and you are able to take the remains and finish the quest anyway.
  -  You can make her appear by the command `enable 00103499`.

- At the end of the quest, if you back out of dialogue before [Styrr](/wiki/Skyrim:Styrr "Skyrim:Styrr") has said his last line, the quest may not be able to be completed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

- At the end of the quest, if you engage in dialogue with [Styrr](/wiki/Skyrim:Styrr "Skyrim:Styrr") before [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard"), the quest may not be able to be completed.
  -  Using `setstage ms06 150`,or closing and restarting the game, then speaking to Falk, may allow the quest to advance.

## Quest Stages

| The Wolf Queen Awakened (MS06) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 50 |  | Potema has been summoned from beyond the grave and is gathering power. Falk has sent me to Styrr to get the key to Potema's Catacombs. *Objective 50:* Speak to Styrr |
| 100 |  | Potema has been summoned from beyond the grave and is gathering power. Styrr has given me the key to Potema's Catacombs. I must enter the catacombs and prevent Potema from fully resurrecting by acquiring her bones. *Objective 100:* Defeat Potema |
| 125 |  | *Objective 125:* Retrieve Potema's remains |
| 150 |  | Potema has been summoned from beyond the grave. I've defeated her in the Catacombs and retrieved her bones. I must return them to Styrr for blessing and tell Falk Potema has been defeated. *Objective 150:* Return to Falk Firebeard  *Objective 155:* Give Potema's remains to Styrr |
| 250 | ☑ | I have defeated Potema and been rewarded by Falk Firebeard. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 5, 10, 60, 160, 170, 190.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MS06 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MS06`.

Words of Power, Way of Voice

## Radiant Options

This quest can send you to *almost* any dungeon or dragon lair that contains a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"). The list of possible values of `Dungeon` is:

| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Bonestrewn Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonestrewn_Crest "Skyrim:Bonestrewn Crest") | [Ancient's Ascent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient%27s_Ascent "Skyrim:Ancient's Ascent") [Shriekwind Bastion](/wiki/Skyrim:Shriekwind_Bastion "Skyrim:Shriekwind Bastion") [Sunderstone Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunderstone_Gorge "Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge") | [Kilkreath Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsaken_Cave "Skyrim:Forsaken Cave") [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins") [Shearpoint](/wiki/Skyrim:Shearpoint "Skyrim:Shearpoint") [Silverdrift Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverdrift_Lair "Skyrim:Silverdrift Lair") [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud") | [Dead Crone Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Crone_Rock "Skyrim:Dead Crone Rock") "Skyrim:Mount Anthor") |

The list of word walls you will *not* be sent to includes the following, most of which have an associated quest. In addition to those listed here, no Dawnguard or Dragonborn word walls will ever be targeted by this quest except Arcwind Point.

| Location | Shout | Quest |
| --- | --- | --- |

## Detailed Walkthrough

After completing [The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller"), you can talk to [Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir") and tell him that you would like to learn more about the Voice. He will respond:

:   *"You have learned so much already, Dragonborn. Growing your gift too quickly would be dangerous. But there are many Words of Power in Skyrim, carved in the Dragon tongue. Even from here, we can feel the Thu'um resonate from them. Finding these lost Words would be a sufficient test, to temper your abilities with experience. Ask when you are ready to search."*

Thereafter, you can ask him whether the Greybeards have located any words of power. He has two possible replies:

:   *"There is only silence right now. Perhaps later we will hear one of the lost Words."*
:   *"We have felt the whisper of a Word. Give me your map, and I will show you where its echo can be found."*

The latter response will cause the location of the word wall to be marked on your map, and you will be given a new quest objective.

This quest can be repeated multiple times, and it can also be active simultaneously with the other word wall quest, [Shout - learn about word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Shout_-_learn_about_word_wall "Skyrim:Shout - learn about word wall"). Both quests can even point you to the same location as the other. However, if you choose to [kill](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(quest) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (quest)") [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)") for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades"), this quest is no longer available.

## Notes

- If you have *[Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")* installed, Arngeir won't help you learn any Words of Power on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").

## Bugs

- If sent to [Arcwind Point](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcwind_Point "Skyrim:Arcwind Point"), finding the word wall may not mark the quest as completed in your journal. Arcwind Point may be given as a destination even when the word wall has already been found, preventing progress in the quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.1a, fixes this bug.
  -  Using the command `SetStage FreeFormHighHrothgarA 20` will end the quest and allow you to acquire another quest normally. Setting Arcwind Point as cleared via `SetLocationCleared fd685 1` will prevent getting sent there again.
- If you learn a word from a different word wall from the one that Arngeir points you to before visiting the quest-marked one, the test may be prematurely logged complete. For instance, after being directed to [Shearpoint](/wiki/Skyrim:Shearpoint "Skyrim:Shearpoint") by Arngeir, visiting [Lost Tongue Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Tongue_Overlook "Skyrim:Lost Tongue Overlook") instead can complete the quest. This is another possible solution for the Arcwind Point bug mentioned above.

## Quest Stages

| The Words of Power (FreeformHighHrothgarA) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Find the Word of Power in <Alias=Dungeon> |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 20.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformHighHrothgarA stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformHighHrothgarA`.

# Skyrim:The World-Eater's Eyrie

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Main.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Main.png) | **Battle through [Skuldafn](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuldafn "Skyrim:Skuldafn") to reach [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin")'s portal to [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Odahviing](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing") |
| Location(s): | [Skuldafn](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuldafn "Skyrim:Skuldafn") |
| Reward: | [Nahkriin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nahkriin_(item) "Skyrim:Nahkriin (item)"), Word for the [Storm Call](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Call "Skyrim:Storm Call") shout |
| ID: | MQ303 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen") | **Next →** [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(quest) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (quest)") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen") | | → Next | [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(quest) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (quest)") | | |

Alduin's portal to Sovngarde

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Set [Odahviing](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing") free.
2. Talk to Odahviing.
3. Reach Alduin's portal to [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)").
4. Enter Sovngarde.

#### Preparation

You cannot take any followers with you on the final two quests, so not only can they not fight alongside you, they cannot carry your burdens. Also, you can never come back here, so you need to take anything you want (particularly the unique items) in your one visit, making carrying space a concern. You will likely be of a high level when completing this quest, resulting in the loot being of higher quality, but better quality is penalized with higher weights.

Only take the bare essentials, strip yourself of anything you don't normally use, though bear in mind you will face some tough fights, so if you rely on food or potions to heal you will need to bring enough. One set of armor, one melee weapon setup (one hand and shield, dual wield, or two handed), and one ranged weapon, should be all you carry.

The [Dremora Butler](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Butler "Skyrim:Dremora Butler")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), [Dremora merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Market "Skyrim:Black Market")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), [the Steed Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Steed_Stone "Skyrim:The Steed Stone") power, and the [Extra Pockets](/wiki/Skyrim:Extra_Pockets "Skyrim:Extra Pockets") perk from the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") skill can all help to provide some relief. Also consider using the Twin Souls perk from Conjuration to at least have twice as many summoned entities. The Spectral Assassin spell will work well, and Rieklings might randomly join you to combat enemies; both can respectively be unlocked from 'Bound Until Death' and 'The Chief of Thirsk Hall'.

### Set Odahviing Free

In order to free Odahviing, talk to the [Whiterun guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard") standing on the second floor (there is a stone staircase near where the jarl is standing). After a short discussion, the guard will release Odahviing for you. You can also pull the chain to release the dragon yourself without talking to the guard, which is useful if the guard is incapacitated or there is a [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime#Bounties "Skyrim:Crime") on your head. Tell Odahviing you're ready to travel and he will fly you directly to [Skuldafn](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuldafn "Skyrim:Skuldafn").

### Upon Arrival

Skuldafn overview

Upon arriving at the Skuldafn courtyard, you'll encounter two dragons and multiple [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). Battle or sneak your way past them to enter the temple complex. The two Towers (North and South) have only minor loot and won't get you any closer to the Temple itself. If you have a high enough sneak skill, it is possible to sneak past all enemies, including the dragons. It is also possible, though tedious, to scale the mountain beside you as high as you can go, and jump along the mountainside until you reach the temple. At this point you can drop down and sneak through the [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") at the base of the mountain.

### Skuldafn Temple

After entering the Temple area, you come to a large chamber with draugr. Be careful of the [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") in the western pathway. Continuing leads you to the first puzzle in [Skuldafn](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuldafn "Skyrim:Skuldafn"), which is used to open two doorways. The puzzle consists of three pillars, each separated by a wall, and a switch between the pillars and the doorways. Each pillar has three pictographs: **[Eagle, Snake, and Whale](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Totems#Totem_Symbols "Skyrim:Puzzle Totems")**. On the walls beside the two outside pillars are matching pictographs for those pillars. The west pillar is a **Whale** and the east is a **Snake**. Set the outer pillars so that the pictographs face each other (e.g., **Snake** faces **Snake**). Above each doorway are more pictographs. Above the east doorway is an **Eagle**. This way just leads to a treasure chest and a collapsed wall. Above the west doorway is a snake, which leads to the destination. Face the pictograph on the central pillar that matches the desired door to face north, toward the doors. Pull the lever to open door (with your back to the lever, you should see Eagle, Eagle, Eagle to open and close the dead-end door. With your back to the lever, you should see Eagle, Snake, Eagle to open and close the progressing door. You must close one door before you can open the other).

The next small room is full of draugr, and the following one has multiple [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") who made good use of their webbing to block a door and cover a chest.

The second puzzle room is solved by **Whale—Snake—Eagle** (upper level left, middle lower level, upper level right), with the solutions for the first and third shown above them and the second behind the platform. A chest can also be found behind the platform. [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") can be used from the platform to bypass the puzzle. Enter the door to go to another section of [Skuldafn Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuldafn_Temple "Skyrim:Skuldafn Temple").

Take out the draugr and keep moving (there isn't much loot around). Cross the bridge (from its eastern entry to the west, seen from entrance) but be careful of the [pressure plate trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") at the doorway to the next room. Activating it releases a lantern that lights up the [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick") ahead and also triggers a dart trap. Go up the staircase to meet three draugr, which can be dispatched easily with another oil slick and lantern. Pull the lever near the oil (in a small window) to open the gate on the other side of the room. Don't forget the chest (by the other window).

Follow the wide tunnel, grabbing the contents of the chest on the right side. Be careful when you reach the large oil slick, as there is another lantern poised over it that will drop if you step on the pressure plate in front. It is a useful way to dispose of upcoming high-level draugr; by running away and leading him into it.

You will then arrive at a [puzzle door](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Puzzle_Door "Skyrim:Traps") guarded by a leveled draugr or [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") carrying the [diamond claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Diamond_Claw "Skyrim:Diamond Claw") needed to open it. The combination to the door is, from top to bottom, **Fox—Moth—Dragon**; this can be seen by examining the claw in your inventory. The next two rooms (the first large, the next small) are basically empty except for a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"), which teaches you a word for the [Storm Call](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Call "Skyrim:Storm Call") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). Also, just before the door to exit is a room to the right. There are some hidden [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems") in a pot on a shelf to the right: a flawless emerald, a ruby, and a diamond hidden by a linen wrap.

### Dragon Priest

Nahkriin guards the portal at Skuldafn, flanked by two dragons

You will end up on a large rocky platform, above where you first entered Skuldafn. Defeat the [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") who are there to meet you, (Hint: Unrelenting Force will be useful here) and take the wooden platform ahead of you (from where you exited the Temple) to go down a small tower that has some good loot on shelves and a large chest at the bottom. Returning to the top, you may notice two dragons above you, perched on columns. This is where you need to be to finish the quest. But before you can enter Alduin's portal to [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)"), you must get past a [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") named [Nahkriin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nahkriin_(creature) "Skyrim:Nahkriin (creature)"). This dragon priest can be tough if you don't take the fight to him. Additionally, if you engage the two nearby dragons at the same time, the fight can be much more difficult. However, the two dragons may not move from their perches or become hostile. When you reach the top of the stairs Nahkriin will notice you and make his way toward [his staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest_Staff_(Nahkriin) "Skyrim:Dragon Priest Staff (Nahkriin)"). It's best to start your assault immediately. He doesn't attack until he gets his staff, so get to him quickly. After Nahkriin grabs his staff, he'll turn around to face you. Be careful with this one as his staff does 50 [shock damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Shock_Damage "Skyrim:Shock Damage") per second. Any [shock resistance](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Shock "Skyrim:Resist Shock") potions or enchanted apparel you have would be useful now. He doesn't start off with full health, so if you jumped on attacking him before he grabbed his staff you should be able to dispatch him in short time. He can also be pushed off the ledge, and will fall to his death. After defeating Nahkriin, pick up his staff and [mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Nahkriin_(item) "Skyrim:Nahkriin (item)") and activate the Dragon Seal.

Alternatively, you can bypass the fight by getting to the portal before Nahkriin can remove his staff. This can be achieved with the [Slow Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Slow_Time "Skyrim:Slow Time") shout, although you won't be able to collect his [mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Nahkriin_(item) "Skyrim:Nahkriin (item)"), which will make it impossible to complete the untracked quest to collect all the dragon priest masks.

## Notes

- If this quest is active, every dragon that you encounter on the landscape while traveling will shout at you, *"Skuldafn fen kos dinok."* (Skuldafn will be [your] death).
- Sometimes the Whiterun Guard who releases Odahviing dies in battle. It is also possible that the guard will repeat the *"Wait... I know you"* line instead of releasing Odahviing. In these cases, you must pull the chain yourself to release Odahviing.
- If you can get between Nahkriin and his staff he won't attack you, as his focus is entirely on removing it. You can proceed to kill him though.
- If you kill Nahkriin before he is able to retrieve his staff you do not need to remove and replace it; you can simply walk into the portal.
- The portal begins to close as soon as the staff is taken out of the platform hole. It is possible to kill Nahkriin immediately after he takes the staff, loot him for his mask and staff, and then jump into the portal before it fully closes (thereby keeping the powerful staff).
- The journal entry states that Skuldafn is in the Jerall Mountains, though it is actually in the Velothi Mountains.

## Bugs

- When setting Odahviing free, if you talk to the guard before allowing [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") to complete his interactions, Odahviing will become hostile and you won't be able to talk to him.
  -  This can be fixed by opening the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"), selecting Odahviing, and entering `stopcombat`.
- Balgruuf's and Irileth's last lines are barely audible.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, addresses this issue. They needed a sound override for you to be able to hear them better.
- When traveling to Skuldafn, after the loading screen, you can become stuck on a black screen. **?**
  -  Load a previous save (prior to mounting Odahviing), open the console, enter `cow 278dd 47 -10` to teleport into Skuldafn, then enter `setstageMQ303 50`.
- Near the exit to Skuldafn Temple, there is a draugr whose patrol path makes it try to walk into a wall. It will continue to do this until it dies or detects you, and will return to this position if it loses sight of you.
- If the puzzle door or rotating pillars do not work, check [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzles#Bugs "Skyrim:Puzzles") for possible fixes.
  - A workaround for the second door puzzle if the rings will not move is to use [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") to get to the wooden platform and shimmy your way past the drawbridge.
- If you enter Skuldafn at a high level, Draugr with the full [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout may knock you into areas from which you can't escape, such as rubble-blocked arches and behind walls and nooks. **?**
  - Since fast travel is impossible, the only fix is to load an earlier save.
  -  You may also use the `tcl` console command.

## Quest Stages

| The World-Eater's Eyrie (MQ303) | | |

| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |

His portal to Sovngarde is located in the ancient dragon temple of Skuldafn, high in the Jerall Mountains. The only way to reach it is to set Odahviing free so he can fly me there. *Objective 10:* Set Odahviing free |
| 40 |  | *Objective 20:* Talk to Odahviing |

His portal to Sovngarde is located in the ancient dragon temple of Skuldafn, high in the Jerall Mountains. I set Odahviing free, and he flew me to Skuldafn as agreed. Now I just have to reach the portal. |
| 180 |  | *Objective 40:* Enter Sovngarde |
| 300 | ☑ | The captured dragon Odahviing revealed that Alduin has escaped to Sovngarde, the Nord underworld, where he feeds on the souls of the dead. His portal to Sovngarde is located in the ancient dragon temple of Skuldafn, high in the Jerall Mountains. I set Odahviing free, and he flew me to Skuldafn as agreed. I fought my way to the top of Skuldafn, and entered Alduin's portal to Sovngarde. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 5, 15, 20, 30, 45, 55, 60, 120, 160, 200, 220, 240.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MQ303 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MQ303`.

| # of [Grindstones](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") | 3 |
| # of [Workbenches](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") | 1 |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

The Skyrim Thieves Guild secret entrance in Riften.

The **Thieves Guild** is the headquarters of [the Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") located with the sewers beneath [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), known as [The Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway").

The headquarters are based within [The Ragged Flagon - Cistern](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon_-_Cistern "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon - Cistern") and a bar named [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"). For full details on these places, see their individual pages.

## Residents

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| | The Ragged Flagon | | --- | | [Arnskar Ember-Master](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnskar_Ember-Master "Skyrim:Arnskar Ember-Master")[Equipment](/wiki/File:SR-icon-Equipment.png "Equipment")[†](#intnote_ExtraMerchants)  [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf")[\*](#intnote_Moves)  [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory")[Trainer (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Master)")[Sneak (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Sneak (Master)")  [Dirge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dirge "Skyrim:Dirge")  [Galathil](/wiki/Skyrim:Galathil "Skyrim:Galathil")[DG](#intnote_Dawnguard)  [Gissur](/wiki/Skyrim:Gissur "Skyrim:Gissur")[‡](#intnote_Thalmor)  [Herluin Lothaire](/wiki/Skyrim:Herluin_Lothaire "Skyrim:Herluin Lothaire")[Alchemists](/wiki/File:SR-icon-Alchemy.png "Alchemists")[†](#intnote_ExtraMerchants)  [Syndus](/wiki/Skyrim:Syndus "Skyrim:Syndus")[Equipment](/wiki/File:SR-icon-Equipment.png "Equipment")[†](#intnote_ExtraMerchants)  [Tonilia](/wiki/Skyrim:Tonilia "Skyrim:Tonilia")[Fences](/wiki/File:SR-icon-Fence.png "Fences")  [Vanryth Gatharian](/wiki/Skyrim:Vanryth_Gatharian "Skyrim:Vanryth Gatharian")[Equipment](/wiki/File:SR-icon-Equipment.png "Equipment")[†](#intnote_ExtraMerchants)  [Vekel the Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Vekel_the_Man "Skyrim:Vekel the Man")[Food and Drink](/wiki/File:SR-icon-Food.png "Food and Drink")  [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex")[Trainer (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Master)")[Lockpicking (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Lockpicking (Master)") | | | The Ragged Flagon - [‡](#note_Thalmor)Only appears during [A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat") if left alive during [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity").

[\*](#note_Moves)Relocates to the Cistern or elsewhere after related quest(s).

[DG](#note_Dawnguard)Added by the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") official plug-in. Enables you to change your character's appearance.

### The Ragged Flagon

- **[A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat")**: Locate [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern").[#](#intnote_nonTGQ)
- **[Drowned Sorrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Drowned_Sorrows "Skyrim:Drowned Sorrows")**: Find [Isabelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Isabelle_Rolaine "Skyrim:Isabelle Rolaine"), [Ranmir's](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") lost love.[#](#intnote_nonTGQ)
- **[Imitation Amnesty](/wiki/Skyrim:Imitation_Amnesty "Skyrim:Imitation Amnesty")**: Help get a convicted prisoner released from jail.
- **[Loud and Clear](/wiki/Skyrim:Loud_and_Clear "Skyrim:Loud and Clear")**: Send a message to a former [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") client.
- **[Meet the Family](/wiki/Skyrim:Meet_the_Family "Skyrim:Meet the Family")**: Speak with some of the members of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") and pick up your gear.
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[Silver Lining](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Lining "Skyrim:Silver Lining")**: Recover a stolen [silver mold](/wiki/Skyrim:Curious_Silver_Mold "Skyrim:Curious Silver Mold") for a [silversmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Endon "Skyrim:Endon").
- **[Summerset Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Summerset_Shadows "Skyrim:Summerset Shadows")**: Remove a rival guild from the picture.
- **[Surgery](/wiki/Skyrim:Surgery "Skyrim:Surgery")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Change your appearance.[#](#intnote_nonTGQ)
- **[Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business")**: Collect some debts for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").
- **[The Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:The Dainty Sload")**: Frame a [ship's](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload") captain to get revenge for a [jilted merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur").
- **[The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny")**: Find items for [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") throughout the [questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Primary_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").
- **[The Pursuit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit")**: Break into [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey")'s [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Riftweald_Manor "Skyrim:Riftweald Manor") and search for clues.
- **[The Silence Has Been Broken](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silence_Has_Been_Broken "Skyrim:The Silence Has Been Broken")**: Meet [Amaund Motierre](/wiki/Skyrim:Amaund_Motierre "Skyrim:Amaund Motierre") inside [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud") and learn who he wants assassinated.[#](#intnote_nonTGQ)
- **[Toying With The Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Toying_With_The_Dead "Skyrim:Toying With The Dead")**: Retrieve a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil "Skyrim:Arondil")'s journals for an interested buyer.
- **[Under New Management](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_New_Management "Skyrim:Under New Management")**: Become the Guild Master of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").

**Note:** All [radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") Thieves Guild quests have been omitted from the list.

[#](#note_nonTGQ)Non Thieves Guild quests.

### The Ragged Flagon - Cistern

- **[Meet the Family](/wiki/Skyrim:Meet_the_Family "Skyrim:Meet the Family")**: Speak with some of the members of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") and pick up your gear.
- **[Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business")**: Collect some debts for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").
- **[Loud and Clear](/wiki/Skyrim:Loud_and_Clear "Skyrim:Loud and Clear")**: Send a message to a former [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") client.
- **[Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly")**: Squeeze a [reluctant informer](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei") for information.
- **[The Pursuit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit")**: Break into [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey")'s [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Riftweald_Manor "Skyrim:Riftweald Manor") and search for clues.
- **[Trinity Restored](/wiki/Skyrim:Trinity_Restored "Skyrim:Trinity Restored")**: Become one of the Nightingales, [Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Nocturnal "Skyrim:Nocturnal")'s guardians.
- **[Under New Management](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_New_Management "Skyrim:Under New Management")**: Become the Guild Master of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").

[††](#note_Other_quests)Other Thieves Guild quests exist, but do not require you to enter The Ragged Flagon or Cistern.

### Thieves Guild Headquarters

There are two entrances to the headquarters: one via [the Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway") into [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"), and a second directly into [The Ragged Flagon - Cistern](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon_-_Cistern "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon - Cistern") hidden beneath a tomb that dominates the small graveyard to the east of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften")'s [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Riften) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Riften)").

You can only access the second entrance once you have joined the guild and completed [Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business"). To enter the headquarters using this entrance, press a small button in the center of the tomb; this opens a secret stone staircase. Descend it and open the sewer covering. To exit directly from the Cistern, climb the ladder in the alcove to the southwest, then pull a chain to retract the tomb.

As you progress the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") [questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), complete reputation quests for [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory"), and complete miscellaneous guild quests, the headquarters will be upgraded, and additional thieves will move in.

## Notes

-  An extra room is added to the Flagon by the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"). This room is located to the left of the door leading to [the Ratway Vaults](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway_Vaults "Skyrim:The Ratway Vaults"). It is mainly filled with beds for those who live in the Flagon.
- The special features within the Flagon only appear as the extra merchants move in after completing the required reputation quests.
- There is a "Guild" [Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") to the left of the entrance door from the Ratway Vaults.

## Bugs

-  If the Riften worldspace is loaded incorrectly, it is possible for the secret entrance's button can not be interacted.

# Skyrim:Thieves Guild Caravan Fence Quest

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Deliver [moon sugar](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Sugar "Skyrim:Moon Sugar") to [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Tonilia](/wiki/Skyrim:Tonilia "Skyrim:Tonilia") |
| Location(s): | [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"), [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), or along the road between the two cities |
| Reward: | [Leveled Gold](#Return_to_Tonilia), Access to [Atahbah](/wiki/Skyrim:Atahbah "Skyrim:Atahbah"), [Zaynabi](/wiki/Skyrim:Zaynabi "Skyrim:Zaynabi"), and [Ma'jhad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27jhad "Skyrim:Ma'jhad") as fences |
| ID: | TGFenceCaravan |

Ri'saad outside of Whiterun

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Tonilia](/wiki/Skyrim:Tonilia "Skyrim:Tonilia").
2. Deliver [moon sugar](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Sugar "Skyrim:Moon Sugar") to [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad").
3. Return to Tonilia.

### A Word with Tonilia

Once you have completed three [reputation quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Special_Job_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), speak with [Tonilia](/wiki/Skyrim:Tonilia "Skyrim:Tonilia") in the [Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"). Before you get a chance to say anything, she will ask you to do a favor for her. The Guild needs a reliable way to transport goods across Skyrim, and Tonilia believes the [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit") [caravans](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") can be an asset in this regard - if they are willing, that is. She requests that you speak to the leader of the caravans, a Khajiit peddler named [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad") about securing an alliance between the caravans and the Guild. In addition, you are to deliver a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items "Skyrim:Quest Items") of [moon sugar](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Sugar "Skyrim:Moon Sugar") to Ri'saad as a gift.

### Finding the Caravan

To find Ri'saad, use the map to fast travel close to his caravan. The caravan travels between [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), and stays outside each city for approximately two days before setting out again. Unless the caravan is camped for the night, it will move around. So, expect the target to move while you fast travel, and think about which direction it is traveling in and jump ahead.

### A "Sweet" Deal

After you have located the caravan, speak to Ri'saad, and tell him that you bring an offer from the Thieves Guild. This will cause the Khajiit to become thoughtful. To continue, hand him the moon sugar, which he will gratefully accept, saying that he looks forward to the partnership. Ri'saad will also comment that he and his fellow caravans will buy any stolen goods brought to them.

### Return to Tonilia

To finish the quest, return to Tonilia. She will thank you for your help and reward you with a leveled amount of gold, as detailed below. In addition, the Khajiit [Atahbah](/wiki/Skyrim:Atahbah "Skyrim:Atahbah"), [Ma'jhad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27jhad "Skyrim:Ma'jhad"), and [Zaynabi](/wiki/Skyrim:Zaynabi "Skyrim:Zaynabi") will now fence stolen goods for you.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 200 |
| 16-20 | 300 |
| 21-26 | 400 |
| 27-31 | 500 |
| 32-36 | 600 |
| 37-41 | 700 |
| 42+ | 800 |

## Notes

- When not on the road, the caravan can be found either across the road from [the stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables") outside Whiterun, or just east of [Salvius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvius_Farm "Skyrim:Salvius Farm") outside Markarth.
- The Khajiit do not become available as fences until after you have returned to Tonilia and finished the quest.
- Atahbah is a member of Ri'saad's caravan, as above. Ma'jhad's caravan travels between [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), and Zaynabi's caravan takes a route between [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") and [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").

## Bugs

- Ri'saad might clip through the ground while walking with the caravan, breaking the quest until he respawns. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Thieves Guild Caravan Fence Quest (TGFenceCaravan) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Deliver Moon Sugar to Ri'saad |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Return to Tonilia |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGFenceCaravan stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGFenceCaravan`.

# Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall People

## Overview

Residents are only present at this location if you complete the quest [Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk") in the Nords' favor. Before this point, they will be found at [Bujold's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Bujold's Retreat") or elsewhere as noted.

Thirsk Mead Hall under riekling control

**Thirsk Mead Hall** is a mead hall south-southwest of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") on [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim").

Thirsk Mead Hall under Nord control

[Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") and [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling") battle for control of the hall. It is initially under riekling occupation, but can be restored to Nord control if you complete the quest [Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk").

For historical information on Thirsk Mead Hall, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Thirsk "Lore:Thirsk").

## Thirsk Mead Hall Residents

Residents are only present at this location if you complete the quest [Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk") in the Nords' favor. Before this point, they will be found at [Bujold's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Bujold's Retreat") or elsewhere as noted.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| | Residents | | --- | | **[Bujold the Unworthy](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold_the_Unworthy "Skyrim:Bujold the Unworthy")** ‡ **[Elmus](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus "Skyrim:Elmus")** † **[Halbarn Iron-Fur](/wiki/Skyrim:Halbarn_Iron-Fur "Skyrim:Halbarn Iron-Fur")** [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Blacksmith")‡ **[Herkja](/wiki/Skyrim:Herkja "Skyrim:Herkja")** § **[Hilund](/wiki/Skyrim:Hilund "Skyrim:Hilund")** ‡ **[Kuvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kuvar "Skyrim:Kuvar")** [Trainer (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Master)")[Heavy Armor (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Heavy Armor (Master)")‡ **[Sirkjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Sirkjorg "Skyrim:Sirkjorg")** § | |

† Found at the [Beast Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Beast_Stone "Skyrim:Beast Stone") at night until the stone has been cleansed during the quest [Cleansing the Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones").

§ Found at the [Tree Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak") until the stone has been cleansed by completing the quest [At the Summit of Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:At_the_Summit_of_Apocrypha "Skyrim:At the Summit of Apocrypha").

#### Side Quests

- **[Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk")**: Help [Bujold the Unworthy](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold_the_Unworthy "Skyrim:Bujold the Unworthy") retake Thirsk Mead Hall. \*
- **[The Chief of Thirsk Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Chief_of_Thirsk_Hall "Skyrim:The Chief of Thirsk Hall")**: Help out a [Riekling Chief](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Chief "Skyrim:Riekling Chief") at Thirsk Mead Hall. \*

\* It is only possible to complete one of these quests, as completion of one will automatically cause the other to fail. However, you can start and complete the first two objectives in the [riekling chief](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Chief "Skyrim:Riekling Chief")'s quest, then change allegiance before agreeing to his third objective by deciding to instead support the Nords camped at Bujold's Retreat.

#### Miscellaneous Quests

| Quest Giver | Giver Location | Quest | Objective(s) | Requirement |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Elmus](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus "Skyrim:Elmus") | Thirsk Mead Hall | **[Elmus Favor Quest (berries)](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus_Favor_Quest_(berries) "Skyrim:Elmus Favor Quest (berries)")**: Retrieve some [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") for [Elmus](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus "Skyrim:Elmus"). | - Bring Elmus some Juniper Berries | [Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk") |
| [Bujold's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Bujold's Retreat") | **[Elmus Favor Quest (mead)](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus_Favor_Quest_(mead) "Skyrim:Elmus Favor Quest (mead)")**: Retrieve one bottle of [Ashfire Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfire_Mead "Skyrim:Ashfire Mead") for [Elmus](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus "Skyrim:Elmus"). | - Bring Elmus some Ashfire Mead from Thirsk Mead Hall | Thirsk not reclaimed, [Elmus](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus "Skyrim:Elmus") is alive |
| [Halbarn Iron-Fur](/wiki/Skyrim:Halbarn_Iron-Fur "Skyrim:Halbarn Iron-Fur") | Thirsk Mead Hall | **[Halbarn Favor Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Halbarn_Favor_Quest "Skyrim:Halbarn Favor Quest")**: Find some crafting materials for [Halbarn Iron-Fur](/wiki/Skyrim:Halbarn_Iron-Fur "Skyrim:Halbarn Iron-Fur"). | - Bring 10 Stalhrim Ore and 15 Ebony Ingots to Halbarn | [Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk") |
| [Hilund](/wiki/Skyrim:Hilund "Skyrim:Hilund") | Thirsk Mead Hall | **[Hilund Favor Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hilund_Favor_Quest "Skyrim:Hilund Favor Quest")**: Find fifty [Riekling spears](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Spear "Skyrim:Riekling Spear") for [Hilund](/wiki/Skyrim:Hilund "Skyrim:Hilund"). | - Bring 50 Riekling Spears to Hilund | [Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk") |

#### Rieklings in Control

Thirsk Mead Hall is initially occupied by rieklings. South of the building is an unusable [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), two empty riekling tents, a fenced pen (which will be occupied by [Bilgemuck](/wiki/Skyrim:Bilgemuck "Skyrim:Bilgemuck") after completing the first objective of the quest [The Chief of Thirsk Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Chief_of_Thirsk_Hall "Skyrim:The Chief of Thirsk Hall")), and two large stacks of crates. A total of three [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") plants are nearby, with two on either side of the entrance, and the third north of the building. Several rieklings stand outside the entrance, with another stack of crates and an unusable barrel flanking the door.

#### Nords in Control

After completing the quest [Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk"), the hall will be occupied by the Nords. All riekling structures, fencing, decorations, and crates are removed, and the forge is now available for use. After completing a [favor for Hilund](/wiki/Skyrim:Hilund_Favor_Quest "Skyrim:Hilund Favor Quest"), rows of upright riekling spears will also line the path to the entrance.

#### Rieklings in Control

Interior under riekling control

The entrance leads into a large room featuring haphazardly arranged tables, chairs, benches, and barrels, large bones and other riekling decorations, and riekling tents. The middle of the room is slightly lower than the perimeter, with steps around the room leading down to the area surrounding the central grated firepit. A second small room is beyond a doorway behind a throne opposite the entrance on the north wall.

In the first room, the entire space includes messily stacked and overturned tables, chairs, and benches, as well as scattered large bones and other riekling decorations. In addition to this furniture and debris, on the perimeter, along the west wall are two food barrels, several unusable barrels, and an empty riekling tent. Along the east wall are four food barrels, several unusable barrels, and two empty riekling tents. In the middle area, along the west side of the firepit are eight food barrels, several unusable barrels, and an empty riekling tent, with several rieklings near the tent and five bottles of [ashfire mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfire_Mead "Skyrim:Ashfire Mead") on the floor in front of the tent. Along the east side of the firepit are six food barrels, several unusable barrels, and an empty riekling tent. At the north end of the room is the riekling chief's throne, with two large brewing vats tilted at different angles on either side of the throne.

The second room contains a stack of four unusable single beds in the southeast corner, seven food barrels, several unusable barrels, an overturned table along the north wall, and two riekling tents in the southwest and northeast corners.

#### Nords in Control

Interior under Nord control

The entrance leads into a large room featuring neatly arranged tables, chairs, benches, and barrels. The middle of the room is slightly lower than the perimeter, with steps around the room leading down to the area surrounding the central grated firepit. A second small room is beyond a doorway opposite the entrance on the north wall.

In the first room, on the perimeter, along the west wall is a food barrel, two narrow tables, one of which holds two bottles of [Black-Briar Reserve](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Reserve "Skyrim:Black-Briar Reserve") and a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and four chairs and a long table holding four bottles of Black-Briar Reserve, a [venison chop](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison_Chop "Skyrim:Venison Chop"), a loaf of bread, a piece of bread, a [horse haunch](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Haunch "Skyrim:Horse Haunch"), four [rabbit haunches](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_Haunch "Skyrim:Rabbit Haunch"), and a joint of [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"). Along the east wall are two narrow tables, two food barrels, several unusable barrels, a table holding a loaf of bread, a piece of bread, a rabbit haunch, and a third food barrel, with two bottles of Black-Briar Reserve on the floor near the table, and a chair and a small round table holding another bottle of Black-Briar Reserve. In the middle area, along the west side of the firepit are two tables, each of which holds a food barrel, with a third food barrel and a bottle of Black-Briar Reserve on the floor near the tables, several unusable barrels, and a chair and a small round table holding another bottle of Black-Briar Reserve. Along the east side of the firepit are two chairs and two tables holding a bottle of Black-Briar Reserve and a food barrel, with another food barrel and two more bottles of Black-Briar Reserve on the floor near the tables, and several unusable barrels. At the south end of the firepit is a bench and a table holding a joint of venison, a [mammoth cheese bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Cheese_Bowl "Skyrim:Mammoth Cheese Bowl"), a venison chop, a loaf of bread, a piece of bread, a horse haunch, four rabbit haunches, and a bottle of Black-Briar Reserve. At the north end of the firepit is a bench and a table holding a joint of venison, a venison chop, four rabbit haunches, a bottle of Black-Briar Reserve, a loaf of bread, a piece of bread, a horse haunch, and a pot of [honey](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey "Skyrim:Honey"). Two [cooking spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") are on the west and east sides of the firepit, and two large brewing vats flank the doorway to the second room.

The second room contains five single beds, five food barrels, several unusable barrels, a chair, a table, and two small round tables, with a loaf of bread, a piece of bread, two rabbit haunches, and eleven bottles of Black-Briar Reserve scattered around the room. In total, the hall contains twenty-seven valuable bottles of Reserve, all of which can be freely taken after completing Retaking Thirsk.

## Notes

- [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Thirsk "Bloodmoon:Thirsk") also appears in *[Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon "Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon")*.
- None of the items in the building are considered owned at any time, making everything there free to take.

## Bugs

- Even after Retaking Thirsk is completed, rieklings may continue to spawn.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- Even after Retaking Thirsk is completed, Bilgemuck may remain in the previous pen area.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.
- Even after Retaking Thirsk is completed, the Nords may not move into the hall. **?**
  -  To fix this on PC, enter the console command: `set DLC2ThirskRieklingOwned to 0`.
- Even after Retaking Thirsk is completed, the chairs here may still not work.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- The torches in front of the building may not give out any light.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- Thirsk Mead Hall has a black area on the top part of the building that doesn't belong there.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Thonnir's House

## Overview

Thonnir's House

**Thonnir's House** is the residence of [Thonnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonnir "Skyrim:Thonnir") and his son [Virkmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Virkmund "Skyrim:Virkmund") in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal").

They live in this simple, one-room house at the center of Morthal.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Thonnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonnir "Skyrim:Thonnir")  [Virkmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Virkmund "Skyrim:Virkmund") |

### Exterior

The house is to the north of the [Thaumaturgist's Hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Thaumaturgist%27s_Hut "Skyrim:Thaumaturgist's Hut"). There are two [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") bushes around the building. Two flights of stairs lead up to the decking at the front, which has a wooden bench against the building and a pile of firewood beside it. To the right are a couple of small wooden boat that have been dragged out of the water and overturned for storing. At the end of the jetty that runs in front of the house a small wooden boat has been moored.

### Thonnir's House

Thonnir's home

On your left when entering is a long wooden table holding two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), with a fish barrel to the left and a basket containing two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"). To the right of this is a set of shelves holding two more leeks, four [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), several pieces of cheese on top and hidden under basket on the bottom shelf is a copy of the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Aevar Stone-Singer](/wiki/Skyrim:Aevar_Stone-Singer "Skyrim:Aevar Stone-Singer")*. Above the shelves are two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, two bunches of [elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and two bunches of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") all hanging from the ceiling. To the left of the shelves, hanging from the ceiling is a rack holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). In the southwestern corner is a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel and next to this against the west wall is a tall wardrobe and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot.

In the northwestern corner is a round wooden table holding two bottles of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"). Coming out from the north wall is an owned double bed, where Thonnir sleeps. There is a large fireplace opposite the door in the middle of the north wall. On the mantlepiece there is a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") and in front of the hearth a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand. To the right of the fireplace, hidden behind a basket is a unique item identified as [Michaela's Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Michaela%27s_Flagon "Skyrim:Michaela's Flagon").

In the northeastern corner, against the east wall is a single owned bed where Virkmund sleeps. Next to the bed is a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") and a pair of [drums](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") are at the foot of the bed. In the southeastern corner is a square wooden table and two chairs holding a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and three bottles of Nord mead.
