# Skyrim:Throat of the World

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Landmark.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Landmark.png) | Landmark: Throat of the World ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Throat+of+the+World)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Throat_of_the_World "Lore:Throat of the World")) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Important Treasure | |
| [Notched Pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Notched_Pickaxe "Skyrim:Notched Pickaxe") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| ThroatOfTheWorld01 | |
| Region | |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | |
| Location | |
| Southeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ore "Skyrim:Ebony Ore") | 2 |
| # of [Malachite](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite_Ore "Skyrim:Malachite Ore") | 2 |

The Throat of the World, with High Hrothgar top-left

The **Throat of the World** is the highest mountain in Tamriel, located southeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). It is a major landmark and home to the reclusive [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards"), who are masters of [The Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Voice "Skyrim:The Voice").

The famous Seven Thousand Steps lead up the mountain to [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar"), where the Greybeards live their lives in absolute seclusion. As part of the [Main Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Main_Quest "Skyrim:Main Quest"), you journey to High Hrothgar to learn how to use [Dragon Shouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). Later, you're required to continue up the mountain to the summit, home to [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)"), the leader of the Greybeards.

For historical information about the mountain, see [the lore article](/wiki/Lore:Throat_of_the_World "Lore:Throat of the World").

## Related Quests

- **[The Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World")**: Receive a lesson from [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").
- **[Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge")**: Recover an [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll") to learn an [Ancient Secret](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend").
- **[Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane")**: Exploit the Time-Wound to learn [Dragonrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend") and defeat [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") at the Throat of the World.
- **[Dragonslayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonslayer "Skyrim:Dragonslayer")**: Put an end to the [World-Eater](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin").
- **[Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial")**: Acquire the materials necessary to repair the [White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)").
- **[Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(quest) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (quest)")**: Deal with a [potential threat](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").

## Notes

- Despite supposedly being the tallest mountain in all of Tamriel, the summit of Throat of the World is actually only 766.5 meters above sea level in the game, according to the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit").
- Although the path up is said to be 7,000 steps long, there are only 732 visible. The Creation Kit indicates that there are 1,828 step objects, though many of these are adjacent to each other so can only be counted as one step.
- It is possible to reach the Throat of the World before the quest [The Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World") by scaling up the side of the mountain adjacent to [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar") (or, though more difficult, from the lower sections of the path to High Hrothgar) using a zig-zag technique. Using a horse will make it easier to scale steeper slopes. If you ascend this way before the quest The Throat of the World is active, Paarthurnax will not be there (as he is quest dependent) though the ore veins and the Notched Pickaxe will still be.
- The quest [Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial") will not begin (you will not get the courier's letter) until you have access to this location.
- At the very peak of the mountain, above the ledge where the Throat of the World is located, are two [malachite](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite "Skyrim:Malachite") and two [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") ore veins [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&x=54971&y=-52544&zoom=16&legacy=true). The unique [Notched Pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Notched_Pickaxe "Skyrim:Notched Pickaxe"), an enchanted pickaxe, can be found nearby [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Notched+Pickaxe&zoom=17&legacy=true).
-  In the [Nintendo Switch version](/wiki/Skyrim:Switch "Skyrim:Switch"), a Zelda-themed chest can be found here containing a [Champion's Tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion%27s_Tunic "Skyrim:Champion's Tunic"), a [Hylian Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hylian_Shield "Skyrim:Hylian Shield"), and the [Master Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Sword "Skyrim:Master Sword").
- It is not possible to pass through the freezing winds that block the way up without using the Clear Skies Shout; even with maxed [Magic Resistance](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Resistance "Skyrim:Magic Resistance") and/or Frost Resistance, attempting to pass through will leave you heavily staggered.
- Along the way up to the top of the mountain (where the ore veins are), there are pockets of heavy mist that cause your character to yell in pain when passing through them. If you open the Active Effects menu just as passing through one, you will see: "Oppressive Fog" with the effect description of "The fog slows your progress and dulls your senses" with an active effect time of 4 seconds. Despite the description, it doesn't appear to do anything otherwise. The Clear Skies Shout will dispel the mists for a time.

# Skyrim:Through a Glass, Darkly

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), checked by [Riliane](/wiki/User:Riliane "User:Riliane") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Confront the darkness within yourself to obtain a [powerful weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowrend_(item) "Skyrim:Shadowrend (item)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Automatically added when trying to take [Shadowrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowrend_(item) "Skyrim:Shadowrend (item)") |
| Location(s): | Geyser northeast of [the Atronach Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Atronach_Stone "Skyrim:The Atronach Stone") |
| Reward: | [Shadowrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowrend_(item) "Skyrim:Shadowrend (item)") |
| ID: | BGSSSE018\_ShadowrendQuest |
| Added by: | [Shadowrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowrend "Skyrim:Shadowrend") |

A strange anomaly has appeared in Eastmarch

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to the specified geyser pool in [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch").
2. Attempt to take [Shadowrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowrend_(item) "Skyrim:Shadowrend (item)") and defeat your summoned [Shadow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadow "Skyrim:Shadow").
3. Take either the greatsword or the battleaxe version of Shadowrend.

### Inner Darkness

The Shadow

Once you've installed the [Shadowrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowrend "Skyrim:Shadowrend") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"), you will receive this quest. The journal entry will inform you that an inner voice is drawing you to a geyser pool in [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") in order to confront the darkness within yourself. The geyser can be found near the [Atronach Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Atronach_Stone "Skyrim:The Atronach Stone"), to the northeast of it. Stand with the Atronach Stone at your back and walk toward a trio of pine trees in the water. Continue past the leftmost tree. The pool contains skeletal remains which have stained the water black, and will only begin to froth when you approach.

Above this anomaly, a weapon will appear. It is [Shadowrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowrend_(item) "Skyrim:Shadowrend (item)"), a shadow weapon from the ruins of [Milchar](/wiki/Lore:Milchar "Lore:Milchar") in the [Shivering Isles](/wiki/Lore:Shivering_Isles "Lore:Shivering Isles"). Shadowrend is both a [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword") and a [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), and it will proceed to cycle between each version, with the weapon warping in and out of existence until you attempt to take it. Touching the weapon will summon a [Shadow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadow "Skyrim:Shadow") enemy named "[player]'s Shadow". It is a shadowy clone of you, meaning it will wear your equipment and know all of your [spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells "Skyrim:Spells"), powers, and [shouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Shouts "Skyrim:Shouts").

Defeat the Shadow and claim Shadowrend from its remains to complete the quest. Whichever version of the weapon you didn't select will reappear above the pool, where it will hang in the air indefinitely. You can return to the pool any time in order to switch between the two versions of Shadowrend. You must have it in your inventory for the swap to function, otherwise it will say, "You lack the required item." Each version is a powerful Daedric weapon in its own right, with a 15% [weakness to magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Weakness_to_Magic "Skyrim:Weakness to Magic") enchantment.

## Notes

- Shadowrend originally [appeared](/wiki/Shivering:Shadowrend "Shivering:Shadowrend") in the *[Shivering Isles](/wiki/Shivering:Shivering_Isles "Shivering:Shivering Isles")* expansion for *[Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion")*.
- [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online") also features an unrelated [clannfear](/wiki/Online:Shadowrend "Online:Shadowrend") and [item set](/wiki/Online:Shadowrend_(set) "Online:Shadowrend (set)").
- The [Shadow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadow "Skyrim:Shadow") seems to be a valid target for the [Ebony Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Blade "Skyrim:Ebony Blade").
- The Shadow may choose to instead attack nearby [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit").
- The name of this quest is a Biblical phrase from 1 Corinthians 13:12 (KJV).
  - It also appears quite similar to the name of another quest in *Oblivion*, [Through A Nightmare, Darkly](/wiki/Oblivion:Through_A_Nightmare,_Darkly "Oblivion:Through A Nightmare, Darkly").

## Quest Stages

| Through a Glass, Darkly (BGSSSE018\_ShadowrendQuest) | | |

| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 5 |  | An inner voice is telling me I must confront a darkness within myself. I am drawn toward a geyser pool in Eastmarch. Perhaps answers lie there. *Objective :* Go to Eastmarch Geysers |
| 10 |  | The weapon I attempted to take has pulled something from within me - a dark shadow of myself. I must defeat this doppelganger. *Objective :* Defeat your Shadow |
| 15 |  | I have defeated my shadow and feel at peace. I should retrieve the weapon from its remains. *Objective :* Retrieve Shadowrend |
| 20 | ☑ | I have discovered and defeated my shadow doppelganger, and have obtained the weapon Shadowrend. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage BGSSSE018_ShadowrendQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest BGSSSE018_ShadowrendQuest`.

# Skyrim:Tilted Scales

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Retrieve a set of ancient armor from an old warrior.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Reading *[The Crimson Dirks, v4](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Crimson_Dirks,_v4 "Skyrim:The Crimson Dirks, v4")* |
| Location(s): | [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall"), [Yorgrim Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Yorgrim_Overlook "Skyrim:Yorgrim Overlook") |
| Reward: | Set of [studded Dragonscale armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Dragonscale_Armor "Skyrim:Studded Dragonscale Armor") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE060\_MiscQuest, ccBGSSSE060\_Quest |
| Added by: | [Alternative Armors - Dragonscale](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragonscale "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragonscale") |

Claim the armor of Ulfnir Bone-Skin

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read *[The Crimson Dirks, v4](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Crimson_Dirks,_v4 "Skyrim:The Crimson Dirks, v4")* at the bottom floor of [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall").
2. Defeat [Ulfnir Bone-Skin](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfnir_Bone-Skin "Skyrim:Ulfnir Bone-Skin") at [Yorgrim Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Yorgrim_Overlook "Skyrim:Yorgrim Overlook") and take his [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Overlook_Key "Skyrim:Overlook Key").
3. Claim the set of [studded Dragonscale armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Dragonscale_Armor "Skyrim:Studded Dragonscale Armor").

## Detailed Walkthrough

In order to start the quest, you need to read *[The Crimson Dirks, v4](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Crimson_Dirks,_v4 "Skyrim:The Crimson Dirks, v4")* in [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall"). It recalls a tale where a young Bosmer named [Fathrys](/wiki/Skyrim:Fathrys "Skyrim:Fathrys") had hoped to wed Zaharia. She dismissively rejected him by saying that she would only accept him if he were to give her a dragon scale. Hearing this, the drunken bandit mage Antonius regaled an old Nord legend where the warrior [Ulfnir Bone-Skin](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfnir_Bone-Skin "Skyrim:Ulfnir Bone-Skin") slew the dragon Vithrelnaak, fashioning armor from his scales and ultimately burying it with him. Antonius claims that Ulfnir's corpse protects this armor through death in the barrow near [Yorgrim Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Yorgrim_Overlook "Skyrim:Yorgrim Overlook").

With this, the quest directs you to Yorgrim Overlook to investigate. When you reach the overlook, you will find the lifeless skeleton of Fathrys holding his *[Poem for Zaharia](/wiki/Skyrim:Poem_for_Zaharia "Skyrim:Poem for Zaharia")*. You will be attacked by two generic skeletons and the skeleton of Ulfnir Bone-Skin himself. Defeat them and loot the [Overlook Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Overlook_Key "Skyrim:Overlook Key"). With it, you can unlock the gate.

Claim the [Studded Dragonscale Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Dragonscale_Armor "Skyrim:Studded Dragonscale Armor"), [Studded Dragonscale Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Dragonscale_Boots "Skyrim:Studded Dragonscale Boots"), [Studded Dragonscale Gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Dragonscale_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Studded Dragonscale Gauntlets"), and [Studded Dragonscale Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Dragonscale_Helmet "Skyrim:Studded Dragonscale Helmet") from the chest. With this quest completed and the [Dragon Armor perk](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing#Skill_Perks "Skyrim:Smithing"), you will be able to craft more Studded Dragonscale items.

## Notes

- If Yorgrim Overlook is visited before you have read the book, the two skeletons will still attack you, but neither Fathrys' nor Ulfnir's skeletons will be there. Defeating the two skeletons will clear the location. The gate can still be unlocked and the chest looted, but there will be no Dragonscale armor. If the quest is attempted after doing this, Fathrys and Ulfnir will appear as normal and the armor will be added to the chest.
  - By clearing Yorgrim Overlook and unlocking the gate before reading *The Crimson Dirks, v4*, you will be able to easily retrieve the armor and complete the quest without defeating Ulfnir.
- Regular Dragonscale armor starts appearing in leveled lists at level 46, but this creation's quest can be completed by characters of any level for its armor set.
- Yorgrim Overlook is also the ruin just across and upslope from the small Dark Seducer camp that's just off the road and one of the first locations in the Saints and Seducers Quest line.

I should head to the barrow and see what I can uncover. *Objective :* Investigate Yorgrim's Overlook |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE060_MiscQuest, ccBGSSSE060_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE060_MiscQuest, ccBGSSSE060_Quest`.

# Skyrim:To Kill an Empire

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Attempt to assassinate the [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") while disguised as the [Gourmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourmet "Skyrim:Gourmet").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") |
| Location(s): | [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary"), [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | DB09 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Recipe for Disaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster") | **Next →** [Death Incarnate](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Incarnate "Skyrim:Death Incarnate") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Recipe for Disaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster") | | → Next | [Death Incarnate](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Incarnate "Skyrim:Death Incarnate") | | |

[Gianna](/wiki/Skyrim:Gianna "Skyrim:Gianna"), ready to cook a meal for the Emperor

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").
2. Enter the castle using the [Gourmet's letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourmet%27s_Writ_of_Passage "Skyrim:Gourmet's Writ of Passage").
3. Cook the [Gourmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourmet "Skyrim:Gourmet")'s famous stew and poison it at the end.
4. Escape when the [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(decoy) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (decoy)") dies.
5. Return to the [Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary").

### This Soup Is To Die For

The Emperor's decoy tasting his last meal

After [securing the writ of passage into the Emperor's service](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster"), the rest of the plan is ready to fall into place. Following [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid")'s instructions, travel to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") with the [poisonous herb](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarrin_Root "Skyrim:Jarrin Root") she gave you and report to head of security, [Commander Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro"). Show him the [writ](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourmet%27s_Writ_of_Passage "Skyrim:Gourmet's Writ of Passage") you stole from [the Gourmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Balagog_gro-Nolob "Skyrim:Balagog gro-Nolob") to gain entrance to the [castle](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour,_Emperor%27s_Tower "Skyrim:Castle Dour, Emperor's Tower"). Maro will allow you to pass with no trouble (commenting on your clothing depending on whether or not you are wearing the chef's hat or clothes), telling you to report to the castle's chef, [Gianna](/wiki/Skyrim:Gianna "Skyrim:Gianna"). When Gianna greets you, she is both nervous and excited at the prospect of working with the great Gourmet. If you have yet to don your chef's hat, she will direct you to one on the shelf; you cannot begin "cooking" until you are appropriately attired. Once you are ready, say, **Enough! The Gourmet is here to cook, not talk! Let us begin.**

Gianna flusters, *"Oh! Yes, but of course. Ahem. The Emperor has requested your signature dish - the Potage le Magnifique. I've taken the liberty of getting it started. But the cookbook only says so much, and everyone makes the Potage differently. I would be honored if we could make it... the Gourmet's special way. The base broth is already boiled. We can get started right now. So... which ingredient should I add next?"*

The Potage le Magnifique, as described in *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste"),* consists of a basic recipe and more ingredients added based on the chef's inspiration. Thus, you now have four ingredients to select, at each stage there are three options: the normal, the strange, and her choice.

| Option | Dialogue option | Responses |
| --- | --- | --- |
| First ingredient | | |
| Normal | [Carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"). | "Carrots? Really? Okay... What next?" |
| Strange | A [sweetroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"). | "Ooohh.... how decadent. I never would have guessed it. What next?" |
| Her choice | Remain silent. | "Oh, I get it. This is a test, right? You want to see how well I know the Potage le Magnifique. Well then, I think a pinch of frost salts should do the trick, right? Now what?" |
| Second ingredient | | |
| Normal | You must now add a splash of [mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). | "Ah, of course. I suspected as much." |
| Strange | The next ingredient is... [vampire dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust"). | "Vampire dust? Seriously? Hmm... yes. I guess I can see how that would add a more... earthy texture. And, oddly enough, we do have some on hand... All right. What next, then?" |
| Her choice | Remain silent. | "My choice, then? Very well. I think we should add some Chaurus eggs. For additional flavor." |
| Third ingredient | | |
| Normal | One [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"). | "Really? Oh, I use Nirnroot as a special seasoning all the time as well. What a wonderful idea. Okay. Now what?" |
| Strange | We shall now add... a [giant's toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe")! | "A... giant's toe? You're... sure about that?", **I said a giant's toe! Do not question the Gourmet!**, "Of course! I.... I'm sorry. One giant's toe. There. What, um... What next?" |
| Her choice | Remain silent. | "Ooookay.... Um.... Let me see. Thistle? Yes, let's try that. Just a sprig or two..." |
| Fourth ingredient | | |
| Normal | Diced [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat"). | "Hmmm... horker. So delicious. I swear, is there a soul alive who doesn't enjoy the taste of... Sorry, I didn't mean to get carried away. There we go, one cup of diced horker meat. I have to say, the stew seems done. Add anything else, and we may dilute the distinct flavors. So... is that it?" |
| Strange | You must add... a [septim](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold#Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). | "A Septim? As in... a gold coin? Really? Ah, I see now. That would give the Potage le Magnifique a slightly metallic - but delicious - aftertaste. Simply brilliant. I have to say, the stew seems done. Add anything else, and we may dilute the distinct flavors. So... is that it?" |
| Her choice | Remain silent. | "My choice, hmm? All right, then - tomatoes. Simple, yet infinitely flavorful. Don't you agree? Well, I have to say, the stew seems done. Add anything else, and we may dilute the distinct flavors. So... is that it?" |

When you are finished don't forget to add your "special" [final ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarrin_Root "Skyrim:Jarrin Root"):
*"Oh? What is this, some kind of herb? Are you sure? The Potage tastes perfect as it is. Any other ingredient might..."*

**Now, now, Gianna. Who's the Gourmet here?**

*"Heh, I'm sorry. Of course. It's your most famous recipe, after all. All right then, your secret ingredient's been added. And if I may say so... it has been an honor, getting a chance to prepare a meal with, well... the best chef in the entire Empire. I'll carry the stew pot, and lead the way up to the dining room. I'm sure the Emperor and his guests are dying to meet you."*

It is not necessary to poison the Emperor with the Jarrin Root, however, in order to successfully complete the quest—you may kill him any way you want.

### The Last Supper

When the Potage is complete, follow Gianna into the dining room as she serves the food to the Emperor. Right before you go in, there is a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Weapon_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments")* on the table to your left. The Emperor will be speaking to the [diners](/wiki/Skyrim:Nobleman "Skyrim:Nobleman") and [a noblewoman](/wiki/Skyrim:Noblewoman "Skyrim:Noblewoman") about his [cousin's](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") murder when you enter, while two [Penitus Oculatus](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus") agents stand guard behind him. Gianna will serve the Emperor the meal you cooked and, regardless of the ingredients, he will compliment its amazing taste.

If you added the Jarrin Root, the Emperor will soon die a rather unspectacular death. If you didn't add the poison, the Emperor and his guests will continue to slurp their soup until you assassinate him, which is easy enough since he has only 1 health point. The guards will attack you upon the Emperor's death, and Gianna will attempt to defend you before fleeing, although this may be avoided by successfully sneaking as he dies.

Once the Emperor is dead, exit through the door opposite where you entered upstairs.

### Betrayal

Once out the door it looks like you are home free. However, as you cross the bridge, you will be ambushed by Commander Maro and several of his agents. He reveals that the man you killed was a decoy. Maro explains that someone from the Dark Brotherhood betrayed you and revealed to Maro your plans to assassinate the Emperor. Maro agreed to allow the Brotherhood to continue its business in exchange for you. He then tells you that because the Dark Brotherhood killed his son he intends to go back on his word and wipe them out. He has sent his agents to attack the sanctuary already. As soon as the conversation with Maro begins, your bounty in [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") will be set to 1500, so the city guards will be on the lookout for you. Escape the city by following the tower's stairs to the very bottom and head to the Brotherhood Sanctuary. You cannot fast travel directly to the sanctuary, so the quickest option is to fast travel to [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") and head west. The quest ends when you reach the [Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary").

## Notes

- You will be blamed for the emperor's death even if you kill him in a stealthy way that would normally avoid incurring a bounty.
- Two Penitus Oculatus Agents outside Castle Dour are never disabled after you finish the quest.
- In [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition") or [Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition") with [The Gray Cowl Returns!](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed. It is possible to use the [Gray Cowl of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:Gray Cowl of Nocturnal") to avoid the bounty from the Solitude Guards. Wearing the cowl during the bridge encounter allows you to kill members of the Penitus Oculatus with no bounty. Guards are not hostile when you remove the cowl afterwards but members of the Penitus Oculatus might still remain hostile. Scripted bounty for murder goes to the Gray Cowl. When the headpiece is taken off, guards will have no suspicion on the Dragonborn.
- Without Creation Club content, it's still possible to finish the quest without ever incurring any bounty (or other negative side effects), by utilizing [glitches](/wiki/Skyrim:Glitches "Skyrim:Glitches").
  - After exiting the dining room, glitch [through](/wiki/Skyrim:Glitches#Clipping "Skyrim:Glitches") or [over](/wiki/Skyrim:Glitches#Object_Flying "Skyrim:Glitches") the wall of the bridge, to avoid triggering the encounter with Maro. After finishing the quest, plan a [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") and re-visit the bridge. Your character will get stuck around the spot where the Maro encounter would have triggered. By in-game waiting until you miss your wedding ceremony, you'll re-gain control over your character.
  - This alternate method may also work [*verification needed — Doesn't seem to work anymore, see [talk page](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:To_Kill_an_Empire#No_Bounty "Skyrim talk:To Kill an Empire")*]: After exiting the dining room, cast a Destruction spell with a large area of effect (e.g. [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball")) a couple of times in both the upper and lower doors across the bridge, and slowly walk across. You'll be stopped as if Maro was talking, but you'll quickly exit back out, not getting attacked by the Penitus Oculatus or getting the bounty. You can then easily leave. As long as you don't kill the men you won't get a bounty. You will need to leave the city by foot as the guards are scripted to be hostile, which prevents fast-travel. Killing any single Solitude guard undetected may remove the bounty.

- If you do get a bounty, then, as long as the three Penitus Oculatus men are dead, you can remove the bounty using your Thane status or Thieves Guild association (provided you have them available). However, even if you are a Thane of Haafingar, you will not be able to remove your bounty using your Thane status if Solitude is still under Imperial rule (fixed in Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.0).
- You should remove all items you own or want from the sanctuary before completing this quest, or they may be lost. However, the [Unusual Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") located in Astrid's room will still be available.
- Maro will have different dialogue based on your equipment when you arrive. If you are wearing a Chef's Hat or Chef's Tunic, he will say *"Your clothes... of course... I should have realized..."* Otherwise, he tells you *"You are not dressed as I had expected."* Regardless, he allows you to pass.
- If you are in the form of a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf") or [vampire lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord") while crossing the bridge, you'll automatically change back when Maro appears.
- After the quest, the Emperor's Tower will still be freely accessible, both from the walkway escape exit and from the front door inside the castle courtyard. However, the door to the dining hall will be permanently locked from both sides. The tower is completely abandoned after this point, so you can take what you want without consequence. Be aware that the whole place respawns, however, so it cannot be safely used as a house.
- After you tell Gianna to add the jarrin root to the recipe, if you quickly enter your menu you can drop it from your inventory; this allows you to retrieve it later. The quest will continue and the Emperor will still die of poisoning.
- According to the recipe that [exists](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste") in the game, carrots are a part of the "basic broth" that Gianna has already prepared. Yet, she will not object or even mention it if you suggest to add carrots.

## Bugs

- Gianna may not talk to you if you are inflicted with certain diseases.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- This quest may not start on completion of [Recipe for Disaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster").
  -  Setting the stage through console does not work, as the stage always remains 0. The cause of the bug is currently unknown, and the easiest way to overcome it is to skip the quest entirely. To do this, move to a location away from the Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary, and use the console commands `completequest db09` followed by `setstage db10 10`. This immediately starts you on the following quest.
- The guards who arrive with [Commander Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro") may either remain there if you snuck past without killing them, or respawn if you did kill them. They stand still and scowl at you, and will never attack, though they do appear as red dots on the compass if you come near the sky bridge and prevent fast travel like any other enemy. You can kill them without incurring any additional bounties, and they will not fight back. If you have an aggressive follower with you, your follower may attack them; they still will not fight back.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.
  -  Their reference numbers are `643D4`, `643D5` and `643D6`. The problem can be fixed on the PC by entering the console (press "~") and typing `prid 643D4` followed by `disable`, and then repeating for the other two numbers.
- Looting the Emperor's dead body seems to cause a glitch where the world incorrectly loads and you travel on the land under the buildings' foundations, causing the quest to become stuck on "Escape from the tower".
  - To fix this, load from the previous autosave before cooking the Emperor's last meal, and do not loot the Emperor's dead body.
  - You can get around this on Special Edition if you pickpocket his robes off while he's still alive (requires associated pickpocket perks).
- If you have a follower, you can ask them to stand in the way of the conversation between you and the cook; they may interrupt your conversation. This also happens if guards are chasing you after you clear Commander Maro but before you enter the Castle Dour. **?**
  - To fix this, simply reload the last save.
- After you finish the quest, the items stored in the containers in the sanctuary may disappear. **?**

## Quest Stages

| To Kill an Empire (DB09) | | |

| 10 |  | Using the Writ of Passage issued to the chef known as "The Gourmet," I must enter Castle Dour and play the part of the culinary master, who is scheduled to prepare a feast. This will be my opportunity to assassinate the Emperor, using any tools at my disposal. *Objective 10:* Report to Commander Maro |

Despite his deal, Maro has sent troops to destroy the Sanctuary. I must return there and help my Family! *Objective 70:* Return to the Sanctuary |
| 200 | ☑ | After learning the Emperor was actually Titus Mede II's double, and being confronted by Commander Maro, I learned Maro had betrayed the betrayer, and sent troops to destroy the Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary. I returned there, to lend aid to my fellow Family members. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 75, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DB09 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DB09`.

# Skyrim:Tolfdir the Absent-Minded

## Overview

Tolfdir's Alembic

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note:** This quest does not appear in your journal.

1. Speak to [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir").
2. Hunt down his missing [alembic](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir%27s_Alembic "Skyrim:Tolfdir's Alembic") in the [College](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").
3. Return to Tolfdir.

### Good Old Tolfdir

Tolfdir is an elderly mage and professor at the College of Winterhold and one of the first people encountered at the college. When you have completed [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal") and have begun [Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books") Tolfdir will be residing at the college. If you run across him looking confused, ask him if he needs help.

### Tolfdir's Alembic

Embarrassed, Tolfdir will admit to misplacing his [alembic](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir%27s_Alembic "Skyrim:Tolfdir's Alembic"). And, while he could indeed use a different one, he has a strange sentimental attachment to this particular piece of equipment. Help the professor out by finding this lost item.
The alembic will appear in one of three randomly-selected locations in the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance"):

- On the top floor: in the northern room, on top of a barrel to the right of the central dining bench.
- On the top floor: underneath the left display case in the enchanting room.
- On the bottom floor: on a crate in the eastern room, with the big barrel in it.

However, even without the quest being activated, you will run across the alembic numerous times in your wanderings about the college. Simply return the alembic to Tolfdir when you speak to him, and earn the reward each time. Tolfdir will give you thirty gold and an empty petty, lesser or common soul gem for returning his misplaced property.

## Notes

- Finding Tolfdir's Alembic before triggering the quest will not change the quest dialogue or outcome; you can simply start the quest and give the alembic to Tolfdir to receive your reward.
- Unlike previous titles where alembics were a major part of [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy"), this is the only individual alembic that can be found in the base [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") game. The [Farming](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming "Skyrim:Farming") creation adds a second one in the basement of [Goldenhills Plantation](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenhills_Plantation "Skyrim:Goldenhills Plantation"). All other alembics in the game are permanently attached to alchemy stations.
- Sometimes, the alembic will get dislodged from its normal location, possibly falling behind other objects or onto the ground nearby.
- Version 1.0 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") adds journal objectives to this quest.

## Bugs

- Tolfdir may offer the dialogue option that initiates the quest after it has already been completed. Selecting this option will re-add the quest to your journal, but the Alembic will not respawn, leaving the objective permanently stuck in your journal.
  -  Entering the console command `player.additem "00026c31" 1` to give yourself a second alembic will allow you to complete the quest by speaking to Tolfdir as normal.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MGR01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MGR01`.

# Skyrim:Tolvald's Cave

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Tolvald's Cave ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Tolvald%27s+Cave)) | | |

Tolvald's Cave

**Tolvald's Cave** is a large [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northeast of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). It contains three zones: *[Tolvald's Cave](#Tolvald.27s_Cave)*, *[Tolvald's Gap](#Tolvald.27s_Gap)*, and *[Tolvald's Crossing](#Tolvald.27s_Crossing)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The cave is in the [Velothi Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Velothi_Mountains "Skyrim:Velothi Mountains") north of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). A leveled creature guards the entrance.

### Tolvald's Cave

Many of the Falmer inhabiting the cave will hop out of [chitinous holes](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Pod "Skyrim:Falmer Pod") in the wall to ambush you, so be on your guard. Using the spell [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") will help you turn the tables.

In the first room, there is an abandoned camp with three bedrolls, an overturned [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), a locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") by the pillar to the left, and on the standing stool, a *[Hunter's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter%27s_Journal_(Tolvald%27s_Cave) "Skyrim:Hunter's Journal (Tolvald's Cave)")*, which reveals that a few [hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") tracked some animals to the cave and decided to investigate the ruins within. To the right of the chest is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"), and atop the ledge are a few sacks and spilled [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). To the right of the bedroll farthest from the entrance is a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein"), and starting down the path to the northwest is a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") beside a second iron ore vein. The first leveled creature is standing over a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit")'s body between another three bear traps. To the right is a [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") fungus, and to either side is a bunch of [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") mushrooms.

Just before the lantern in the tunnel is a [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") cluster, with a [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") just after the lantern. The next section contains a leveled creature standing over some bloody bones. Spread around the area are various fungi, including a [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), a bleeding crown, and a white cap. In the small room to the right is a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"). To the west is a small room with two [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry"), and to the right are two blisterworts. The path continues past the blisterworts into a room guarded by another leveled creature standing over some more remains. Around this room are numerous types of fungi, including a Namira's rot, an [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), two clusters of white caps, and three bunches of [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") on the walls. The tunnel out contains five bunches of glowing mushrooms, an imp stool, a fly amanita, a bleeding crown, a Namira's rot, a [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), a small coin purse, and three loose coins.

The room behind the door contains a leveled [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), a piece of [gold ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore "Skyrim:Gold Ore"), a large coin purse, and a Dwemer chest. On both sides of the room there are hidden doors, with a pull chain by the western door that activates both doors. The chest is [rigged](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") such that, when opened, a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") will shoot from the walls and Falmer will come through the hidden doors. The darts cannot be circumvented, but opening the doors before the chest will prevent the Falmer from coming down the tunnels. Both tunnels contain bunches of glowing mushrooms. There are two Falmer patrolling the room at the end of the tunnels, and the Falmer scheduled to come through the doors, one of which carries the [shaman's key](/wiki/Skyrim:Keys#Shaman.27s_Key "Skyrim:Keys"), are waiting in the next passage. In the room at the end of the tunnels is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"), beside which is a random [ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), three random [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), and some [Falmer equipment](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Falmer_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear") (a war axe, a bow, and arrows). To the left of the lab is a gruesome corner with a random assortment of potions, weapons, and armor. The nearby cage contains a dead hunter, and throughout the room are four bunches of glowing mushrooms and eleven [chaurus egg sacs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"). The next passage contains one glowing mushroom and eighteen chaurus egg sacs before opening up into a Falmer camp.

In the center of the camp is a sacrificial table with a dead hunter watched by a single Falmer. The tent to the northwest contains a few random ingredients, while the tent to the southeast contains a [spider egg sac](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg"). There is a Falmer chest in the northwest flanked by two [tanning racks](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"). The next large section contains three tents, two spider's egg sacs, an assortment of fungi consisting of two bleeding crowns, two fly amanitas, two imp stools, two white caps, four Namira's rot, and a blisterwort. Two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), a [pine thrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") nest, and a set of [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales") are in the first tent, three random ingredients are by the fire, and a few loose chaurus eggs are scattered about. The area is guarded by a Falmer and two frostbite spiders. Two Falmer will appear behind you when you approach the fire. There is a locked chest to the right of the first tent, and a chest in the tent with the gate. The passage to *Tolvald's Gap* is nearby to the south.

### Tolvald's Gap

The path leading down is patrolled by a Falmer, with a random creature at the bottom. There are five more Falmer patrolling the area (one of which carries another shaman's key), another Falmer on the ledge above, and two frostbite spiders in the next room. The room to the west contains seven bleeding crowns, four white caps, three fly amanitas, two blisterworts, three Namira's rot, six imp stools, fourteen glowing mushrooms, two baskets with a mix of the various ingredients, and a Falmer chest and three chaurus egg sacs in the tent. Exiting the room, there is a chest on a small ledge to the left. Under the glowing mushrooms, following the path, are three blisterwort fungi and a leveled potion. To the right, under the previous side path, is a locked chest.

The second room contains a Falmer to the right of the tent near a spider egg sac, a dead chaurus, and some Falmer swords and loose arrows, and to the left, two frostbite spiders. In the spider webs to the east are two dead skeevers. The next tunnel contains a skeever, more mushrooms and chaurus egg sacs to harvest, and three random poisons and a Falmer bow in one corner of the passage. The next room is a chaurus nest, with two chaurus and a chaurus reaper guarded by a single Falmer. There are approximately seventy chaurus egg sacs and a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") in this room. To the left of the next tunnel is a locked Falmer chest, with a few more loose chaurus eggs on the ground, as well as two [charred skeever hides](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") and a Falmer sword lying on a rock nearby. The tent to the right along the next passage contains a skeever, and an alcove to the right farther along contains a random potion and a random poison. The path takes you back to the ledge near the beginning of the zone with a single Falmer, two tents (one of which contains a Falmer chest), and several loose glowing mushrooms on the ground. The path proceeds south, offering more glowing mushrooms, a Falmer war axe next to a campfire, and more chaurus egg sacs before continuing on to *Tolvald's Crossing*.

### Tolvald's Crossing

Crown of Barenziah

There is a Falmer patrolling below the waterfall, and human bones to the left in the following tunnel. Beside the remains is a *[Faded Diary](/wiki/Skyrim:Faded_Diary "Skyrim:Faded Diary")* and a leveled potion. The diary reveals the torment suffered by the writer seeing the death of a brother during the eruption of [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain") in [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"), and plans to move to [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") due to the resulting poverty. To the left farther along the tunnel is a second quicksilver ore vein. Straight ahead on the right is a crushed cart with a locked chest, and to the left of the cart is a skeleton with a *[Tattered Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Tattered_Journal_(Tolvald%27s_Cave) "Skyrim:Tattered Journal (Tolvald's Cave)")*, which details a fight with "white elves". There is another crushed skeleton in the nearby rubble next to a leveled [staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Staves "Skyrim:Staves"). This skeleton is cradling a large rock, and is wearing a silver amethyst ring on its right hand. The large room beyond this area contains the remains of a caravan, with multiple skeletons, leveled swords and arrows, two dead chaurus, and a randomly enchanted sword near the skeleton in the middle. The last skeleton's hand is outstretched toward the middle of the rubble, where the [Crown of Barenziah](/wiki/Skyrim:Crown_of_Barenziah "Skyrim:Crown of Barenziah") appears (after finding all 24 Stones of Barenziah) when the quest [No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned") has advanced far enough. Two to three [Dunmer ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_Ghost "Skyrim:Dunmer Ghost") appear beside the crown after you take it, and will attack you. They are wearing [Elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") armor. Note: the large room containing the crown will be blocked off and invisible on your map if you enter the dungeon before you have advanced far enough in the quest No Stone Unturned.

The path to the previous tunnel has a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") at the start, which activates a [claw trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Claw "Skyrim:Claw") from the right. There is a Falmer on the ledge high above. By the pillar in the middle are two [Falmer ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Ear "Skyrim:Falmer Ear"), a random poison, and a small coin purse. There are some more wrecked carts and spilled goods and items behind the pillar, which include a few loose chaurus eggs, a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Battle of Red Mountain](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_Red_Mountain "Skyrim:Battle of Red Mountain")*, a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill book *[Mystery of Talara, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_v3 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, v3")*, a level-locked chest, another small coin purse, and some jewelry. On the ledge above is a master-locked chest. The path leads past an alcove on the right containing a potion sitting among mushrooms, then proceeds into another room with two Falmer, one patrolling and one standing watching the passage. At the bottom of the ascending stone ramp is a table with two poisons, a leveled potion, a leveled dagger, and a [skeever tail](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail"), while a Falmer chest is in the tent at the top.

The next tunnel is guarded by a skeever, and leads to a room with a winding path upwards. At the bottom is a table with some ingredients, a [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a small coin purse, and a *[Ruined Trailbook](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Trailbook "Skyrim:Ruined Trailbook")*. It provides details as to why the caravan tried to cross under the mountains. Just before you reach the next tanning rack and table with an assortment of [alchemical](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") and [smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") items, four Falmer will appear from around the room. There is a small side room that holds a Falmer chest, a potion, and a chaurus egg sac. The next room has a Falmer in the tent to the left, and across the bridge, another Falmer in the tent to the right, two more near the fire to the left, and a chaurus in between them. Between the fire and the gated exit from this room is an unlocked boss chest standing on end, making it easy to miss. On the right wall a short distance past the gate is a [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein"). The path continues to the north of the waterfall, which is the same waterfall encountered at the start of this section. The path leads around to the left, across some pipes, and back to the first zone *Tolvald's Cave*.

You emerge in a small room in the first zone with a pull chain that opens a stone door, past which is the abandoned camp in the first room of the dungeon.

| Plants |
| --- |
| 21 [Bleeding Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown")  14 [Blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort")  13 [Fly Amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita")  282 [Glowing Mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom")  20 [Imp Stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool")  17 [Namira's Rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot")  1 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")  2 [Snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries")  25 [White Cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") |

## Notes

- The dungeon contains the highest number (282) of glowing mushrooms and the second-highest number (243) of chaurus eggs in the game.
- There is an iron ore vein a short distance northwest of the entrance.
- The path leading to the Crown of Barenziah will be blocked by rubble until you're given the quest No Stone Unturned by [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex").
- In the room where the Crown of Barenziah is found, there is a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") on the ground which you may not be able to interact with. It is to the right of the path immediately before you cross the first stream. The activation spot is tiny, just between the knapsack buckle and the rock the knapsack is leaning against. There is a lootable dead chaurus opposite.
- During No Stone Unturned, there's a chance only a single male Dunmer Ghost shows up by the crown and that it's not hostile. When talked to, he may say something along the lines of "It's been so many years...", or he may not speak at all. He can also be pickpocketed for an [Elven Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Shield "Skyrim:Elven Shield").

## Bugs

- Some of the bodies in *Tolvald's Gap* disappear abnormally quickly.
- A knapsack in *Tolvald's Crossing* cannot interacted with. It appears to be placed awfully close to a rock formation.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- During No Stone Unturned, the Dunmer Ghosts in the cave can become hostile towards each other due to an improper faction setup.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.0, fixes this bug.
- During No Stone Unturned, the Dunmer Ghosts do not drop proper ghost loot or turn into the right kind of ash piles when killed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.6, fixes this bug.
- During No Stone Unturned, one of the Dunmer Ghosts in the cave has 4 Elven maces in its inventory, when it doesn't need that many.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.8, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  Tolvald's Cave
- 

  Tolvald's Gap
- 

  Tolvald's Crossing

# Skyrim:Totems of Hircine

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [90.222.231.175](/wiki/Special:Contributions/90.222.231.175 "Special:Contributions/90.222.231.175"), checked by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70") |

The Totem of Brotherhood in its receptacle in the Underforge

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to the indicated location on your map.
2. Retrieve the Totem by any means necessary.
3. Return to the [Underforge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Underforge "Skyrim:The Underforge"), then use one of the totem receptacles to complete the quest and receive your reward.

### Accepting the Quest

Asking [Aela the Huntress](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress"), *"Is there any work to be done?"* will prompt her to tell you about the Totems of Hircine. She will say that she has located one and would be honored if you go with her to retrieve it. If you accept the quest, she will become your Shield-Sister and will replace your current companion.

### Retrieve the Totem of Hircine

Aela prays to the Totem

Journey to the location given by Aela and kill the enemies lurking around. The location is [radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"), and it can be any [animal den](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Animal_Dens "Category:Skyrim-Places-Animal Dens"), [vampire lair](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Vampire_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Vampire Lairs"), or [warlock lair](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs") with a boss chest. The totem is most often found in the boss chest. Once you have the totem, Aela will approach and ask if you have it. When you tell her you do, she will tell you to bring it back to the [Underforge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Underforge "Skyrim:The Underforge"). When you return to the Underforge, place the totem on the marked area—the quest will finish and you will receive a leveled amount of gold. You can now pray to the totem to receive a new power while in [Beast Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Beast_Form "Skyrim:Beast Form"), which replaces your old one.

There are three total totems, each granting a different ability in Beast Form.

### Reward

| Levels[†](#intnote_LevelNote) | Reward[‡](#intnote_RewardBug) | USLEEP Reward |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 100 | 100 |
| 10–19 | 150 | 150 |
| 20–29 | 300 | 200 |
| 30–39 | 300 | 250 |
| 40+ | 300 | 300 |

[†](#note_LevelNote)Level is based on when the player completed the previous quest (or level one for the first quest), not the player's level when receiving the quest or its reward.

[‡](#note_RewardBug)The reward amounts for radiant Companions quests do not progress as intended.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=20007))

## The Totems of Hircine

Left to Right: Totem of the Hunt, Totem of Fear, Totem of Brotherhood

The totems are described in detail in the tome, *[The Totems of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Totems_of_Hircine "Skyrim:The Totems of Hircine")*. By praying to these totems, you will be given a unique ability that replaces the older Howl of Terror; it is activated by pressing the shout button while in [beast form](/wiki/Skyrim:Beast_Form "Skyrim:Beast Form"). All abilities last for 60 seconds, though the duration can be increased by 15 seconds by equipping the [Ring of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Ring of the Moon")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") before activating Beast Mode.

- **Totem of Fear**: Causes [Fear](/wiki/Skyrim:Fear_(spell) "Skyrim:Fear (spell)")
- **Totem of Brotherhood**: Summons 2 [Pack Members](/wiki/Skyrim:Pack_Member "Skyrim:Pack Member")
- **Totem of The Hunt**: Grants [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(effect) "Skyrim:Detect Life (effect)")

## Notes

- If [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed, some radiant locations may be on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). If you are in Skyrim, you will not receive a quest marker pointing you to the quest location, but must travel to Solstheim first (at which point any quest markers you have to quests in Skyrim will disappear).
- The location you are sent to may be an already "cleared" location, even if there are other non-cleared locations of the same type yet to be cleared or even discovered: the game does not, in this case, appear to prioritize new locations over known locations.
- You can only trigger this quest if you are still a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf"). If you have purified yourself, you are unable to do this quest.
- If Whiterun is under attack, you cannot enter the [Underforge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Underforge "Skyrim:The Underforge") until Whiterun is back to normal. It will tell you a key is needed to enter and that it cannot be lockpicked.
- At the end of this quest, Aela will begin praying to the new totem in the Underforge. It is possible to ask her to follow you while she is praying; her dialogue will change, and she will allow you access to her inventory, but will not stop praying or move away from the totem.
- Aela will not give these quests while she is an active follower, though she will give Animal Extermination quests.
- As you and Aela recover each totem, once she tells you to return the totem to the Underforge, speaking to her will only cause her to say *"This is not the time for talk. Let's get to the Underforge and see what this can do.*" You also won't be able to ask her for training in [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") until then.
- If you have just dropped off a totem in the Underforge, Aela will be praying to it and only offer an Animal Extermination quest (dialogue option, *"I'm looking for work"*). Leave the Underforge, return, then talk to Aela again. Repeat until Aela (still in prayer) offers the next totem quest (dialogue, *"Is there any work to be done?"*).
- This quest is considered by the game as 1 even if it appears 3 times in the journal (once for each totem). This means that the counter for "Quests Completed" and "The Companions Quests Completed" will permanently increase by 1 only by the end of the third quest (it appears as increased by 1 every time you complete one of the three quests, but it will drop back in a few in-game cell loadings).

## Bugs

- Although you receive the message that she has replaced your current follower, Aela might not replace them but instead join as a secondary follower, lacking the standard follower dialogue options. **?**
  - This bug was observed with [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") (after completion of [Kindred Judgment](/wiki/Skyrim:Kindred_Judgment "Skyrim:Kindred Judgment") and cured of vampirism) as primary follower, so it may be due to an interaction with her unique framework.
- If you've completed [A Daedra's Best Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Daedra%27s_Best_Friend "Skyrim:A Daedra's Best Friend"), you may be taken to Haemar's Cavern and your system can lock up when entering Haemar's Shame. You won't be able to complete the quest and will have Aela as a follower, but with no dialogue options.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
  - This also seems to happen if the totem is located in Morvunskar, and [A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember") has been completed. This can be worked around by carefully navigating around the point where the portal to the Misty Grove was placed earlier. **?**
  -  This can be resolved by manually advancing the quest with the console command `setstage cr12 20`.
- Curing yourself of lycanthropy while this quest is active causes the Underforge door to become unresponsive. You cannot end the quest or get rid of Aela as a result.
  - You can finish the quest using the console command `coc "WhiterunUnderForge"` and placing the totem in its place, but Aela may stay inside, forcing you to use the command each time. **?**
- Aela is supposed to comment on each totem you find with unique dialogue. She repeats the first one because the dialogue doesn't check the totem count variable.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- While recovering a totem located in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund"), it is possible that one of the swinging axe traps may knock Aela through a hole in the map, rendering the quest un-fulfillable. Aela may reappear at a later time although the trigger is unknown. Common factors such as fast traveling and waiting are worth trying. **?** One method that has been found effective is to pray at one of the previously acquired totems. Aela may then appear at the entrance of the Underforge.
- If Aela won't give you the first totem quest, check the status of this quest with the console command `sqs cr12`. If both Stage 0 and Stage 1 are marked as completed (with a 1 behind the respective stage), use the console command `resetquest cr12`. It is recommended to do this after handing in an Animal Extermination quest but before asking for more work.
- If you do not complete all of the radiant quests of Aela the Huntress in the initial wave before advancing, you will be stuck doing Animal Extermination quests from her indefinitely, unable to collect the Totems of Hircine. **?**
  -  Firstly, use the console command `setstage CR12 1`. Then, get an [Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(A) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (A)") quest from Aela. Now use the console command `setstage CR01 20` or `setstage CR02 20` (depending on which version of the quest you're assigned), and return to Aela to finish the quest. Ask for work from her again and use the command `setstage CR12 20` to complete the quest, and go to the Underforge to place the totem, which completes this quest. Repeat these steps 2 more times for the remaining 2 totems. The crucial part seems to be to Tab out of the conversation before Aela finishes her voiceline, when finishing the Animal Extermination quest. If you keep her dialogue open, she will have another Animal Extermination for you. If you close the dialogue before she finishes, she will have a dialogue for the Totems of Hircine quest. Alternatively, this can be fixed by marrying Aela, then again asking her for work after deciding on a place to live. [*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Totems_of_Hircine#Animal_Extermination)*]
- If Aela is chosen as your wife, after completing a totem quest she will stay and pray at the totem and will not return home.
  -  This can be fixed on Xbox 360: You need lots of healing and dual-casting master illusionist abilities. Have her as a follower, take away all her weapons and give her a cheap sword. Then punch her enough times to get her to attack you (heal yourself as needed). Go through the front exit so you are outside of Jorrvaskr... she should follow you out and continue to attack you. Lead her off a good ways at which point, Dual-cast Calm on her and immediately talk to her and have her re-join you. Test her compliance by drawing a weapon or spell (she should do likewise, not just stand there - if she doesn't draw, restart the process). Once she's drawn a weapon, fast-travel to another location. She should now act normally, and if a spouse or steward, should remain at other locations when dismissed.
- When obtaining the quest for the second totem, your quest marker may point to Jorrvaskr instead of the dungeon indicated in your quest log. The reason is that the quest item spawned on the floor in the main hall of Jorrvaskr instead of in the intended dungeon. The quest item will not be located anywhere in the dungeon indicated in the quest log. **?**
  -  The item is located in an inaccessible cell within Jorrvaskr. By the way, this problem may also occur for another totem (e.g., the third instead of the second totem). Furthermore, the quest log may offer nothing more than the direction to go collect the totem. Anyway, to resolve this problem, open the console and type `movetoqt CR12` which will move the player to a small interior unlighted cell after closing the console. The totem will be found on the ground. Pick up the totem to advance the quest. Next reopen the console and type `player.moveto 1A697` and the player will now move to a position beside Aela the Huntress. She should then ask the player if he or she has the totem and the quest can now carry on as normal.
- Once you place the totems at their receptacles, praying at them may not affect you in any way. **?**
  - Leave the Underforge then re-enter, wait 24 hours, or do another quest for Aela.

## Quest Stages

| Totems of Hircine (CR12) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Aela has tracked one of the Totems of Hircine to <Alias=Dungeon>, and has come with me to retrieve it. *Objective 10:* Retrieve the Totem of Hircine |
| 20 |  | Aela and I retrieved a Totem of Hircine from <Alias=Dungeon>. *Objective 20:* Take the Totem to the Underforge |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 100.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CR12 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CR12`.

# Skyrim:Touching the Sky

## Overview

For the book, see [Touching the Sky (book)](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky_(book) "Skyrim:Touching the Sky (book)").

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dawnguard Dawnguard.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dawnguard_Dawnguard.png) | **Find and retrieve [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow").** |
