Serana confronts Vyrthur at the Temple of Auriel

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Locate [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow").
2. Speak to [Gelebor](/wiki/Skyrim:Knight-Paladin_Gelebor "Skyrim:Knight-Paladin Gelebor").
3. Fill the [Initiate's Ewer](/wiki/Skyrim:Initiate%27s_Ewer "Skyrim:Initiate's Ewer").
4. Kill [Vyrthur](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch-Curate_Vyrthur "Skyrim:Arch-Curate Vyrthur").
5. Retrieve Auriel's Bow.

### Last of the Snow Elves

Serana gazing out over the Forgotten Vale

After learning the location of [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow"), travel to [Darkfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave") in the far northwestern reaches of Skyrim, just south-southwest of the [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") [Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur").

The cave is very dark, so you may wish to light your way using torches, the [Vampire's Sight](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Sight "Skyrim:Vampire's Sight") ability, or [light](/wiki/Skyrim:Light "Skyrim:Light") spells. Follow the path, past a frostbite spider until you come to a bridge and what seems like a dead end. Once you try to cross back over the bridge, you will be forced, by either a rock trap or the bridge collapsing, into a very fast moving underground river that sends you downstream. Try to keep your head above the water, unless you have a [waterbreathing](/wiki/Skyrim:Waterbreathing_(effect) "Skyrim:Waterbreathing (effect)") ability. Eventually, you'll be thrown out of the current, and immediately attacked by a few [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). Continue along the cavernous path, until you reach a small camp with a dead Breton; a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave_Note "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave Note") on her body sheds light on what happened: [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll").

From here you can either head down the path beyond the dead Breton, where after negotiating a [falling boulders trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Traps") you will arrive in a chamber with two frost trolls. At the far western side is a stone shrine and [Knight-Paladin Gelebor](/wiki/Skyrim:Knight-Paladin_Gelebor "Skyrim:Knight-Paladin Gelebor"), one of the last two Snow Elves. Alternatively, you arrive immediately behind Gelebor by pulling the chain hidden behind the dead Breton's lean-to and taking the passage it reveals.

Speak to Gelebor, and he will offer you a deal: slay his brother, [Vyrthur](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch-Curate_Vyrthur "Skyrim:Arch-Curate Vyrthur"), who was corrupted by [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), and Gelebor will help you in obtaining Auriel's Bow. Vyrthur is hiding in the [Inner Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale) "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)") of the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"), a gigantic outdoor elven ruin with [Ayleid](/wiki/Lore:Ayleid "Lore:Ayleid")-like architecture. In order to make your way there you must fill a jug, the [Initiate's Ewer](/wiki/Skyrim:Initiate%27s_Ewer "Skyrim:Initiate's Ewer"), with water from five wayshrines: the Wayshrines of Illumination, Learning, Radiance, Resolution, and Sight.

### Seeking Illumination

The first wayshrine, the Wayshrine of Illumination, is in [Darkfall Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Passage "Skyrim:Darkfall Passage"), which can be accessed through the portal Gelebor opens. The Portal appears in the back of the shrine-like building that Gelebor raises from the ground. It may be invisible, with no Quest Marker pointing to it, but walking to the back of the shrine wall you will be able to activate the Portal none the less (see the [Bugs](#Bugs) section for more info).

The passage is just as dark as the cave, but is illuminated by tube worms, which look like odd pink flowers that retract into their tubes when you come near, whose faint pink light help to guide the way. Along the winding underground trek you will encounter several leveled [falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"); be sure to destroy any [chaurus cocoons](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Cocoon "Skyrim:Chaurus Cocoon") you come across before they have a chance to hatch. The shrine itself is in the final chamber of the passage, a radically different environment to the rest of the zone where [vale deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Vale_Deer "Skyrim:Vale Deer") and [vale sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Vale_Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Vale Sabre Cat") inhabit a small forest. The Shrine is tended to by [Prelate Sidanyis](/wiki/Skyrim:Prelate_Sidanyis "Skyrim:Prelate Sidanyis"), who will activate it for you. Fill your ewer from the font and head through the portal to the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale").

### Resolving to Learn and See

The Wayshrine of Resolution

The second wayshrine, the Wayshrine of Sight, can be found soon after emerging from Darkfall Passage into the Forgotten Vale and is tended to by [Prelate Athring](/wiki/Skyrim:Prelate_Athring "Skyrim:Prelate Athring"). It is to the north of the path that climbs up out of the entry vale through a set of stone arches, and west-northwest of the [Forgotten Vale Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Cave "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Cave"). To find it, stop at the highest stone arch just before entering a narrow pass and head north along the cliff side, past a small frozen pond and several fallen trees, until you reach a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore"). Just beyond is the Wayshrine, shrouded amidst a dense layer of fog.

The third shrine, the Wayshrine of Learning, is tended to by [Prelate Celegriath](/wiki/Skyrim:Prelate_Celegriath "Skyrim:Prelate Celegriath"). To reach it, head back to the stone arches and instead press on west, negotiating a narrow pass inhabited by [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). Make your way down to the narrow river valley to a skeleton and the [Unknown Book, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:Unknown_Book,_Vol._I "Skyrim:Unknown Book, Vol. I"); reading it will start the [Forgotten Vale Books Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Books_Quest "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Books Quest"). Head downstream for a little while to reach the wayshrine.

To reach the fourth shrine, the Wayshrine of Resolution, cross the river and make your way up the turnpike path until you reach a large, frozen lake. Beware of the two dragons, [Naaslaarum](/wiki/Skyrim:Naaslaarum "Skyrim:Naaslaarum") and [Voslaarum](/wiki/Skyrim:Voslaarum "Skyrim:Voslaarum"), who will attack you while you cross the lake (provided you have completed [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising")). The wayshrine, tended to by [Prelate Nirilor](/wiki/Skyrim:Prelate_Nirilor "Skyrim:Prelate Nirilor"), is above the northwest bank of the lake. Don't forget to pick up the [Drain Vitality](/wiki/Skyrim:Drain_Vitality "Skyrim:Drain Vitality") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Shout "Skyrim:Shout") from the large rock jutting out from the middle of the frozen lake south of this wayshrine.

### The Long Walk to Radiance

The fifth and final wayshrine, the Wayshrine of Radiance, is north of the Wayshrine of Resolution and is reached after a long, arduous trek through the Forgotten Vale and [Glacial Crevice](/wiki/Skyrim:Glacial_Crevice "Skyrim:Glacial Crevice"). To reach the latter, you can press on north and negotiate a long series of Falmer encampments and bridges suspended across the cliff-faces, or alternatively head southwest from the wayshrine across the mountainside and overlooking the lake. After a short while you arrive in a hanging valley with some [moonstone ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore"); from here you can head down to the entrance of the Crevice. If you're looking for *[Unknown Book, Vol. III](/wiki/Skyrim:Unknown_Book,_Vol._III "Skyrim:Unknown Book, Vol. III")* for the [Forgotten Vale Books Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Books_Quest "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Books Quest"), you can find it in a Falmer hut a couple of bridges before reaching the Crevice entrance.

The Crevice itself consists of a series of glacial chambers with icy ledges and rope bridges that ascend among a scattering of Falmer tents. Dispose of the many leveled Falmer and the odd [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") that occupy this zone until you once again emerge out into the Forgotten Vale. This [final part](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale#Falmer_Fissure "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") of the Vale consists of a confusing maze of Falmer tents and platforms crowded within a series of narrow, twisting canyons. Pick up *[Unknown Book, Vol. IV](/wiki/Skyrim:Unknown_Book,_Vol._IV "Skyrim:Unknown Book, Vol. IV")* from a hut in the second village just before the entrance to the tunnel which takes you to the Wayshrine of Radiance, tended to by [Prelate Edhelbor](/wiki/Skyrim:Prelate_Edhelbor "Skyrim:Prelate Edhelbor").

Vyrthur destroying Auriel's Chapel

### Breaching the Sanctum

Down the path from the Wayshrine of Radiance and across a stone bridge lies the [Inner Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale) "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)"). Pour water from your Ewer into the stone basin, and the door in front of you will be bathed in green light before opening. Inside you will find a number of chambers with frozen Falmer and chaurus. Many of the Falmer hold items that can be looted, which may cause one or more of them to break out of their icy state and attack you. There is a chest tucked away in a partially hidden corner, some loose items lying about, and a number of lootable skeletons that Serana will raise during combat. Head north through the chambers, placing the Ewer on any pedestals to open the gates nearby, until you reach an icy tunnel leading to [Auriel's Chapel](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale)#Auriel.27s_Chapel "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)"). This tunnel branches to the left and doubles back leading to another chest and some more loose items.

Once you enter Auriel's Chapel, jump down from the stone ledge where you emerge and you will arrive in a stone chamber full of frozen Falmer and chaurus. From this point, you will not be able to retreat but can only continue forward. Vyrthur sits on a throne at the far end of the room, behind an impenetrable claw-like barrier. Once you come near, he will come to life and commence a fierce battle: the frozen Falmer and chaurus will start unfreezing in groups, while Vyrthur periodically summons a [Frost Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Frost Atronach"), collapses parts of the ceiling and then hurls the broken boulders at you.

Once all enemies are defeated, in a mixture of rage and panic, Vyrthur will collapse the rest of the roof on you through a huge magical explosion, commencing a cutscene during which the only action you can undertake is walking or running. You awake to Serana telling you to get up and get on the balcony. Follow her until you reach Vyrthur, who will explain that after having been forsaken to [vampirism](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism") by [Auri-El](/wiki/Lore:Auri-El "Lore:Auri-El"), he created the [prophecy](/wiki/Lore:Tyranny_of_the_Sun "Lore:Tyranny of the Sun") that [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon") is chasing. By dousing [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow") with the blood of a Daughter of Coldharbour—Serana— Vyrthur would exact his revenge by corrupting Auri-El's influence on [Nirn](/wiki/Lore:Nirn "Lore:Nirn").

Understandably displeased, Serana will lift him by the throat but will be thrown back as Vyrthur uses magic to free himself from her grip and attacks you. Once he has been defeated, a wayshrine will appear and Gelebor will walk through it. He will be surprised that the real reason for Vyrthur's actions was vampirism rather than corruption by the Falmer and thank you by proclaiming you worthy to carry Auriel's Bow. He will also bless some [Sunhallowed arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunhallowed_Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Sunhallowed Elven Arrow") for you if you ask, and remain there if you wish to come back for more at any time. Retrieve Auriel's Bow from the newly-appeared wayshrine to complete the quest.

## Notes

- You may use [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow") to blot out the sun. It is not permanent and will only last until 7pm (which is sunset; you can shoot out the sun again the next day, as the sun will rise at 5am).
- After a wayshrine is opened, it will contain portals to three of the other four opened wayshrines, as well as to [Darkfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave").
- At the end of this quest there is an opportunity to gain a second permanent follower. Right after you kill the boss, Serana will stop following you around and you can fast travel away to grab a second follower. There isn't a direct return point, but you can fast travel back to Forgotten Vale and use the portals, then run quickly back through the castle and finish the quest by speaking with the NPC waiting for you and taking Auriel's Bow. This time, your second follower slot should be permanent - though you should make sure to have two followers for 'Kindred Judgement' and any plot quests that are instanced. You can swap your other follower, but never dismiss Serana or you will lose the second slot.
- If you have not killed Naaslaarum and Voslaarum it is possible for one of them to fly to the balcony and interfere in the fight with Vyrthur. They can even kill him for you.
- South of the Temple balcony is a hanging valley with a waterfall pouring from it down to the frozen lake. This valley is the location that the [Emerald Paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald_Paragon "Skyrim:Emerald Paragon") gives access to, and can be reached from the balcony by using the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout and careful cliff walking. What's more, you can easily use [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") to shout Vyrthur down the balcony, and give him a falling death.

## Bugs

**Note**: Nearly all of the bugs mentioned below occur because Gelebor, Serana, or Vyrthur have uncompleted scripts running. Be sure to allow any dialogue they are speaking to complete before taking further action. Also, make sure that the scripted actions with the Initiate's Ewer and the Wayshrines have completed before going on to the next wayshrine. Furthermore, when attempting the aforementioned by loading a saved game, some variables might not reset, thus rendering the attempt unaffected - shutting down Skyrim and launching it again will wipe out any residue from the memory.

- You may be able to ask Serana to wait somewhere even though this is clearly not intended in the scripting. She is supposed to refuse when you ask her to wait for the duration of this quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.2, addresses this issue. This was likely due to the previous quest's script not properly delaying things before this one starts. Serana's follower settings were ending up in an unreliable state as a result.
- Serana may attack Gelebor immediately after you finish the first dialogue with him, ceasing quest progression. **?**
  -  Using the console command `killall` will fix this. You will have to wait a bit, until dialogue starts between Serana and Gelebor. They will both remain in the crouched, dying position, but they will go back to normal once a new area is entered.
- Knight-Paladin Gelebor may not activate the first wayshrine.
  -  Open the console and select Gelebor, enter the code `disable`, then `enable`.
  -  Sometimes Serana can get stuck in combat mode, preventing her dialogue with Gelebor. Open the console and select Serana, enter the code `disable`, then `enable`.
  -  You can fix this problem by using the console command `setstage DLC1VQ07 50`. This fix will not work unless Serana is next to you when you first speak with Gelebor. Serana has extensive dialogue exchange with Gelebor which leads to him giving you the Initiate's Ewer. Without the Ewer in your inventory, advancing the quest stage to open the Wayshrine will not help you.[*verification needed — is this true?*]
- When you activate the first wayshrine, the portal may not appear. **?**
  - The portal may be invisible. Pressing the 'activate' button while standing in the back of the wayshrine may activate the invisible portal.
- When given the objective to fill the Initiates Ewer, one of the wayshrines may not give you any water making the quest impossible to complete.
  - Reloading and visiting the wayshrines in a different order may fix this.
  - If you can't get water because Skyrim thinks you are in combat, exit the cell then re-enter it.
- When you have finished collecting the ewer, and are about to pour it in the basin, it won't react and you will be stuck.
  -  If you have this problem, open the console and enter `GetStage DLC1VQ07` . If it returns 132.00, that means that somehow the quest progressed past the next stage of the quest. Since you cannot go back stages, the only way to solve this problem would be to use SetStage for every stage past "Gain Entry to the Inner Sanctum" until the current stage number is above 132 (meaning `SetStage DLC1VQ07 200` , completing the quest, giving you the bow, and starting the next quest). This will mean skipping quite a lot of stages, but there's no way to fix this bug at the moment without skipping.
  -  Alternatively you can use console command `coc DLC1FalmerTemple01` and `SetStage 110` (assuming you are just stuck at the basin).
  - If coc is useless, and your queststage is 110, use the [sapphire paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_Paragon "Skyrim:Sapphire Paragon"). You must use console command `tcl`, and then you can gain entry to the Inner Sanctum (remember to use `tcl` again after gaining entry). Then, leave from the Inner Sanctum via the door, and Serana will be with you again.
- After confronting Arch-Curate Vyrthur and defeating the first wave of unfrozen enemies, he may not react and spawn a second wave, ceasing quest progress. **?**
  - Each subsequent wave will only occur after all mobilized enemies have been killed. These enemies are not the frozen ones standing about but are spawned as the waves progress, sometimes replacing the frozen variety. Sometimes they spawn inside the architecture or get stuck in odd places. If area effect spells cannot kill them, reloading a save is your only recourse. After each wave there is a pause before Vyrthur gives another rant and unleashes the next wave. Sending an arrow or two, or an area damage spell in his direction may speed things along a little.
  -  This can also be fixed by using the command `killall` in the boss arena (note that both Vyrthur and Serana will be put in the bleed out state as both of them are set to essential at the moment and can't die) but this updates Vyrthur's scripts and can hopefully allow you to progress. If that's the case and Vyrthur summons the [Ancient Frost Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Ancient Frost Atronach"), immediately hit the console, click on Serana and use the command `resurrect`. Once you kill the Atronach, Vyrthur will do a shockwave and run to the balcony. As he reaches the balcony he will die (because he is not set to essential anymore), so just click on his corpse and `resurrect` him too, and that may trigger the following scene and boss fight to progress normally.
- You may be unable to kill Arch-Curate Vyrthur. **?**
  -  If that happens use the console command `killall`. You might have to give Serana the `resurrect` command in the console afterward.
- The final objective to 'Retrieve Auriel's Bow' may not properly register as completed as it should, even after picking it up. A message signifying the quest's completion will still turn up, though the game ceases to progress after that. Neither Serana nor Gelebor will have proper dialogue options, and the following quest, 'Kindred Judgement', does not begin.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
  -  Use the console command `setstage DLC1VQ07 200` to properly complete the final 'Retrieve Auriel's Bow' objective.
- After finishing the quest, Serana might not have the dialogue to start Kindred Judgment but will allow you to use her blood to make Bloodcursed arrows.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
  - Completing a minor side quest before fighting Vyrthur may fix this.
- The tier 5 Ancient Frost Atronach that is generated during this quest was incorrectly set to the same record as the tier 4 alias directly before it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug.
- You can talk to Serana about helping the snow-elf priests while playing the vampire and Dawnguard sides of the quest. This is an error as the Editor ID indicates it was supposed to be exclusive to the vampire side.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.3, addresses this issue. This was due to a missing variable check to be sure you are in fact playing for Harkon's side.

I've been given an Initiate's Ewer which will ultimately provide me access to the Chantry's Inner Sanctum where both Arch-Curate Vyrthur and Auriel's Bow are located. *Objective 50:* Survive Darkfall Passage |

| 200 | ☑ | It's been revealed to me that the Tyranny of the Sun was created by Arch-Curate Vyrthur as his revenge upon Auriel for rebuking him when he was turned into a vampire. He possessed Auriel's Bow, but still needed the blood of a pure vampire to complete his ritual. This placed Serana in mortal danger, and I had no choice but to destroy him. I now possess the final piece of the Tyranny of the Sun, Auriel's Bow. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 35, 36, 60, 65, 70, 80, 81, 82, 85, 86, 87, 90, 91, 92, 95, 96, 97, 105, 130, 131, 132.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1VQ07 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1VQ07`.

# Skyrim:Tower of Mzark

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

The Tower of Mzark

The **Tower of Mzark** is a small [Dwarven tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach"). The tower can only be initially accessed from Blackreach. It is in the southwestern corner of the cavern, on a spire between two waterfalls. There is a stone bridge over the river which connects to the northern face of the tower.

The tower has an [exterior](#Exterior), an [interior](#Tower_of_Mzark) zone, and the [surface exterior](#Surface) where the lift is.

## Related Quests

- **[Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane")**: Uncover the secrets of the mysterious Dwemer lockbox.
- **[Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge")**: Recover an [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll") to learn an [Ancient Secret](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend").
- **[Scroll Scouting](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_Scouting "Skyrim:Scroll Scouting")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Obtain information on the Dragon Elder Scroll.[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")
- **[Seeking Disclosure](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeking_Disclosure "Skyrim:Seeking Disclosure")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Bring the Elder Scrolls to [Dexion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus").[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")

### Exterior

After crossing over the bridge, you will see a winding set of stairs going down to your left, as well as a door ahead which opens to a lift that will take you up to the interior of the tower. Proceeding down the flight of stairs, you will come across an unlocked chest to your right, along with two pieces of [Dwemer scrap metal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ores_and_Ingots#Dwemer_Metal_.28Smeltable.29 "Skyrim:Ores and Ingots"): a [solid Dwemer metal](/wiki/Skyrim:Solid_Dwemer_Metal "Skyrim:Solid Dwemer Metal") and a [bent Dwemer scrap metal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bent_Dwemer_Scrap_Metal "Skyrim:Bent Dwemer Scrap Metal"). The chest will always contain either a piece of [jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Jewelry "Skyrim:Jewelry") or an [amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Amulet_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Specialty Gear") of one of the Nine Divines. Other leveled loot may include more jewelry, [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and/or [scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls "Skyrim:Scrolls").

Continuing down the flight of stairs, you will reach the southern face of the tower, with stone arches and a Dwemer pipe overhead. There is a [crimson nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Nirnroot "Skyrim:Crimson Nirnroot") growing among some mushrooms here. If you continue to proceed down the stairs, you will eventually reach a stone platform raised slightly above the water between the two waterfalls. Towards the west of the platform is a short flight of stairs going down into the water. Across the water to the south is a [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") campsite inhabited by three leveled Falmer. The camp has a Falmer chest, three [corundum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein"), and in the tent at the top of the hill, a Dwemer boss chest.

### Tower of Mzark

The first chamber inside the Tower of Mzark

Upon using the lift beyond the door on the northern face of the tower, you will arrive in a short corridor leading to a small chamber. After entering the chamber, immediately to your right is a stone chair and three tiers of shelves. There are forty-one [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book") resting on the shelves, as well as two [Dwemer gyros](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Gyro "Skyrim:Dwemer Gyro") and a random [heavy armor helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Helmets_2 "Skyrim:Armor"). There are also two Dwemer chests resting on the shelves, one of which has a novice-level lock. Directly opposite these shelves, in the east corner of the room, is another shelf with a random soul gem.

In the middle of the room, surrounded by more than a dozen stone benches, is an extinguished campfire with two pots hanging over it. One pot contains two samples of [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"), while the other pot contains one [glowing mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom"). Nearby is an unowned bedroll and a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") propped up against an unusable barrel.

Moving ahead to the far right (west) corner, you will see three stone chairs in front of two tables littered with twelve more ruined books. Resting on one of the tables is a copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Armorer's Challenge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Armorer%27s_Challenge "Skyrim:The Armorer's Challenge")*, as well as one of five random potions (a potion of [cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease"), [cure poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Cure_Poison "Skyrim:Potions"), [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), or [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina")). To the left of the skill book is a Dwemer shelf holding a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), a bowl of [spriggan sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan_Sap "Skyrim:Spriggan Sap"), two [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), and two [Dwemer plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Plate "Skyrim:Dwemer Plate"). A [Dwemer cog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Cog "Skyrim:Dwemer Cog") rests on top of the shelf.

On the opposite side, in the south corner of the room, is a symmetrical arrangement of three stone chairs, two tables, and another Dwemer shelf. The shelf contains eleven more ruined books, two Dwemer cogs, and another chest with a novice-level lock. The adjacent table holds an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), a [scroll of Candlelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Candlelight "Skyrim:Scroll of Candlelight"), a [scroll of Muffle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Muffle "Skyrim:Scroll of Muffle"), and various items of clutter. A [Dwemer dish](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Dish "Skyrim:Dwemer Dish") and a Dwemer plate are between the two tables. Resting on the other table with two more ruined books is a leveled [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength").

The Oculory's focusing lenses hanging in the main chamber

Continuing through the door to the southwest brings you to a short passage with two Dwemer urns on flanking shelves and a closed door at the end. The door leads you to a large circular main chamber which houses the Oculory, a curious device created by the Dwemer for unknown purposes. Enter the chamber and continue to move in a clockwise direction up the winding ramp, eventually reaching the Oculory. This device has numerous focusing lenses, and is used during the related quests [Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge") and [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane") to acquire an [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll") and extract information using the [Blank Lexicon](/wiki/Skyrim:Blank_Lexicon "Skyrim:Blank Lexicon"). Controls for the device are on a raised podium, which features several buttons and a receptacle for placing the lexicon. Behind the controls, along the back wall of the main chamber, is a Dwemer shelf with five Dwemer cogs piled up next to it. This is especially helpful to the Dragonborn during the first part of the quest [Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor").

Directly below the podium, you will find the skeletal remains of [Drokt](/wiki/Skyrim:Drokt "Skyrim:Drokt"), along with [his journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Journal_of_Drokt "Skyrim:Journal of Drokt") beside him. From reading his journal, you can deduce that he became obsessed with the Oculory, but died without successfully focusing it. Reading it may also aid you in solving the Oculory puzzle during the related quests. Drokt carries exactly eighteen gold, three pieces of [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal"), a roll of paper, a sample of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), and a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger").

Proceed through the door below the focusing controls along a short passage to the lift that will take you back to the surface.

### Surface

The lift on the surface with the abandoned campsite

Upon reaching the surface, you will find yourself in an enclosed area. Simply activate the lever to the right side of the gate to unlock it; this adds a new marker to your map if you have the [Runed Lexicon](/wiki/Skyrim:Runed_Lexicon "Skyrim:Runed Lexicon"), allowing you to fast travel to this lift. The lift, together with the three [Great Lifts](/wiki/Skyrim:Other_Places#Dwarven_Lifts "Skyrim:Other Places"), will now serve as an easy access point to [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach").

Outside the lift is an abandoned campsite with two tents. After exiting the lift, immediately to your left is a lit campfire with a pot hanging over it containing two [pheasant roasts](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Roast "Skyrim:Pheasant Roast"). To the right of the stairs is a table with [small](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Dwemer_Plate_Metal "Skyrim:Small Dwemer Plate Metal") and [large Dwemer plate metals](/wiki/Skyrim:Large_Dwemer_Plate_Metal "Skyrim:Large Dwemer Plate Metal"), a Dwemer plate, and a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). A knapsack leans against this side of the stairs next to a [shovel](/wiki/Skyrim:Shovel "Skyrim:Shovel"). Both tents contain unowned bedrolls, and between the two tents is an unlocked chest. Inside the larger tent lies an empty chest beside a sack and a table strewn with various equipment, including an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), and a [saw](/wiki/Skyrim:Saw "Skyrim:Saw"). If you approach the campsite first, you can enter the tower from there by putting a plate or platter against the wall, and sprinting your way across.

## Notes

- There is a second [crimson nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Nirnroot "Skyrim:Crimson Nirnroot") just northwest of the tower in Blackreach, under the stone bridge.
- There is an [ebony ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Ebony Ore Vein") northeast of the tower in Blackreach, on a small island nearby in the river.
- There is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") southwest of the lift on the surface, up the steep slope.
- Two [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") plants can be found near the lift on the surface, around the abandoned campsite.
- The **Tower of Mzark** and the surrounding area appears in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online") as [Mzark Cavern](/wiki/Online:Blackreach:_Mzark_Cavern "Online:Blackreach: Mzark Cavern")*.*

## Bugs

- The navmesh in the exterior area is incomplete and followers are unable to use the Great Lift as a result.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- The Tower of Mzark lift is erroneously marked as being in [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, addresses this issue. The tower has been set to be part of [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") instead.
- Everything outside of the tower may respawn despite it being classed as a "no reset zone".
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
- If you don't take the Elder Scroll during [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane") and eventually go on to end that quest without doing so, it becomes impossible to take the scroll later due to the activator being set for an alias in said quest.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.4, addresses this issue. The activator is instead set to use the alias in [Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge") to get the scroll since Elder Knowledge is a background quest that is never terminated during the life of the game.

## Maps

- 

  Tower of Mzark

# Skyrim:Towers

## Overview

Pinefrost Tower

This page lists all the **towers** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

### Imperial Towers

:    **[Abandoned Prison](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Prison "Skyrim:Abandoned Prison")** — A small Imperial prison southwest of Windhelm containing the ghosts of its drowned prisoners. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Abandoned+Prison)
:    **[Falkreath Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Watchtower "Skyrim:Falkreath Watchtower")** — A small ruined tower north of Falkreath containing a necromancer. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath+Watchtower)
:    **[Pinefrost Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinefrost_Tower "Skyrim:Pinefrost Tower")** — A small ruined tower northwest of Dragon Bridge containing leveled animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pinefrost+Tower)
:    **[Refugees' Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Refugees%27_Rest "Skyrim:Refugees' Rest")** — A small ruined tower east of Windhelm containing leveled animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Refugees%27+Rest)
:    **[Rift Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Watchtower "Skyrim:Rift Watchtower")** — A small tower east of Ivarstead containing Orc bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rift+Watchtower)
:    **[Shor's Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Watchtower "Skyrim:Shor's Watchtower")** — A small tower north-northeast of Shor's Stone. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shor%27s+Watchtower)
:    **[Snowpoint Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowpoint_Beacon "Skyrim:Snowpoint Beacon")** — A small tower southwest of Winterhold containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Snowpoint+Beacon)
:    **[Stendarr's Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Beacon "Skyrim:Stendarr's Beacon")** — A small tower southeast of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Stendarr%27s+Beacon)
:    **[Whitewatch Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Whitewatch_Tower "Skyrim:Whitewatch Tower")** — A small tower north-northeast of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whitewatch+Tower)
:    **[Widow's Watch Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Widow%27s_Watch_Ruins "Skyrim:Widow's Watch Ruins")** — A small ruined tower west-northwest of Solitude containing a hag. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Widow%27s+Watch+Ruins)

### Nordic Towers

:    **[Bannermist Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Bannermist_Tower "Skyrim:Bannermist Tower")** — A small ruined Nordic tower northwest of Falkreath containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bannermist+Tower)
:    **[Bleakwind Bluff](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakwind_Bluff "Skyrim:Bleakwind Bluff")** — A small ruined Nordic tower inhabited by hagravens and Forsworn, located northwest of Rorikstead on an outcrop of rock. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bleakwind+Bluff)
:    **[Cradle Stone Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Cradle_Stone_Tower "Skyrim:Cradle Stone Tower")** — A small ruined Nordic tower west of Bard's Leap Summit containing a hagraven. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cradle+Stone+Tower)
:    **[Dead Crone Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Crone_Rock "Skyrim:Dead Crone Rock")** — A small ruined Nordic tower inhabited by Forsworn, located south-southwest of Markarth, just above Hag Rock Redoubt. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dead+Crone+Rock)
:    **[Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch_(place) "Skyrim:Myrwatch (place)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch") — A mage tower player home east of Morthal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Myrwatch+%28CC%29)
:    **[Nilheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilheim "Skyrim:Nilheim")** — A small ruined Nordic tower east-northeast of Ivarstead containing bandits disguised as guards. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nilheim)
:    **[Peak's Shade Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Peak%27s_Shade_Tower "Skyrim:Peak's Shade Tower")** — A small ruined Nordic tower east of Falkreath containing a spriggan. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Peak%27s+Shade+Tower)
:    **[South Skybound Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:South_Skybound_Watch "Skyrim:South Skybound Watch")** — A small Nordic tower and ruin northeast of Helgen containing bandits and a giant frostbite spider. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skybound+Watch+Pass)
:    **[Sundered Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Sundered_Towers "Skyrim:Sundered Towers")** — A small pair of linked ruined Nordic towers southeast of Karthwasten containing Forsworn and hagravens. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sundered+Towers)
:    **[Valtheim Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Valtheim_Towers "Skyrim:Valtheim Towers")** — A small pair of linked ruined Nordic towers east of Whiterun containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Valtheim+Towers)

## Notes

- Version 2.0.7 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces the Imperial tower map icon for Widow's Watch Ruins with the one for Nordic towers.
- Version 4.1.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch") replaces Western Watchtower's [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") map icon with the one used for Imperial towers.

Pinefrost Tower

### Nordic Towers

:    **[Bannermist Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Bannermist_Tower "Skyrim:Bannermist Tower")** — A small ruined Nordic tower northwest of Falkreath containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bannermist+Tower)

:    **[Cradle Stone Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Cradle_Stone_Tower "Skyrim:Cradle Stone Tower")** — A small ruined Nordic tower west of Bard's Leap Summit containing a hagraven. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cradle+Stone+Tower)
:    **[Dead Crone Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Crone_Rock "Skyrim:Dead Crone Rock")** — A small ruined Nordic tower inhabited by Forsworn, located south-southwest of Markarth, just above Hag Rock Redoubt. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dead+Crone+Rock)
:    **[Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch_(place) "Skyrim:Myrwatch (place)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch") — A mage tower player home east of Morthal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Myrwatch+%28CC%29)
:    **[Nilheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilheim "Skyrim:Nilheim")** — A small ruined Nordic tower east-northeast of Ivarstead containing bandits disguised as guards. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nilheim)
:    **[Peak's Shade Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Peak%27s_Shade_Tower "Skyrim:Peak's Shade Tower")** — A small ruined Nordic tower east of Falkreath containing a spriggan. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Peak%27s+Shade+Tower)
:    **[South Skybound Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:South_Skybound_Watch "Skyrim:South Skybound Watch")** — A small Nordic tower and ruin northeast of Helgen containing bandits and a giant frostbite spider. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skybound+Watch+Pass)
:    **[Sundered Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Sundered_Towers "Skyrim:Sundered Towers")** — A small pair of linked ruined Nordic towers southeast of Karthwasten containing Forsworn and hagravens. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sundered+Towers)
:    **[Valtheim Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Valtheim_Towers "Skyrim:Valtheim Towers")** — A small pair of linked ruined Nordic towers east of Whiterun containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Valtheim+Towers)

## Notes

- Version 2.0.7 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces the Imperial tower map icon for Widow's Watch Ruins with the one for Nordic towers.
- Version 4.1.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch") replaces Western Watchtower's [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") map icon with the one used for Imperial towers.

# Skyrim:Towers

## Overview

Pinefrost Tower

This page lists all the **towers** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

### Imperial Towers

:    **[Abandoned Prison](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Prison "Skyrim:Abandoned Prison")** — A small Imperial prison southwest of Windhelm containing the ghosts of its drowned prisoners. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Abandoned+Prison)
:    **[Falkreath Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Watchtower "Skyrim:Falkreath Watchtower")** — A small ruined tower north of Falkreath containing a necromancer. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath+Watchtower)
:    **[Pinefrost Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinefrost_Tower "Skyrim:Pinefrost Tower")** — A small ruined tower northwest of Dragon Bridge containing leveled animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pinefrost+Tower)
:    **[Refugees' Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Refugees%27_Rest "Skyrim:Refugees' Rest")** — A small ruined tower east of Windhelm containing leveled animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Refugees%27+Rest)
:    **[Rift Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Watchtower "Skyrim:Rift Watchtower")** — A small tower east of Ivarstead containing Orc bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rift+Watchtower)
:    **[Shor's Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Watchtower "Skyrim:Shor's Watchtower")** — A small tower north-northeast of Shor's Stone. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shor%27s+Watchtower)
:    **[Snowpoint Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowpoint_Beacon "Skyrim:Snowpoint Beacon")** — A small tower southwest of Winterhold containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Snowpoint+Beacon)
:    **[Stendarr's Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Beacon "Skyrim:Stendarr's Beacon")** — A small tower southeast of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Stendarr%27s+Beacon)
:    **[Whitewatch Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Whitewatch_Tower "Skyrim:Whitewatch Tower")** — A small tower north-northeast of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whitewatch+Tower)
:    **[Widow's Watch Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Widow%27s_Watch_Ruins "Skyrim:Widow's Watch Ruins")** — A small ruined tower west-northwest of Solitude containing a hag. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Widow%27s+Watch+Ruins)

### Nordic Towers

:    **[Bannermist Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Bannermist_Tower "Skyrim:Bannermist Tower")** — A small ruined Nordic tower northwest of Falkreath containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bannermist+Tower)
:    **[Bleakwind Bluff](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakwind_Bluff "Skyrim:Bleakwind Bluff")** — A small ruined Nordic tower inhabited by hagravens and Forsworn, located northwest of Rorikstead on an outcrop of rock. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bleakwind+Bluff)

:    **[Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch_(place) "Skyrim:Myrwatch (place)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch") — A mage tower player home east of Morthal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Myrwatch+%28CC%29)
:    **[Nilheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilheim "Skyrim:Nilheim")** — A small ruined Nordic tower east-northeast of Ivarstead containing bandits disguised as guards. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nilheim)

# Skyrim:Toying With The Dead

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Retrieve a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil "Skyrim:Arondil")'s journals for an interested buyer.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Vekel the Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Vekel_the_Man "Skyrim:Vekel the Man") |
| Location(s): | [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"), [Yngvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild "Skyrim:Yngvild") |
| Reward: | Leveled one-handed enchanted weapon |
| ID: | FreeformRiften21 |
| Required Items: | [Arondil's Journal, Part 1](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil%27s_Journal,_Part_1 "Skyrim:Arondil's Journal, Part 1")  [Arondil's Journal, Part 2](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil%27s_Journal,_Part_2 "Skyrim:Arondil's Journal, Part 2")  [Arondil's Journal, Part 3](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil%27s_Journal,_Part_3 "Skyrim:Arondil's Journal, Part 3")  [Arondil's Journal, Part 4](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil%27s_Journal,_Part_4 "Skyrim:Arondil's Journal, Part 4") |
| Suggested Level: | 8 |
| Difficulty: | Medium |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business") | | |

Arondil on his throne

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to [Yngvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild "Skyrim:Yngvild").
2. Collect the four journals.
3. Return to [Vekel](/wiki/Skyrim:Vekel_the_Man "Skyrim:Vekel the Man").

### The Proposition

If you approach Vekel in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") and ask him for work, he will tell you about some journals that he's been after: *"I have a buyer with a very odd taste in literature, looking for some particular books. I'm told they're the ravings of a madman, a wizard named [Arondil](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil "Skyrim:Arondil") and his peculiar cravings. It's said to be in four volumes and very hard to come by. My client is offering quite a reward for them, which I'd split with you."* If you ask for him to elaborate further on the journals, he will go on to say, *"Recently, a woman was found... naked and shivering along the road to [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). The only information the guard could get from her were tales of strange experiments and Arondil scribbling in his journals."*

Asking about Arondil won't get you much, as Vekel says, *"Only rumors. He used to have a home in Dawnstar until they burned it down. The people say he was doing unspeakable experiments on reanimation... rituals only a necromancer would perform. After he made for Yngvild, he was never heard from again."*

Once you agree to retrieve the journals, he will conclude the conversation with: *"Then we have a deal. In his later years, Andoril*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *moved into some ice caves known as Yngvild. He prefered*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *the solitude in which to perform his, um... experiments."*

### Yngvild

The ruins of Yngvild

Yngvild is an ice cave located on an island northeast of Dawnstar. To access it, find the entrance on the north side by following the pathway up the island. Once inside, you are able to find the first three journals. The [first journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil%27s_Journal,_Part_1 "Skyrim:Arondil's Journal, Part 1") is located on a table near two [Yngvild ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild_Ghost "Skyrim:Yngvild Ghost") and a leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). The [second journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil%27s_Journal,_Part_2 "Skyrim:Arondil's Journal, Part 2") can be found on a table alongside a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") and a [scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Raise_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Raise Zombie"). The [third journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil%27s_Journal,_Part_3 "Skyrim:Arondil's Journal, Part 3") can be found on a table just before the door leading to [Yngvild Throne Room](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild_Throne_Room "Skyrim:Yngvild Throne Room").

### Yngvild Throne Room

Once you enter the main chamber in the throne room, you will see Arondil sitting on his throne with an Yngvild ghost alongside him. The [fourth](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil%27s_Journal,_Part_4 "Skyrim:Arondil's Journal, Part 4") and final part of the journal lies through the door behind him, on a table along with an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") for the quest [No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned"). Once you have retrieved the journals, you can exit the cave and head back to [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") to receive your reward.

### Reward

Return all four journals to Vekel and he will remark, *"Good. I was hoping you hadn't forgotten about it. As promised, here's your payment for bringing them to me. Got it as part of a fair trade from my client."* Your reward for returning the journals is a leveled and [enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting_Effects "Skyrim:Enchanting Effects") [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons").

## Notes

- You don't have to kill [Arondil](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil "Skyrim:Arondil") to complete the quest, merely get his journals.
- This quest can be started even if you're not a member of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") at all.
- Sneaking into the final chamber unnoticed and removing the Soul Gem from the pedestal next to Arondil causes the ghosts near him to attack and kill him.
- Objectives for this quest will add themselves to the quest log even if you'd never been to see Vekel about finding the books.
  - This is no longer the case with version 4.2.4 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch").

## Bugs

- Vekel will neither reward you on completion of the quest, nor take the journals.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9.26.0.8, addresses this issue. He will now reward you properly, and the journals will no longer be marked as quest items once the quest is complete, and can be dropped or sold.
- As stated above, Vekel does not actually remove the journals from your inventory upon quest completion, even with the Official Patch.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- This quest can be started without talking to Vekel; if you go to Yngvild and pick up all four journals, you will receive a quest update telling you to return them to Vekel, even if you never spoke to him before.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, addresses this issue. He has been given appropriate dialogue to acknowledge the fact that he had never given you the task to find the journals prior.

## Quest Stages

| Toying With The Dead (FreeformRiften21) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Enter Yngvild Barrow |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Retrieve Arondil's Journals (<Global=FFRiften21JFound>/4) |
| 40 |  | *Objective 30:* Return to Vekel |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften21 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften21`.

Traitor's Post

**Traitor's Post** is a crumbling [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") and [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") outpost east of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), and just north of the [Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah").

It is easily found by taking the road northeast from Windhelm towards the border with Morrowind. Once past the three farms on the right, it is the next building on the left, shortly after the road turns to the east.

## Related Quests

- **[Harsh Master](/wiki/Skyrim:Harsh_Master "Skyrim:Harsh Master")**: Take care of a runaway crew member. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Missing Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_Merchant "Skyrim:Missing Merchant")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail"): A powerful set of armor has come on the market.

## Traitor's Post

Traitor's Post

A small band of [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") have made it their home and attack any passing travelers. There are numerous [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes and various colors of [mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") along the road and around the shack, and also several [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") hidden among the vegetation around the building. The shack has no windows or doors, large holes in the ceiling and walls and no stairs leading up to the top floor. A hundred paces farther along the path is the path that leads up to the [Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah"), where the followers of [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah") worship.

The front of the shack has a typical decking area that is damaged like every other part of the building. To the right are a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") and a pile of firewood. Inside are four bandits including a boss-leveled chief. There is a fireplace in the middle of the northeast wall, with a long wooden table to the right against the same wall. On the table are a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), a [carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") in a cast iron pot, and a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"). In the southern corner is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") beside a stack of crates. In the center of the shack are two long wooden tables set end-to-end with three wooden benches. On the tables are a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), two [mammoth steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Steak "Skyrim:Mammoth Steak"), and a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks").

Where to go to reach the top level

There is a wardrobe against the wall towards the front of the building, while to the right, behind a partition wall, is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on the floor. Opposite the wardrobe against the northwest wall is a cupboard with a random [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") [cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor") and a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Dance in Fire, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v2 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v2")* on a shelf. At the northwestern end of the room, against the southwest wall, is a long wooden table with a random empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") and a random [stamina potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") on top. To the right, in the western corner, is a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"). In the northern corner are two hay piles for sleeping and a crate with a food sack on top.

To the northeast is a bedroom area used by the chief containing an unowned double bed in the corner with a dresser at the foot of the bed holding a couple of pieces of cheese. Beside this is a chair. In the southern corner of this area is a novice-locked chest with a random pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor") beside it along with another food sack. There are several barrels around the room; some contain food, and others [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients").

Top floor

It is possible to access the top floor via some rocks helpfully piled up against the rear of the shack. Once you are on the main roof, you need to jump to the wing over the chief's bedroom area in order to climb to the peak of the roof. From there, you can jump back to the main roof at a far higher level, enabling you to drop in through a hole in the roof over the top floor at the southeastern end of the building. The top floor has two unowned single beds, one on each side. On the floor near the foot of the bed against the southwest wall is a random [healing potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), while by the foot of the other bed is a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") on a crate with a random [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") leaning against it. The floor is missing at the northwestern end of the room, with a master-locked boss-level chest and a chair by the edge of the floor. The hole enables you to drop down once you've finished upstairs.

## Notes

- A chest with a novice-level lock on the main floor inside the house contains [Treasure Map VII](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_VII "Skyrim:Treasure Map VII").

## Bugs

- NPCs may only able to be use the double bed on one side due to its placed position against the wall.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, addresses this issue. The double bed is now a singular bed.
- The bandit leader here isn't named "Bandit Chief" like bandit bosses with the same template at similar locations. Instead, he is assigned a random leveled bandit name.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.2, fixes this bug.

Treva River

**Treva River** is a river in the center of [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift").

Geographically, the Treva River should flow from [Lake Honrich](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Honrich "Skyrim:Lake Honrich") past [Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch") and into [Lake Geir](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Geir "Skyrim:Lake Geir") (see [Bugs](#Bugs)).

## Bugs

- The water current markers are pointing in the wrong direction, so the river actually flows from Lake Geir towards Lake Honrich. **?**
