Treva's Watch

**Treva's Watch** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southeast of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). It contains two zones: *[Treva's Watch Escape Tunnel](#Treva.27s_Watch_Escape_Tunnel)* and *[Treva's Watch](#Treva.27s_Watch)*.

You may wish to get the quest [Infiltration](/wiki/Skyrim:Infiltration "Skyrim:Infiltration") from [Stalleo](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalleo "Skyrim:Stalleo") before entering the fort for the first time; Stalleo is camped with two [bodyguards](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalleo%27s_Bodyguard "Skyrim:Stalleo's Bodyguard") just east of the fort. The quest directs you to access the fort through its secret escape tunnel.

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Infiltration](/wiki/Skyrim:Infiltration "Skyrim:Infiltration")**: Help [Stalleo](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalleo "Skyrim:Stalleo") take back Treva's Watch.
- **[Retrieval](/wiki/Skyrim:Retrieval "Skyrim:Retrieval")**: Journey to a random location to retrieve a fragment of [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The fort is off the road between Ivarstead and [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") on the north shore of the [Treva River](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva_River "Skyrim:Treva River"). A camp with two small tents and bedrolls occupied by Stalleo and his two bodyguards is located near a secret back entrance to the fort east of the main entrance. There is a cart containing a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel and a sack nearby. Speaking with Stalleo, you can offer your services to help reclaim his home. Approaching the fort will cause several bandit archers to fire upon you from the walls. The main courtyard area comprises several levels, and is initially occupied by six bandits, including archers and some heavy hitters. If exiting into the courtyard from the main keep, you appear inside a wooden hut with a lever that lowers the spears blocking access to the courtyard for Stalleo and his bodyguards, although you may wish to wait until you've taken care of any remaining bandits, especially at higher levels. Opposite the hut are wooden stairs leading up to the battlements, which feature a campfire with four whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") hanging over it, a long wooden table with five [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steaks and three bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and a set of shelves holding two more bottles of wine. To the east are more stairs leading up to a higher level, where another campfire has been lit. Two lean-tos with unowned bedrolls under them are around the fire, with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and a long wooden table beside one of the lean-tos. An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") can be found southeast of the fort, and another one can be found west of here.

### Treva's Watch Escape Tunnel

Typically you will enter this fort through the secret entrance, which leads to the basement. The entrance places you in a man-made tunnel descending to the west, then turning to the south and climbing a flight of stairs. At the top are three bandits: two archers and a melee fighter. They are all standing in an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick"), with an [oil lantern](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") hanging above. Behind them is a long wooden table holding six loose [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), a loose random [arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows"), a bottle of wine, and a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), with a random [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") leaning against the table. To the left is a food barrel, and to the right is a set of shelves holding two sheaves of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), two loaves of bread, and four sliced and whole cheese wheels. The room opens up to the west, with a passage heading south, and beyond this to the west a storage area on a slightly raised platform guarded by a bandit sitting at a long wooden table. On the table is a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), a random [cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"), a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). Behind this are two sets of shelves separated by an unlocked chest, with a second unlocked chest to the right of the shelves. The shelves hold a single random arrow, two empty random [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and two food sacks.

Following the passage south, you can hear someone hammering metal at an anvil. A [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") is on the floor in the middle of the passage, after which the passage turns to the east. In front is a flight of stairs leading up into an L-shaped room, with a smaller room ahead through a large doorway. This is where the person working with metal is located. The smaller room contains a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), and two sets of shelves. One of the sets of shelves holds a piece of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"), six [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), and four leather strips, with a fifth strip on the workbench. The other set of shelves holds a random light armor cuirass, two pairs of light armor [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"), a [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), and two swords. There is a second wide doorway out into the L-shaped room. Here there are three more sets of shelves and a smaller shelving unit, which between them hold many small barrels of mead, a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), three bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), seven bottles of wine, six bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two random [potions of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and a random [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"). To the west is a small storeroom filled with many food barrels and the bodies of two [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_(dead) "Skyrim:Nord (dead)") and an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_(dead) "Skyrim:Imperial (dead)"), presumably family and members of Stalleo's household related to the storyline of the quest Infiltration. A door to the south opens into *Treva's Watch*.

### Treva's Watch

The entrance from the escape tunnel leads into a passage that twists and turns, with two bear traps on the floor. Ahead are stairs leading up to a wider passage. Just before the stairs is an alcove on the left with a short passage opposite that ends at a cave-in. At the top of the stairs is a bandit, with a second farther back out of sight who will be alerted even to a stealthy kill of the first ruffian. Where the passage widens, a cupboard is on the left, with a long wooden table opposite. On the table is a bucket containing two bottles of wine, while the cupboard holds a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"), an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and a woodcutter's axe. The passage continues to the south, where a doorway on the right opens into a dormitory with two bandits: one sleeping in the first bed, the second standing at the rear of the room. Any fighting may alert one of the bandit chiefs to your presence. There are three single unowned beds in the room, an unlocked chest at the foot of the middle bed, and two sets of shelves against the wall holding three random cuirasses, a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), a potion, a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), and several [common books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"). Opposite the doorway is an adept-locked door that opens into a small storeroom containing an unlocked chest, a tall wardrobe, and a set of shelves holding a random [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), a bottle of poison, a random potion of healing, a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), a [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), and two food sacks. There is also a food barrel with a large coin purse on top.

Continuing along the passage, you pass an alcove on the right containing a set of shelves holding a random sword, [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), and bow, two random pairs of boots, and a random helmet. Just beyond the alcove, the passage turns to the west and passes a doorway on the left, which is where the bandit chief will be found if not previously alerted to your presence. In this room is an unowned double bed, a dresser, a tall wardrobe, an unlocked chest, and a long wooden table with a *[Spell Tome: Bound Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Bound_Sword "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Bound Sword")* on top. The passage turns to the north at the far end, and leads out onto a balcony over a dining room, where you can see three bandits sitting and chatting to each other at a pair of tables laid end-to-end. On the balcony is a long wooden table with two common books and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge") on top. Farther along is a set of shelves holding a leather strip, a leveled [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), and a leveled potion of regeneration. To the left is a stack of straw bales, with stairs leading down to the left. At the bottom is a second pair of tables under the balcony, with many chairs pulled up to both pairs of tables. To the left of the stairs is a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). To the west is a doorway out into a narrow passage.

There is a cave-in at the south end of the passage. After a few paces north, the passage turns west and opens into a kitchen where you will encounter two more bandits. There are several tables and small shelving units down the middle of the room, with two campfires against the west wall, one with a kettle in the flames, and the other with a proper [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") over it. On the tables and shelves are two joints of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), three [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), an apothecary's satchel, a rack of [dog meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog_Meat "Skyrim:Dog Meat"), three [chicken breasts](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken_Breast "Skyrim:Chicken Breast"), an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), a woodcutter's axe, a bottle of alto wine, three bottles of wine, a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), and two random potions of healing. Hanging from racks over one of the tables are two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"), and a bunch of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"). There is a set of shelves against the west wall holding clutter, and a long wooden table against the north wall with a bottle of wine between two small mead barrels. In the northwestern corner is a doorway into another room containing several food barrels and sacks, two more sets of shelves holding several more food sacks, and an unlocked chest, with a wooden door to the north.

This door opens into a wide passage. To your right on the floor is a bottle of alto wine and a large coin purse, and beyond that a doorway with some rubble on the left, behind which is a raw [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat") and a small coin purse. The passage ends at the other side of the cave-in seen previously. Take care heading west, as just before the corner, there is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") on the floor that triggers a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") hinged on the right wall. Around the corner, a narrow passage leads off to the west and climbs a short flight of stairs before opening into a large circular room, with a table and a set of shelves in the middle, many food barrels in stacks around the outside, a second set of shelves on the west wall with two bottles of Nord mead and a bottle of wine, and a couple carts on the right holding seven [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). On the first set of shelves is a piece of iron ore, six iron ingots, and two leather strips, with another piece of iron ore on the table. To the south is a wide doorway, with a passage opposite and curved stairs rising on your right.

Partway up the stairs is a bandit standing guard near a long wooden table. The bandit is standing in an oil slick, with an oil lantern hanging above. At the top of the stairs is another large circular room, half of which is raised up a couple feet, with stairs at either end. On this raised section you will find the second bandit chief along with one more bandit. There is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), an unlocked boss chest and a set of shelves holding six iron ingots, an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") to the left, and a tall wardrobe and a dresser back-to-back with them. The wardrobe and dresser both contain clothes, while beside them is a ladder leading outside to the roof of the tower, where you can loot an unlocked chest and snipe any remaining bandits outside. To the right of the enchanter is a long wooden table holding a knapsack, a bottle of the rare [enchanter's elixir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanter%27s_Elixir "Skyrim:Enchanter's Elixir"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a bottle of wine, a small coin purse, a *[Spell Tome: Courage](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Courage "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Courage")*, and copies of *[Ruins of Kemel-Ze](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Kemel-Ze "Skyrim:Ruins of Kemel-Ze")* and the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Twin Secrets](/wiki/Skyrim:Twin_Secrets "Skyrim:Twin Secrets")*. Behind the table is another tall wardrobe and a set of shelves holding a giant apothecary's satchel, a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), an iron dagger, and a copy of *[On Oblivion](/wiki/Skyrim:On_Oblivion "Skyrim:On Oblivion")*. On the lower level between the two flights of stairs is another set of shelves holding five more common books, a pair of [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers") hidden in a cast iron pot, two sheaves of wheat, and a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch").

From the bottom of the stairs, following the passage to the south, you pass two doorways into a prison area on your left, where two bandits are found talking. There are two cells along the eastern wall, one adept-locked, and the other apprentice-locked. Between the two cells, on a hook on the wall or fallen to the floor is a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch_Prison_Key "Skyrim:Treva's Watch Prison Key") that opens the cells. In the center of this room are two long wooden tables side-to-side, with many [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle") in a stack of open crates beside them and loose on the floor. On the tables are two [legs of goat roast](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat_Roast "Skyrim:Leg of Goat Roast"), a [horse haunch](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Haunch "Skyrim:Horse Haunch"), two bottles of wine, and three pieces of bread. On the floor beside the table is a basket of red and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"). Between the two doorways are two tables, one of which has a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") on top. Beside this is another basket of apples. In the northwestern corner is a cupboard, with three bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") coin, a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#00080699 "Skyrim:Boots"), and a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes#00086991 "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") on the shelves. Hanging from a rack from the ceiling are three garlic braids. Against the north wall is a tall wardrobe with an unlocked chest to the right. More food barrels are in the northeastern corner. Finally, against the south wall is another table with an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel") on top.

Take care when continuing along the passage, as a pressure plate that triggers a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") is a short distance past the prison area. Past this on your left is a doorway into a room with a bandit sitting at a long wooden table on the left with a bottle of wine on top, while against the south wall is a tall wardrobe and a set of shelves holding several tiny food barrels and an [iron greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword"). There is a pile of firewood opposite, with a woodcutter's axe leaning against it. To the east is a door leading outside into the courtyard. Before exiting, the passage continues past this room and another pressure plate that triggers a [swinging mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace") trap before ending at a cave-in, with an unlocked chest containing minor loot among the rubble.

## Notes

- Despite returning the fort to Stalleo's care through the related quest, Stalleo and his bodyguards return to the camp and never take control of the fort, while the bandits respawn, enabling you to repeatedly clear the fort.
- There are two [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") on the shore to the south and west of the fort, and on the far side of the river to the west is a [clay deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay_Deposit "Skyrim:Clay Deposit")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire").
- Treva's Watch is built on the land of the former [Treva's Farm](/wiki/Online:Treva%27s_Farm "Online:Treva's Farm") found in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- If [Rescue Mission](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_Mission "Skyrim:Rescue Mission") sends you here, kidnapped NPCs can be seen clipping with the cell door.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.1130, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  Treva's Watch
- 

  Treva's Watch Escape Tunnel

# Skyrim:Trinity Restored

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. The Nightingale induction ceremony

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") and [Karliah](/wiki/Skyrim:Karliah "Skyrim:Karliah") at the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(place) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (place)").
2. Meet Karliah at The Shadow Stone just outside [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
3. Enter [Nightingale Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Hall "Skyrim:Nightingale Hall") and follow Karliah's instructions.
4. Equip the [Nightingale Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Armor "Skyrim:Nightingale Armor").
5. Proceed further into the cave and follow Karliah's instructions.
6. Speak to Brynjolf about the leadership of the Guild.

### Plans Revealed

Return to the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(place) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (place)") after your search at [Riftweald Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Riftweald_Manor "Skyrim:Riftweald Manor") to show [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") [Mercer's](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey") plans for stealing the Eyes of the Falmer. Brynjolf will explain the significance of your findings; Mercer plans one more heist before disappearing for good. The only hope of catching him is to intercept him at the location. Brynjolf informs you that [Karliah](/wiki/Skyrim:Karliah "Skyrim:Karliah") has requested to speak with both of you.

### A Secret Order

When you speak to Karliah, she reveals to you and Brynjolf that Mercer Frey was a [Nightingale](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingales "Skyrim:Nightingales"), an agent of [Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Nocturnal "Skyrim:Nocturnal"). Because of this, Karliah is concerned about being at full strength and on equal footing before pursuing Mercer. She asks you and Brynjolf to meet her at [The Shadow Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shadow_Stone "Skyrim:The Shadow Stone") outside of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

### The Nightingale Edge

Here you will find yourself at the entrance to [Nightingale Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Hall "Skyrim:Nightingale Hall") wherein is the edge over Mercer that Karliah was alluding to. Proceed inside, but don't get too far ahead as Karliah begins telling you more about the [Nightingales](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingales "Skyrim:Nightingales") and their role. She will later remark that this was the Nightingales' base, and that she will return here once done with Mercer. After crossing a bridge, you can find a copy of the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Purloined Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Purloined_Shadows "Skyrim:Purloined Shadows")* to the right.

Your first stop is the armor chamber. Activate the stone Karliah indicates and the [Nightingale Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Armor "Skyrim:Nightingale Armor") is placed in your inventory. You must equip it in order to continue. Once you have donned the armor, Karliah will discuss the next step: your sworn oath to Nocturnal. Follow Karliah further into the cave past side passages leading to sleeping quarters where you can find a copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") skill book *[The Red Kitchen Reader](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Kitchen_Reader "Skyrim:The Red Kitchen Reader")* and living spaces.

### Trinity Restored

The first step towards your induction.

Once you have agreed to Nocturnal's conditions on becoming a Nightingale, Karliah will operate the pull chain for the gate leading into the Hall's "Welkinsight Chamber"[[1]](#cite_note-TESVSPOGG-1):298 where you will take your oath to become a Nightingale. You will be directed to stand on a specific platform. If you have a follower with you, their presence does not affect the outcome in any way. Karliah summons Nocturnal and asks to resume her role as a Nightingale as well as induct you and Brynjolf into their ranks. Nocturnal agrees.

Now that you are officially inducted into the Nightingales, Karliah will explain that Mercer got into the vault by using the [Skeleton Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton_Key "Skyrim:Skeleton Key") which he stole from the [Twilight Sepulcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher"); a grievous insult to Nocturnal which threatens the very foundations of the Nightingales. The key needs to be returned to the Sepulcher to set things right and return the uncanny luck of the Thieves Guild.

This is a big day for you as now Brynjolf has something to add. With Mercer disgraced, the issue of the leadership of the Thieves Guild is at hand. Brynjolf states that he and Karliah think you would be the right person for the job, once you've proven yourself by dealing with Mercer and completing all of the Thieves Guild additional jobs. From here, leave for [Irkngthand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand "Skyrim:Irkngthand") to begin [Blindsighted](/wiki/Skyrim:Blindsighted "Skyrim:Blindsighted").

## Notes

- Although Karliah insists that you equip the Nightingale armor, you can then immediately unequip it again if you prefer your existing armor. It is not necessary to wear the Nightingale armor during the oath-taking ceremony.
- There is no way to proceed with the questline without swearing service to Nocturnal intermittently during your lifetime and permanently after your death.

## Bugs

- Brynjolf may not begin walking towards Karliah in the Ragged Flagon and the dialogue will not initiate to begin the quest.
  - Reloading from an earlier save may fix this.
  -  Use the console command `setstage TG08A 15` to have her start speaking, regardless.
  -  If Karliah or Brynjolf are stuck (won't move, don't complete actions), the console command `resurrect` will sometimes force them to resume their usual scripted behavior.
- It's possible that Brynjolf will walk away when you've arrived in the hall and are asked to get your armor.
  - Push him through the cave.
  -  You can use the console by clicking on him (or typing `prid 20545`), and then typing `moveto player` to teleport him to you. Make sure he's near you when you don the armor when Karliah is about to ask you to take the oath, which should fix his AI (confirmed by his comment on his new outfit).
  -  If only you and Karliah make it to the stones before taking the oath and Brynjolf is still walking away, use console command `setstage TG08A 55`. This starts the cinematic sequence without Brynjolf, who will join the show slightly later.
- Karliah sometimes may not meet you at Nightingale Hall, making the quest impossible to finish.
  - Karliah will sometimes go back to the [Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth") where you have met to decrypt Gallus' journal. It is related to the bug in the quest [Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers") where the stages will not update. Redo Hard Answers step by step, and the quest Trinity Restored will reactivate.
  -  You can use the console and type `setstage TG06 60` and go to the cellar in the Frozen Hearth to talk again to Enthir and Karliah. After this Karliah and Brynjolf will be at the entrance of the Nightingale Hall. (You can further check if this is the problem by typing `getstage TG06` in the console. If the Stage is smaller than 200 then this is the cause of Karliah's disappearance). If setting the stage to 60 doesn't work, enter `setstage TG06 200` to complete the quest Hard Answers. Karliah will then begin her long trek to Nightingale Hall. Fast travel to the hall, wait for 24 hours and she will show up.
  -  Alternatively, type in the console `prid 00020545` (for Brynjolf) or `prid 00058F1A` (for Karliah), followed by the command `moveto player`. Use the latter command as many times as necessary to lead the selected NPC to the stones; you may need to activate the stone multiple times to get Brynjolf and/or Karliah to equip their Nightingale armors. You may still be required to use the command as you continue further down the halls. Do *not* use the `placeatme` commands on unique NPCs, as you will create a clone of the NPC which will cause undesirable results in-game - only use `moveto player`.
- Sometimes, Karliah will simply turn around and walk out of the cave instead of opening the gate. As she is the only one able to open it, this will render the quest impossible to complete.
  - After Karliah asks you to take the oath and is done talking, immediately wait 1 hour, this will allow her to warp to the chain and open the gate. Worked on my first try.
  - After Brynjolf accepts the terms of becoming a Nightingale, Karliah will ask you if you accept. Accept the terms, Karliah will then turn and head to the gate. Immediately interrupt her and ask her any question. This lets Brynjolf move ahead of her and fixes this bug. In some cases you might need to interrupt Brynjolf rather than Karliah and let her get to the gate first. This can be achieved by standing in his way.
  - Attacking Karliah may cause her to turn around and open the gate.
  - Exiting the conversation with her will allow the stage to reset itself, and may fix this.
  - Since the bug seems to involve the conversation with Brynjolf, you can sometimes circumvent the bug by talking to Brynjolf continually until Karliah opens the gate.
  - Allow the cell to completely reset and quickly run to the gate.
  - You can also fix Karliah from walking away if you tell her that you don't understand the full meaning of being a Nightingale. She will ask you again and then if you say you are ready, you can enter the room to finish the ritual.
  - Before accepting Nocturnal's conditions from Karliah, force her to and keep her directly at the gate using [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") and [Paralyze](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralyze_(spell) "Skyrim:Paralyze (spell)"). Accept the conditions and keep her at the gate until Brynjolf joins you both. She may then pull the chain and progress the quest.
  -  Open the console, click on the gate and use the command `disable`, then `setstage tg08a 52`. You can now see the cinematic involving Nocturnal. As with all console commands, exercise extreme caution.
  -  Karliah may be going to the exit instead of opening the door to the Nightingale contract. To repair this, use `disable` on the door, and use `disable` on Karliah and `enable` to fix her before using `moveto player` to teleport her to you. After that, use `setstage tg08a 52` and they may walk to their own spots.
  -  The same can be done as above only instead of disabling the door, it is possible to run `activate 58f1a` on the door (which simulates Karliah pulling the chain instead of removing the door from the game).
  -  Also, you can attack Karliah while she is talking to Brynjolf and use relenting force to move her to where the chain is. After, use Emperor's Voice to calm her down and then talk to her. She will then pull the chain and you can proceed. If you are not an imperial and do not have this power, you can use the command `/showracemenu` to change it to imperial and then change it back to your original race.
  -  If none of the above works, run to the gate while Karliah talks to Brynjolf. After they are done talking, open the console and execute the following commands: `prid 58f1a` and `moveto player`. This should teleport Karliah to you. If she doesn't start a conversation with you just talk to her. After you accept the oath she should now open the gate and proceed inside the chamber
  -  The following solution worked on multiple tries. After accepting the oath, run up to the chain by the bars and open up the console and execute the following commands `prid c6996`. Then execute `activate 58f1a`. That should simulate Karliah pulling the chain to bring the bars down. Run inside and then bring up the console again and execute `prid 58f1a` and then `moveto player` to teleport Karliah to you. Once you and Karliah are both inside execute `setstage tg08a 52` to progress the quest.
  -  Just go ahead to the gate and ignore them. After they have talked before the stairs, Use console move karliah near the gate opener and talk to her to progress the quest.
  - When presented with the choice to take the oath hit your Escape key to end the conversation. Use the command console, select Brynjolf, run to the previous room or the room before that and `moveto player` Brynjolf. Then run back to Karliah and accept the oath. She will open the gate, allowing the quest to continue. Brynjolf will join shortly.
- When you stand on the marker to summon Nocturnal, nothing may happen.
  - Move around a little until the cinematic begins.
  -  If the above fails, make sure you have exhausted all dialogue with Karliah and try again.
- After entering Nightingale Hall and donning the Nightingale armor, Karliah may pull the chain for the gate twice, when it should only be once. Because only Karliah can activate the chain, this can be problematic, trapping Karliah, Brynjolf, and possibly you inside or outside the cave.
  - Quickly talk to Karliah before she can pull the chain a second time.
- If you enter the cave with your followers, Karliah may stop before the bridge and not go any farther.
  - Have your followers wait outside.

## Quest Stages

| Trinity Restored (TG08A) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Before intercepting Mercer Frey, Karliah wishes to speak to both Brynjolf and myself. *Objective 10:* Listen to Karliah |
| 15 |  | *(Karliah initiates dialogue)* |
| 20 |  | Karliah has indicated Brynjolf and I are to meet her at an old standing stone just outside the Southwest Gate of Riften. Her motivations for doing so are mysterious, but I suspect it has something to do with the Nightingales. *Objective 20:* Meet Karliah at the standing stone |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Follow Karliah |
| 40 |  | Karliah has informed Brynjolf and I that we're to join the elite ranks of the Nightingales and assist in reforming the trinity that was disrupted over twenty-five years ago when Mercer Frey murdered Gallus. *Objective 40:* Activate the Armor Stone  *Objective 42:* Equip the Nightingale Armor *(once Brynjolf and Karliah have donned their armor)* |
| 45 |  | *Objective 45:* Follow Karliah |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Stand on vacant floor glyph |
| 57 |  | I've undertaken the Oath and I'm now a Nightingale, guardian of the Twilight Sepulcher and a dedicated sentinel of the goddess Nocturnal. |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Speak to Karliah |
| 70 |  | *Objective 70:* Speak to Brynjolf |
| 200 | ☑ | Karliah has finally revealed the fundamental mission of the Nightingales... the guardianship of the Skeleton Key of Nocturnal. This powerful artifact, normally kept safely within the Twilight Sepulcher, has been stolen by Mercer Frey. As a Nightingale, the duty to recover the Skeleton Key falls squarely upon my shoulders. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 25, 35, 42, 47, 52, 55.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TG08A stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TG08A`.

# Skyrim:Trouble in Skyrim

## Overview

|  |

| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") |
| Location(s): | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Kill the leader of the assigned location.
2. Return to Farkas.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This is a radiant quest given by [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") when asked for work.
Farkas has received a contract to clear out a troublesome area. The enemies you encounter depend on the location of the quest.
In order to complete the contract, you need to travel to the location and kill the leader.
The quest is randomized and repeatable.

## Radiant Options

The target location is randomly chosen from 118 possible locations, amounting to a majority of the [dungeons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") that contain boss-type enemies. The location will be limited to holds that you have previously visited, so early in the game you may only receive destinations within Whiterun Hold, but later in the game there are many more possible destinations. Possible types of locations are:

- A [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") Camp or Bandit-Occupied Fort: ([28 possible locations](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit Camps")) — *"Nothing but a bunch of lowly bandits. Cowards, who will take little effort."*
- A [Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") Crypt: ([17 possible locations](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Draugr_Crypts "Category:Skyrim-Places-Draugr Crypts")) — *"The restless dead. Not pretty, but if you don't stop them, they'll move on to the locals."*
- A [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") Hive: ([12 possible locations](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Falmer_Hives "Category:Skyrim-Places-Falmer Hives")) — *"The Falmer. There have been reports that they've been attacking people at night."*
- A [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") Camp: ([8 possible locations](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Forsworn_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Forsworn Camps")) — *"It's a problem with the Forsworn. Unpredictable, unknowable, and dangerous. Be careful."*
- A [Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") Camp: ([12 possible locations](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Giant_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Giant Camps")) — *"It's a clan of giants. The war is driving them out of their lands, and they've started attacking settlements."*
- A [Hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") Nest: ([11 possible locations](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Hagraven_Nests "Category:Skyrim-Places-Hagraven Nests")) — *"You'll be clearing a nest of those Hagraven things. I've never faced one myself, but I hear... disturbing things about them."*
- A [Spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") Grove: ([8 possible locations](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Spriggan_Groves "Category:Skyrim-Places-Spriggan Groves")) — *"Oddly enough, Spriggans. Usually they let alone, but for some reason, this particular grove isn't."*
- A [Vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") Lair: ([6 possible locations](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Vampire_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Vampire Lairs")) — *"Bloodsuckers. Vampires. Take every precaution. One bite, and you could end up as one of them."*
- A [Warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") Lair: ([17 possible locations](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs")) — *"Rogue wizards. I've never trusted magic types. The College is bad enough. Destroy them."*

(Note that the provided categories list all locations with the given type of occupant, including locations that do *not* have a boss-type enemy and therefore cannot be possible destinations for this quest).

### Reward

| Levels[†](#intnote_LevelNote) | Reward[‡](#intnote_RewardBug) | USLEEP Reward |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 100 | 100 |
| 10–19 | 150 | 150 |
| 20–29 | 300 | 200 |
| 30–39 | 300 | 250 |
| 40+ | 300 | 300 |

[†](#note_LevelNote)Level is based on when the player completed the previous quest (or level one for the first quest), not the player's level when receiving the quest or its reward.

[‡](#note_RewardBug)The reward amounts for radiant Companions quests do not progress as intended.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=20007))

## Notes

- If [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed, some radiant locations may be on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). If you are in Skyrim, you will not receive a quest marker pointing you to the quest location, but must travel to Solstheim first (at which point any quest markers you have to quests in Skyrim will disappear).

## Bugs

- Despite having dialogue and quest stages to send you to a [Giant Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps"), the quest does not have the correct conditions to select a Giant Camp as a destination. **?**
- If you clear Driftshade Sanctuary (or any of radiant locations this quest can get) prior to starting this quest, it may become uncompleteable. This bug can occur even if you haven't discovered the location to which the quest directs you.
  -  You may use the console to manually enable the next stage in the main companions quest line. First enter the command `setstage C01 0` then `setstage CR05 0` and then `setstage CR05 20` ; then speak to whoever who gave you this quest so you can finish this quest without doing it again. This seems to work, though other issues may or may not arise later (has not been thoroughly tested).
  -  You can also use the console command `setstage cr05 20` to manually progress the quest to the next stage.
  -  If you are using console commands, you should deselect the quest beforehand; if you do not, the quest may remain highlighted, leaving a permanent quest marker on your map.
  -  You may `resurrect` the bandits and kill them again.
- The quest is greyed out in the journal (completed) when you've returned to Farkas.
  -  The quest is switched to "completed" at a point outside of Whiterun as you return. (This bug is from multiple radiant locations.) Whether you fast travel or not back to Whiterun, the quest is "completed" but you can not accept further work as you are stuck on this particular quest.
  -  Use the console command `setstage cr05 100`. You will receive a reward and be able to ask for more work.
  -  Another solution is to load a save prior to taking the quest, decline it when offered, then take a quest from another Companion leader.
  -  On PC, you can also reload a previous save, then use the console command `prid 1A693` followed by `moveto player` in order to select Farkas and teleport him to your location. There you will be able to talk to him and turn in the quest as normal. He will then slowly walk back home but if you don't want to wait, you can travel back to the hall and use the exact same commands to teleport him back there.
- If the location of the quest is [Dimhollow Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Dimhollow_Crypt "Skyrim:Dimhollow Crypt") and you haven't started [Awakening](/wiki/Skyrim:Awakening "Skyrim:Awakening") yet, some of the dungeon is inaccessible, preventing you from killing the dungeon boss. **?**
  - Start [Awakening](/wiki/Skyrim:Awakening "Skyrim:Awakening") to gain access to the area and proceed completing both quests.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CR05 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CR05`.

# Skyrim:Trueflame (quest)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Restore power to the Dwarven Forge in [Fahlbtharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz") to restore a [powerful artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Trueflame "Skyrim:Trueflame").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Hand Kenro's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Kenro%27s_Note "Skyrim:Hand Kenro's Note") |
| Location(s): | [Fahlbtharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz"), [Old Attius Farm Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Attius_Farm_Cellar "Skyrim:Old Attius Farm Cellar"), [Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear"), [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") |
| Reward: | [Trueflame](/wiki/Skyrim:Trueflame "Skyrim:Trueflame") |
| ID: | ccASVSSE001\_QuestE |
| Added by: | [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal") |
| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | |  | **Concurrent** [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_(quest) "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)"), [Buyer Beware](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer_Beware "Skyrim:Buyer Beware"), [Careless Curation](/wiki/Skyrim:Careless_Curation "Skyrim:Careless Curation"), [Her Word Against Theirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Word_Against_Theirs "Skyrim:Her Word Against Theirs"), [Ashen Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Heart "Skyrim:Ashen Heart") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Concurrent | [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_(quest) "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)"), [Buyer Beware](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer_Beware "Skyrim:Buyer Beware"), [Careless Curation](/wiki/Skyrim:Careless_Curation "Skyrim:Careless Curation"), [Her Word Against Theirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Word_Against_Theirs "Skyrim:Her Word Against Theirs"), [Ashen Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Heart "Skyrim:Ashen Heart") | | |

Reforge the ancient blade of [Nerevar](/wiki/Lore:Nerevar "Lore:Nerevar")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. *(Optional)* Enter [Fahlbtharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz") Forge.
2. Locate all four [Fahlbtharz Forge Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz_Forge_Gem "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz Forge Gem").
3. Take the [Unenchanted Weapon](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Unenchanted_Weapon&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Unenchanted Weapon (page does not exist)") from [Hand Kenro Hlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Kenro_Hlan "Skyrim:Hand Kenro Hlan") at Fahlbtharz Forge.
4. Place the weapon and the four gems into the forge to obtain [Trueflame](/wiki/Skyrim:Trueflame "Skyrim:Trueflame").

### An Unenchanted Weapon

Finding any of the four Dwarven Forge Gems hidden throughout Solstheim or entering the Temple in Raven Rock and stumbling upon the [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_(quest) "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)") quest will begin this quest.

Trueflame is located in the Dwarven Forge in Fahlbtharz where [Hand Kenro Hlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Kenro_Hlan "Skyrim:Hand Kenro Hlan") will attack you. He is in possession of Trueflame, although it appears as an [Unenchanted Weapon](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Unenchanted_Weapon&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Unenchanted Weapon (page does not exist)") without the enchanted flames it traditionally bears. He also has a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Kenro%27s_Note "Skyrim:Hand Kenro's Note") giving direction, and a sample of [Pyroil Tar](/wiki/Skyrim:Pyroil_Tar "Skyrim:Pyroil Tar") which will be needed once you have all four Gems.

### Fahlbtharz Forge Gem Locations

The gems are found:

1. On the body of [Hand Kenro Hlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Kenro_Hlan "Skyrim:Hand Kenro Hlan").
2. On the body of the [buyer](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer "Skyrim:Buyer") after following the [Redoran guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard "Skyrim:Redoran Guard") during [Buyer Beware](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer_Beware "Skyrim:Buyer Beware").
3. In the armory in [Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear").
4. On the body of [Erden Relvel](/wiki/Skyrim:Erden_Relvel "Skyrim:Erden Relvel") at the end of the quest [Ashen Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Heart "Skyrim:Ashen Heart").

### Reforging the Blade of Nerevar

With the Unenchanted Blade and all four gems in hand, you must return to Fahlbtharz Forge and place the four gems within the forge's receptacles. You will then need to apply the pyroil tar to the blade and place it in the sword slot; doing so will complete this quest and reignite the weapon with a visually impressive [fire damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage") enchantment. Congratulations, you now possess [Trueflame](/wiki/Skyrim:Trueflame "Skyrim:Trueflame"), the legendary Blade of [Nerevar](/wiki/Lore:Nerevar "Lore:Nerevar").

## Notes

You must also complete all the other related quests in order to obtain the 4 [Fahlbtharz Forge Gems](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz_Forge_Gem%7C).

These quests are :
[Ghosts of the Tribunal](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_(quest)%7C)
[Her Word Against Theirs](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Word_Against_Theirs%7C)
[Buyer Beware](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer_Beware%7C)
[Careless Curation](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Careless_Curation%7C)
[Ashen Heart](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Heart%7C) (All previous quests must be completed to unlock the armory and the Ashen Heart quest)

## Bugs

-  The animations for creating Trueflame will cause the screen to freeze on the [Nintendo Switch](/wiki/Skyrim:Switch "Skyrim:Switch"). You need to close and restart the game to continue.
  - The easiest way to bypass this bug is by pressing A to insert the blade, followed immediately by waiting for an hour, skipping the animation that freezes the game.
  - This bug can be solved by going into sneak mode, then placing the Unenchanted Weapon and opening the character menu simultaneously. Without exiting the menu, press start and manually save the game. After that, exit both menus. If the screen is still frozen, close and restart the game, loading up the mid-animation save. After that, you should be able to take the Trueflame without issue.
- Sometimes the pyroil tar does not apply to the unenchanted weapon.
  - To fix this bug, try unequipping all apparel items then continue with the quest normally.
- If you add the gems to the forge and ignite the forge before inserting the unenchanted weapon, you may not be able to finish the quest normally. You can use the console to advance the quest, as discussed below, but you will still have the unenchanted weapon in your inventory, unless you also remove it with console commands. **?**
- The game may freeze if you perform the Trueflame ritual too quickly.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.1130, fixes this bug.

- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccASVSSE001_QuestE stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccASVSSE001_QuestE`.

# Skyrim:Truth Ore Consequences

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Retrieve an [ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quest Items") sample from [Filnjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar "Skyrim:Filnjar").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Hafjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Hafjorg "Skyrim:Hafjorg") |
| Location(s): | [Elgrim's Elixirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim%27s_Elixirs "Skyrim:Elgrim's Elixirs"), [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") |
| Reward: | Random potions |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1([Hafjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Hafjorg "Skyrim:Hafjorg")) |
| ID: | FreeformRiften17 |
| Suggested Level: | 1 |
| Difficulty: | Easy |

Head over to Shor's Stone.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Hafjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Hafjorg "Skyrim:Hafjorg").
2. Obtain an unusual [quicksilver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quest Items") sample from [Filnjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar "Skyrim:Filnjar").
3. Return the ore sample to Hafjorg.

### Helping out

Should you find yourself in [Elgrim's Elixirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim%27s_Elixirs "Skyrim:Elgrim's Elixirs"), commiserate with [Hafjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Hafjorg "Skyrim:Hafjorg") about how much she has to do at the shop. She will tell you that caring for her husband, [Elgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim "Skyrim:Elgrim"), is holding her back from getting things done; specifically running an errand to [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") to retrieve an unusual ore sample. Offer to fetch it for her:

:   **You've got your hands full, eh?**
:   *"I swear, if I wasn't around, Elgrim would forget to eat his meals. How we make any coin at all is beyond me. In fact, I need to arrange for someone to pick up an ore sample for me in Shor's Stone... goodness knows Elgrim won't lift a finger to do it."* Telling her that you could get it for her will have her say,
:   **I could get it for you.**
:   *"You would? Oh, that would be wonderful. Speak to Filnjar in Shor's Stone. He's got some sort of ore sample he wants us to identify and was willing to pay us well for it."*

### Shor's Stone

Sample of quicksilver

In Shor's Stone, seek out [Filnjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar "Skyrim:Filnjar") at his home and smithy. Let him know you are there for the ore, and after some derisive comments about Elgrim, he hands over a sample of quicksilver. He explains that he needs Elgrim to examine this particular piece as its discovery coincided with a strange invasion of [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") in [Redbelly mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Redbelly_Mine "Skyrim:Redbelly Mine"):

:   **I'm here for Elgrim's ore sample.**
:   *"It's about time; I sent them a letter weeks ago. That [Elgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim "Skyrim:Elgrim")... he'd forget his own pants if his wife didn't help him dress. Here you go. Tell Hafjorg that she can chip off whatever she thinks is a fair trade for their time."*
:   **What's so special about this ore?**
:   *"Redbelly is supposed to be nothing but an iron mine. Been working it for years. Then right before the spiders had moved in, we found that chunk of ore. Never seen anything like it. I want to know what I'm dealing with before I start tearing it out of the ground."*

### Four Potions

Bring the sample to Hafjorg. She makes a sarcastic comment about her husband's busy schedule, but had him make you four leveled [skill](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") potions to compensate you for your travel:

:   **I've brought the ore sample from Filnjar.**
:   *"Thank you. I'll be sure to get Elgrim to examine this as soon as his... busy schedule allows. Here, I had him make you a few things for all that travel."'*

## Notes

- The [ore sample](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quest Items") is a special variety of [quicksilver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore"); it cannot be used for [smelting](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter").
- Although Filnjar has apparently been waiting for a courier for some time, the quest can only be started through Hafjorg.
- While it is implied that the special ore is in some way related to the appearance of the spiders at the mine, this is never addressed or brought up again in any other quests.

## Bugs

- The quest incorrectly sets disposition for Filnjar instead of Hafjorg upon completion. Although Filnjar is also involved, these quests normally only raise the disposition with the quest giver.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.4, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=24400))

## Quest Stages

| Truth Ore Consequences (FreeformRiften17) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Obtain Ore Sample from Filnjar |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Return Ore Sample to Hafjorg |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 200, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften17 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften17`.

# Skyrim:Tumble Arch Pass

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |

Tumble Arch Pass

**Tumble Arch Pass** is a [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") northeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Giant "Skyrim:Bounty: Giant")**: Kill a problematic [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") for a bounty reward. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill the Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Giant_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Giant (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") by killing a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Walkthrough

Tumble Arch Pass

One [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") and one [mammoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") occupy the camp, which features the painted stones and mammoth ribs and skulls typical of giant camps. The camp has a large campfire and a pile of firewood with a dead [deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer "Skyrim:Deer") beside it. A [mammoth cheese bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Cheese_Bowl "Skyrim:Mammoth Cheese Bowl") is beside the fire, with three more to the west. Southeast of the fire against some rocks is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Above the camp on the rocks to the south is a large stone bowl containing three sprigs of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") and a [giant club](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Club "Skyrim:Giant Club") (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

## Notes

- Up the mountain southeast of the camp is a skeleton on the ground with a [shrine of Julianos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Julianos "Skyrim:Shrines") almost covered by snow and a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") nearby. This area is easier to reach from [Shearpoint](/wiki/Skyrim:Shearpoint "Skyrim:Shearpoint") to the south. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=70163&y=26768)
- Version 2.0.8 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces all [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") pieces here with the snow-covered version of the same plant.

## Bugs

- The giant club cannot be used by you, but can be picked up by a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") if you order them to do so. However, it will then be impossible to remove it from their inventory.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Tundra Homestead (place)

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |

Tundra Homestead

**Tundra Homestead** is a cottage that can be purchased in [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), located just northeast of [Battle-Born Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle-Born_Farm "Skyrim:Battle-Born Farm").

A note from the previous owner titled *[Homestead For Sale](/wiki/Skyrim:Homestead_For_Sale "Skyrim:Homestead For Sale")* is posted next to the door. The note directs you to the steward of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), either [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci") or [Brill](/wiki/Skyrim:Brill "Skyrim:Brill"), to buy the house for 7,500 gold.

The cottage consists of two areas, *[Tundra Homestead](#Tundra_Homestead)* and *[Tundra Homestead, Cellar](#Tundra_Homestead.2C_Cellar).*

## Related Quests

- **[Bandit Attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Attack "Skyrim:Bandit Attack")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"): Rescue your beloved from kidnappers. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Build Your Own Home](/wiki/Skyrim:Build_Your_Own_Home "Skyrim:Build Your Own Home")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"): [Construct](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") a house for yourself.

### Exterior

The property includes several outdoor features. Behind the cottage there is a garden with eight open plots of [Fertile Soil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fertile_Soil "Skyrim:Fertile Soil"), three [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") plants, two [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), two [gourds](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), and two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"). Nearby are two [apiaries](/wiki/Skyrim:Apiary "Skyrim:Apiary") that work the same way as the one at [Lakeview Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Lakeview_Manor "Skyrim:Lakeview Manor"). Two covered areas are in front of the house, and the one to the east has almost all the necessary [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") tools: a [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter"), [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), and [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"). The property itself does not include a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") (useful for [ammunition](/wiki/Skyrim:Ammunition "Skyrim:Ammunition") crafting), but those can easily be found nearby in both [Battle-Born Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle-Born_Farm "Skyrim:Battle-Born Farm") and [Chillfurrow Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Chillfurrow_Farm "Skyrim:Chillfurrow Farm").

### Tundra Homestead

Tundra Homestead interior

The large room you enter into features a fireplace on the opposite wall with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") and a baking surface that functions as an [oven](/wiki/Skyrim:Oven "Skyrim:Oven"). This room also contains several storage [safes](/wiki/Skyrim:Safe "Skyrim:Safe") and a copy of [*The Aetherium Wars*](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars"). The bedroom on the left contains a double bed and two single beds intended for children, as well as shrines to [Akatosh](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Akatosh "Skyrim:Shrine of Akatosh") and [Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mara "Skyrim:Shrine of Mara"). On the right, there is a smaller circular room with an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"), an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), and a [Shrine of Julianos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Julianos "Skyrim:Shrine of Julianos"). Notably, the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Game at Dinner](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Game_at_Dinner "Skyrim:A Game at Dinner")* and [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") skill book *[Enchanter's Primer](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanter%27s_Primer "Skyrim:Enchanter's Primer")* are found next to their respective crafting stations. A [Bone Hawk Skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Hawk_Skull "Skyrim:Bone Hawk Skull") can be found next to the arcane enchanter. This room has a trapdoor down to the cellar.

### Tundra Homestead, Cellar

Tundra Homestead, Cellar

At the bottom of the ladder, you find yourself in a circular room similar to the top level. Directly ahead is a large trophy room filled with display cases, mannequins, weapon racks, weapon plaques, and holders for various unique items. Four display cases and two mannequins in the center take up the majority of the space. Starting on the left, there is a wooden board with places to hold all ten [dragon claws](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Dragon Claw"). Four mannequins, three display cases, and three weapon plaques cover the north wall. The east wall has two high shelves; one holds the five [bugs in a jar](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items#Bugs_in_a_Jar "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items"), [Torsten's Skull Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Torsten%27s_Skull_Key "Skyrim:Torsten's Skull Key"), and [Saerek's Skull Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Saerek%27s_Skull_Key "Skyrim:Saerek's Skull Key"), while the other holds the five [paragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Other_Unique_Items "Skyrim:Other Unique Items") from the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"), [Auriel's Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Auriel's Shield"), and the [Initiate's Ewer](/wiki/Skyrim:Initiate%27s_Ewer "Skyrim:Initiate's Ewer"). Between these two shelves is a set of busts to hold all of the [dragon priest masks](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest_Mask "Skyrim:Dragon Priest Mask") except [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(item) "Skyrim:Miraak (item)"). There are also weapon racks below the high shelves. Finally, the south wall is lined with four more mannequins.

## Notes

- The house contains many unique static objects, such as new paintings and decorative items.
- The exterior is close to several spawn points, which can result in attacks from [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragons "Skyrim:Dragons") and wild animals. A [World Interaction](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") spawn point is located on the road right beside the house.
- A [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") vein can be found outside. It is also present without the Creation installed.
- The exterior barrels and single small sack are not safe for storage.
- The stables are too small to put a horse inside, making them decorative only. note-these now are able to hold horses
- The house has the signature Whiterun Dragonhead decor upon the roof.

- potential bug? - Static Potato, Leek, Cabbage, Gourd in Garden area may not re-grow after being harvested,{needs verification i.e. is there a days past in game reset?} leaving the garden soil plots barren.

## Bugs

- This location is marked as undiscovered on your map from the start of the game.
- Spouses and children will not move to Tundra Homestead, but instead be stuck in place where you first told them to move there, or disappear from the game entirely.
- The [Golden Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Claw "Skyrim:Golden Claw") may fall off the wall each time you enter the cellar. This seems to happen because it's marked stolen.
  -  In the console, selecting the claw on the floor and then entering`setownership` can be used to fix this.
  - Another option is to store it in a container you own and have a no-crime follower take everything out of it, then take the claw from their inventory. The claw will be marked as stolen if you take it from its holder or drop it, and consequently it gets the red steal text when selecting it, but it won't actually be considered stolen until you take it from its holder ensuring it stays in place.
- The [Initiate's Ewer](/wiki/Skyrim:Initiate%27s_Ewer "Skyrim:Initiate's Ewer") will not sit on top of the cellar shelf where its stand is located, but will appear to clip halfway through the shelf or even float under the shelf upon subsequent visits.
- The [dragon claws](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Dragon_Claws "Skyrim:Quest Items") will not stay in a set location, and will float in front of the cellar display.
- A few books and a [Dwemer cup](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Cup "Skyrim:Dwemer Cup") on the desk to the right of the front door may fall off or fly across the room when the zone loads.
- The three barrels in the smithing area are not safe for storage.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.318, fixes this bug.
- The [Wooden Mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Wooden_Mask "Skyrim:Wooden Mask") or other dragon priest masks may become stuck inside of its bust instead of on top of it. The dragon priest masks may also not be placed properly on their respective busts. A possible fix is to position yourself next to the bust and look towards the wall, slowly drift your look towards the mask and the option to take it will show.
-  Mannequins downstairs will sometimes create previously equipped clothing and equip it, unequipping armor that was placed on it.
- The [greater soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Greater_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Greater Soul Gem") on display by the [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") will move, fall off the table, or fly across the room when interacting with the enchanter or loading the zone. There is a chance the [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem") will also move, fall off the table, and fly across the room too. **?**
  - Additionally, when interacting the enchanter, sounds of items colliding with one another or a surface may occur to the left of the enchanter, despite nothing moving at all.
- When interacting with the display items in the cellar, the game may freeze. **?**
-  Reinstalling the game causes all items stored in the Tundra Homestead to be lost. **?**

# Skyrim:Tusked Terror

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Slay Fangtusk.** |

| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Crustacean Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Crustacean_Extermination "Skyrim:Crustacean Extermination") | **Next →** [Private Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:Private_Lessons "Skyrim:Private Lessons") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Crustacean Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Crustacean_Extermination "Skyrim:Crustacean Extermination") | | → Next | [Private Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:Private_Lessons "Skyrim:Private Lessons") | | |

Tusked Terror

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read *[Bounty: Fangtusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Fangtusk "Skyrim:Bounty: Fangtusk")*.
2. Obtain an [Arctic Grayling](/wiki/Skyrim:Arctic_Grayling "Skyrim:Arctic Grayling").
3. Travel northeast of [Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow").
4. Place the grayling on the rock.
5. Kill Fangtusk.
6. Search Fangtusk for the [Vampiric Ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampiric_Ring "Skyrim:Vampiric Ring").
7. Speak to the steward of Windhelm.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This quest can be started after [Crustacean Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Crustacean_Extermination "Skyrim:Crustacean Extermination") has been completed by talking to Viriya:

:   **Know of anyone in need of fishing work around Skyrim?**
:   *"Of course. It's all in this note."*

She will hand you the [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Fangtusk "Skyrim:Bounty: Fangtusk"), read it and you will learn of a monsterous horker known as Fangtusk, which has been terrorizing fishermen north of Hollyfrost Farm.

You need to obtain an arctic grayling and then head northeast of [Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow") to a rock by water that has two skeletons lying next to it, place the arctic grayling on the rock and Fangtusk will emerge from the icy water.

Once you have killed Fangtusk, inspect his body and you will find [vampire dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust"), [vampire gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Gloves "Skyrim:Vampire Gloves"), and a [Vampiric Ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampiric_Ring "Skyrim:Vampiric Ring"), suggesting Fangtusk ate a vampire.

Take this ring to the steward of Windhelm and speak to them:

:   **Fangtusk has been slain.**
:   *"It's really dead, then? It may be dead now, but... where did it come from?"*
:   **An enchanted ring in Fangtusk's gut seems to have been the source of its power.**
:   *"You've done well."*

    :   **Travellers should be safe now. At least, safe from giant vampire horkers.**
    :   *"Thank you. Here, this is for you."*
    :   **Alright, I've held up my end of the bargain. Time to pay up.**
    :   *"Thank you. Here, this is for you."*

You will then be rewarded 200 gold.

## Bugs

- The bounty on Fangtusk may not be marked as a quest item, even though you need to read it to advance the quest.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.4, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Tusked Terror (ccBGSSSE001\_Misc\_Windhelm) | | |

Fishermen have learned that it seems to enjoy arctic grayling above all other fish. I should obtain an arctic grayling and leave it near its feeding grounds in order to lure it out. *Objective 0:* Obtain an arctic grayling  *Objective 10:* Place an arctic grayling at Fangtusk's feeding grounds |

| 70 |  | After slaying Fangtusk, I discovered the remains of a vampire inside its gut, along with an enchanted vampiric ring. I should show the Jarl's steward the ring as proof that the deed is done. *Objective 80:* Speak to <Alias=Steward> in Windhelm |
| 200 | ☑ | I showed the vampiric ring taken from Fangtusk to Jarl of Windhelm's steward, who rewarded me for fulfilling the bounty. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Misc_Windhelm stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Misc_Windhelm`.

# Skyrim:Tutorials

## Overview

These **tutorial** quests provide a way to learn about the three crafting [skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") ([Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy"), [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting"), [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing")). They are available from a few [NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"), [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), and [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") near the game's starting point. The quest giver will show your character how to use the skills.

Note that you can use crafting skills without doing any of the tutorial quests, and the quests themselves do not give you any advantage in using the skills.

- **[Alchemy Tutorial](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Tutorial "Skyrim:Alchemy Tutorial")**: Learn the basics of potion making. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Blacksmithing Tutorial](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmithing_Tutorial "Skyrim:Blacksmithing Tutorial")**: Learn the basics of [smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Enchanting Tutorial](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting_Tutorial "Skyrim:Enchanting Tutorial")**: Use an [Arcane Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter").

# Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Ruin.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Ruin.png) | Nordic Ruin: Twilight Sepulcher ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Twilight+Sepulcher)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Twilight_Sepulcher "Lore:Twilight Sepulcher")) | | |
