## Related Quests

**Primary Quests**—quests that largely take place in the keep

- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.
- **[Bothela's Discreet Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela%27s_Discreet_Delivery "Skyrim:Bothela's Discreet Delivery")**: Deliver the [Stallion's Potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stallion%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Stallion's Potion") to [Raerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek") or [Reburrus](/wiki/Skyrim:Reburrus_Quintilius "Skyrim:Reburrus Quintilius").
- **[Buy Dwarven artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Buy_Dwarven_artifact "Skyrim:Buy Dwarven artifact")**: Bring your newly-obtained [Dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven "Skyrim:Dwarven") artifact to [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Coated in Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Coated_in_Blood "Skyrim:Coated in Blood")**: Bring a [Daedra heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") to [Moth gro-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Moth_gro-Bagol "Skyrim:Moth gro-Bagol").
- **[Compelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Stormcloaks)")**: Blackmail a [Talos worshipper](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek") into helping the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Deliver Spiced Beef to Voada](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Delivery to Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery_to_Calcelmo "Skyrim:Delivery to Calcelmo")**: Deliver a ring to [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo").
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Hagravens) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Hagravens)")**: Do a favor for [Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund"), the Jarl of Markarth, by retrieving a [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrolfdir%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Hrolfdir's Shield"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers")**: Help translate [Gallus's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallus%27s_Encoded_Journal "Skyrim:Gallus's Encoded Journal").
- **[If I had a Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:If_I_had_a_Hammer "Skyrim:If I had a Hammer")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Hammer "Skyrim:Stendarr's Hammer"): Steal a legendary hammer of the gods.
- **[Kill the Forsworn Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Forsworn_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Forsworn Leader (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") by killing a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[My Pet Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:My_Pet_Mudcrab "Skyrim:My Pet Mudcrab")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab"): Buy a [Dwarven Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab_(creature) "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab (creature)").
- **[Nimhe, the Poisoned One](/wiki/Skyrim:Nimhe,_the_Poisoned_One "Skyrim:Nimhe, the Poisoned One")**: Kill the giant frostbite spider blocking access to [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").
- **[Search and Seizure](/wiki/Skyrim:Search_and_Seizure "Skyrim:Search and Seizure")**: Find evidence of a [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") [worshipper](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund "Skyrim:Ogmund") for the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").

**Secondary Quests**—quests where only a portion takes place in the keep

- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").
- **[The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny")**: Find items for [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") throughout the [questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Primary_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").
- **[The Lost Expedition](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Expedition "Skyrim:The Lost Expedition")**: Recover the journals from the expedition in [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[Recipe for Disaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster")**: Assume the identity of the famous [Gourmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Balagog_gro-Nolob "Skyrim:Balagog gro-Nolob") in an effort to assassinate the Emperor.
- **[The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death")**: Prepare a [feast](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus") for the [Lady of Decay](/wiki/Lore:Namira "Lore:Namira").
- **[Thane of the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Reach "Skyrim:Thane of the Reach")**: Gain the title of [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Jarl's Palace

Igmund as Jarl on The Mournful Throne

The palace entrance is a set of dwemer gates leading to five sets of side-by-side stairs. This is where [Thongvor Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thongvor_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thongvor Silver-Blood") goes, and stays, after harassing [Brother Verulus](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus") about the closure of the Hall of the Dead when you first enter. The middle set of stairs leads directly to the entrance of the Jarl's throne room, while the other four—two on each side—ascend to the side of the throne room. Two inactive [dwarven centurions](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion") stand in alcoves on either side of the entrance, and two inactive [dwarven spheres](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere") flank the stairs. The Mournful Throne is the throne on which the Jarl of Markarth sits. Just below the throne is a stone chair for the Steward, while the housecarl stands on the other side of the room. There are two additional alcoves here, each containing a Dwemer chest.

From the throne room, the blacksmith's workshop is north, the general quarters and war room are northwest, the kitchen is south, and the Jarl's quarters are southwest. The layout of the area outside the throne room is symmetrical. First, there is a stone bench followed by a table with a single seat by the western wall; opposite the table is another table with two seats, and behind the pillar by the two-seat table is a Juniper tree. On the single-seat table between the throne room and the blacksmith's workshop, there is a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Daughter of the Niben](/wiki/Skyrim:Daughter_of_the_Niben "Skyrim:Daughter of the Niben")*. Between the throne room and the kitchen are the Jarl's two pet [dogs](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog").

[Ondolemar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ondolemar "Skyrim:Ondolemar") paces along the top of the stairs with two [Thalmor Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Soldier "Skyrim:Thalmor Soldier") during the day, in an attempt to influence proceedings when the Jarl holds court. He disappears if the Stormcloaks gain the city.

#### Jarl's Quarters

The Jarl's Quarters are quite large and opulent, and the doors are secured with an adept lock. The first cupboard on the right holds a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and the book *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")*. There is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") by the fire, and a leveled potion on the shelf next to the fire. There is an assortment of food items on the table, and some gold and a leveled necklace can be found on top of the dresser on the other side of the table.

Up the steps by the dresser is the Jarl's bed and a table. There is an end table at the foot of the bed, on top of which is a copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill book *[The Warrior's Charge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrior%27s_Charge "Skyrim:The Warrior's Charge")*, and underneath is a copy of the [Key to Markarth Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Markarth_Keep "Skyrim:Key to Markarth Keep"). The table holds a leveled dagger, some gold, and a [gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems") in a wooden bowl. An alcove between the bed and the table contains a shield, which will be replaced by [Hrolfdir's Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrolfdir%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Hrolfdir's Shield") if you have retrieved it for the Jarl.

On the other side of the dresser is an opening to part of the river running through the keep. If you edge around the pillar you will find a hidden stash of items: a chest, three coin purses, and a display case holding one [gold ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ingot "Skyrim:Gold Ingot") and two [dwarven ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Metal_Ingot "Skyrim:Dwarven Metal Ingot").

#### Kitchen

Anton at work

The kitchen is where the master chef [Anton Virane](/wiki/Skyrim:Anton_Virane "Skyrim:Anton Virane") prepares meals for the residents of the Keep, with help from his two assistants, [Rondach](/wiki/Skyrim:Rondach "Skyrim:Rondach") and [Voada](/wiki/Skyrim:Voada "Skyrim:Voada"). They also sleep in this area, though thankfully not where the food is prepared. An assortment of food items can be found on the corners of the corridor to the kitchen.

The western side of the first room is the food preparation area. Just to the right of the door is the staff dining table with three chairs. Strangely, one of the three chairs faces away from the table. By the fire is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") and a copy of *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")*. There are some shelves by the north wall, opposite which is a small larder. Throughout the area is a very large amount of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), particularly concentrated on the shelves and in the larder.

The eastern part of the room is Anton's. There is a small table with a single chair, and the raised section holds a [dresser](/wiki/Skyrim:Dresser "Skyrim:Dresser") and Anton's bed. Opposite the entrance is a second room which functions as both a storeroom and a bedroom, containing more food as well as two bed rolls for Rondach and Voada.

#### Blacksmith's Workshop

The workshop is maintained by [Moth gro-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Moth_gro-Bagol "Skyrim:Moth gro-Bagol"), who serves as the Jarl's personal smith. Despite serving in the Legion, he retains his position even if the Stormcloaks gain control. The two beds are used by Moth's sister [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol"), who runs the public smithy for Markarth, and her assistant [Tacitus Sallustius](/wiki/Skyrim:Tacitus_Sallustius "Skyrim:Tacitus Sallustius"). This leaves Moth with nowhere to sleep, so he works through the night; you can trade with him twenty-four hours a day.

The workshop is dominated by the [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") in the middle of the room. There is also, clockwise from the door, a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), a training dummy, a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), an armory table, a display rack, Ghorza and Tacitus's beds, and a cupboard. There is an [iron ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") on the workbench, a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") to the left of the tanning rack, and a war axe embedded in the training dummy's head. The armory table and display rack hold an assortment of [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") and [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel") weapons and armor.

#### Living Quarters

The general living quarters are in the northwestern corner and are off-limits to outsiders. The rooms are through the first doorway in the corner and to the right. Both doors have an adept lock, and a guard patrols from here to the war room.

The northern room belongs to the current Jarl's Housecarl. Just to the right of the door is a cooking pot, while on the other side is a stone shelf with some armor. There is a long table with a single chair, a wardrobe, an end table, and a bed. On top of the end table is a copy of the Key to Markarth Keep. The western room is the Steward's, and contains a bed, a dresser, a small table with two chairs, a cooking pot, and an end table. On the dresser is another Key to Markarth Keep and a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")*.

#### War Room

Straight ahead of the same entrance to the living quarters is a set of stairs; there is a potion on a shelf to the right, and the entrance to the war room on the left. There is a large stone table with a [civil war map](/wiki/Skyrim:Maps "Skyrim:Maps") surrounded by four stone chairs. On each side of the main table is another small table with a chair and an end table, as well as a single bed in the middle. There is a bow on the table with a keg, and the other table holds a helmet, a shield, and a Key to Markarth Keep. There is a novice-locked display case on the right-hand end table with two leveled ingots, one of a light armor material and the other of a heavy armor material. The bed belongs to [Legate Emmanuel Admand](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Emmanuel_Admand "Skyrim:Legate Emmanuel Admand"). Ondolemar spends the night here with his bodyguards, eating and sitting at the tables.

### Excavation Base

Nchuand-Zel

The Excavation Base sits at the entrance to an excavation site aimed at unearthing the history and any secrets of [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel"), a cavernous [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") castle carved deep into the mountain. The excavation is headed by Markarth's Court Wizard, [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo"), who is an expert on everything Dwemer, and who has also been placed in charge of curating all artifacts extracted from the ruin.

The base is in a huge hollowed-out part of the mountain, and contains the entire front entrance to Nchuand-Zel. Just to the right is Calcelmo's workstation, where he is aided by [Aicantar](/wiki/Skyrim:Aicantar "Skyrim:Aicantar"). There is an [Arcane Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), an [Alchemy Lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and a stone bench. The small area is flanked by two stone pillars containing some Dwemer items and Dwemer-related books. The pillar to the right also has a [Dwemer Museum Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Museum_Key "Skyrim:Dwemer Museum Key") on it.

To the extreme left, past a Dwemer construction, is Markarth's [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Markarth) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Markarth)"). The entrance to Nchuand-Zel is across a bridge just south of Calcelmo's workstation. There are no items to be found anywhere else in this area. The entrance to Nchuand-Zel is an example of the intricacies found in dwemer buildings and ruins, and can be used to see how each path seems to loop around on itself. The river flowing through the middle of the area is the one from the Jarl's quarters, and is the same river that flows through the center of Markarth.

## Dwemer Museum

The Dwemer Museum

The locked door to the Dwemer Museum is located up the stairs just north of the main entrance to the Keep. There is a guard at the top of the stairs who will warn you that the museum is off-limits. You will need Calcelmo's permission and a key to enter legally. There are a number of keys to be found; two notable keys are the one the museum guard has, and the one near Calcelmo.

There are three guards patrolling the museum. Two are around and near the central display, and the other is to the south of the central display. To the left of the pillar in front of the entrance is a shelf with some Dwemer dishes (bowls, cups, pans, etc.), while a shelf on the right contains some Dwemer construction items (levers, plate metal, scrap metal, etc.). There are four novice-locked display cases ahead, all containing Dwemer household items. Moving around the room to the right, there is an inactive [dwarven spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") on display, with nine [dwemer cogs](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Cog "Skyrim:Dwemer Cog") around the base. There is a shelf and a novice-locked display case to the right with construction items, and some construction items and an expert-locked display case containing a [dwarven dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger") can be found by the inner pillar; these items include eleven more cogs. The outer wall displays a working example of a dwemer mechanism. With the [Stendarr's Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Hammer "Skyrim:Stendarr's Hammer") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, this is the room where you will find [Stendarr's Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Hammer_(item) "Skyrim:Stendarr's Hammer (item)"), lying on a stone display pedestal in the corner.

The next section is a display area for items found on the current inhabitants of Dwemer ruins, the [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"). There are three display cases—one apprentice-locked and two adept-locked—containing a sword, a war axe, a bow, arrows, a shield, and a club, all of which are of Falmer make. On the shelf is an empty Falmer chest, two glowing mushrooms, and a Falmer club. Outside this section is an adept-locked display case containing three Falmer-related books. Next, there are some Dwemer shelves and a Dwemer dresser, all containing household items. There is a corridor in the wall opposite leading to a storage area with an adept-locked gate. There is a Dwemer [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") straight ahead, which activates some [spinning blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Blades "Skyrim:Spinning Blades"). The room contains a random assortment of Dwemer items, food, and other [miscellaneous items](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items"); there is also an apprentice-locked Dwemer chest on the second floor.

Back in the main room and around the corner is an expert-locked display case with mixed Dwemer items and a [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") ingot and necklace. Across the opening is an apprentice-locked display case with mixed Dwemer items. The opening aligns with the corridor asending to the west to Calcelmo's Laboratory, which is adept-locked. By the next pillar is a loaded but inactive [Dwemer ballista](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Ballista "Skyrim:Dwemer Ballista"), and by the wall a broken spinning blade trap is on display. Down the steps there is a stone shelf with an assortment of Dwemer-related books, including the three books Calcelmo wrote. Past the shelf is an adept-locked display case with two dwarven ingots. There is an inactive dwarven sphere on display, along with an assortment of construction items and an expert-locked display case containing an [enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") dwarven sword. In the corner is a working example of dwemer central heating.

There is a room to the south with an expert-locked gate. Inside is a Dwemer dresser, an expert-locked chest, a stone table, and an [Unusual Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") on the table. Back by the entrance to the museum are two adept-locked display cases and three unlocked display cases on the shelves. The two locked cases contain some rare books, including the *[Chronicles of Nchuleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Chronicles_of_Nchuleft "Skyrim:Chronicles of Nchuleft")*, the ordinary version of *[Chimarvamidium](/wiki/Skyrim:Chimarvamidium "Skyrim:Chimarvamidium")*, *[Nerevar Moon and Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Nerevar_Moon_and_Star "Skyrim:Nerevar Moon and Star")*, and *[War of the First Council](/wiki/Skyrim:War_of_the_First_Council "Skyrim:War of the First Council")*.

The museum is centered around an inactive dwarven centurion. Around the pedestal are twelve expert-locked display cases containing one of each type of Dwarven weapon, including an extra sword, some arrows, the [dwarven sphere centurion arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere_Centurion_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere Centurion Arrow"), and also some pieces of Dwarven armor, including a set of boots, a pair of gauntlets, two helmets, and two shields.

Clearing out the museum before starting the Hard Answers quest has no effect, since the guards respawn. During the quest the only difference is that two guards will have a conversation by the first pillar about the extra guards drafted in by Calcelmo before moving to their patrol routes. Two additional city guards do appear during that quest.

### Calcelmo's Laboratory

There is a stone shelf straight ahead that holds a few Dwemer scrap items. Once you enter the main room, there is a room to the left which contains two random [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"). There is an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick") on the ground running from this room around the rubble in the main room to a locked gate. The large room is a mess, with mixed Dwemer items lying on the floor all around the room. Through the unlocked door to the west is a pillar with a stone table by each side. The four tables each have two stone chairs, and hold an assortment of Dwemer items. Past the pillar to the west is a room with four stone benches facing a broken pulpit. There is a guard that patrols around the benches, sometimes sitting at the table to the left. Behind the pulpit is another locked door. There is a room to the north that is ostensibly Calcelmo's, which implies the bedroom to the south belongs to Aicantar. Aicantar's room contains a single bed, an end table, a cupboard, and a fair amount of food.

Calcelmo's room is actually two rooms, with a short L-shaped corridor leading to it from the pulpit area. The first room has a Dwemer dresser and a cooking pot by the fireplace to the left, and a small round table with a single chair and a wardrobe to the right; there is a fair amount of food in this room. A short set of stairs opposite the wardrobe leads to the bedroom. The bedroom contains a double bed, an end table, two dressers, and two chairs. On the left-hand dresser are three scrolls (a [scroll of Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Firebolt "Skyrim:Scroll of Firebolt"), a [scroll of Courage](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Courage "Skyrim:Scroll of Courage"), and a [scroll of Candlelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Candlelight "Skyrim:Scroll of Candlelight")) and a leveled potion or poison. On the right-hand dresser is a small coin purse and an apprentice-locked display case containing the three books written by Calcelmo.

This is as far as you can go without doing the quest [Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers"). Everything that follows is described as when the quest is active, as this is the first time you will be able to access the below areas. All of the living guards from this point are wizard's guards who wear a full set of steel or steel plate armor, making them tough to handle as a group.

#### During the Quest

The [Spider Control Rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Control_Rod "Skyrim:Spider Control Rod") can be found on the table in the first room to the left of the entrance. It controls [Aicantar's Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Aicantar%27s_Spider "Skyrim:Aicantar's Spider"), which is present at all times in the lower Dwemer hatch to the right, though it will not emerge until the rod is lifted. [Aicantar's lab journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Aicantar%27s_Lab_Journal "Skyrim:Aicantar's Lab Journal") is also on the table, and provides some insight into the research and making of the rod and spider.

Look out for these dwemer trap triggers to aid your passage

The traps do reset, and can be used on the [wizards' guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Wizards%27_Guard "Skyrim:Wizards' Guard") that comes through the first locked gate. The gate can only be unlocked by the guard, which will always happen as a scripted event. The second door just past the gate is barred from the other side, so the guard phases through it rather than opening it, meaning you must take the long way around. The Markarth City Guard (who is replaced by a Stormcloak if Markarth changes hands in the Civil War, or as a result of Season Unending) does not respawn if killed beforehand, though a wizards' guard appears either alongside the city guard or on their own. The lock on the door behind the pulpit is changed to a master lock. Both wizards' guards carry a copy of [Calcelmo's Laboratory Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo%27s_Laboratory_Key "Skyrim:Calcelmo's Laboratory Key"), while another copy of the key appears on the table beside Calcelmo's bed.

#### Through the Locked Door

The door behind the pulpit opens to a short zigzag corridor that ends with a set of ascending stairs. To the left at the top of the stairs is a corridor guarded by two wizards' guards, who are discussing previous malfunctions of the mechanisms in the corridor. The corridor is fairly long, with two sets of alcoves, and in between each section there is a static spinning blade trap (a total of three). The two guards patrol along the sides of the corridor, while a third may be present on the other side, but does not venture into the corridor. The first alcove to the left contains a table with two pieces of leveled heavy armor, while the second alcove to the right has a master-locked Dwemer chest behind the Dwemer construction.

To avoid the guards, you must travel underneath them. Follow the path past the corridor to the west from the entrance and descend the ramps, turning right three times until you come to a corridor filled with a green mist. There is a potion hidden in the rubble at the bottom of the ramps. The poisonous gas is quite deadly, though luckily not flammable. Trying to cross in a single movement usually results in death, but there is a trick to crossing. To the north, before entering the mist-filled corridor, is a pressure plate which activates the vents which drain the gas. There are a further five plates strategically placed along the corridor to aid passage, with the additional bonus of being unaffected by the [Light Foot](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Foot "Skyrim:Light Foot") perk. You may want to pause at each plate to recover your health, and consider saving along the way. Characters with strong poison resistance will have little trouble crossing here, but will still slowly take damage, even at 100% resistance.

There is a city guard lying dead by the entrance to the gas-filled corridor, as well as a lootable skeleton straight ahead and a plate immediately to the right, and another guard between the skeleton and the plate. Dragging a guard's body onto a plate is an easy way to turn off the gas. Just before the next dead guard and skeleton there is a plate on either side. Through the arch and immediately to the left is another plate, then a third skeleton by the final plate to the right.

There is a ramp at the other end of the corridor, and at the top of the next ramp to the right is a [valve](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Valve "Skyrim:Traps") that activates the nearby spinning blades. The patrolling guards will be oblivious to the activated blades, and will walk right into them. Past the pillar with the blades is a door to the east which, through a few short linear corridors, leads to the wizards' guards rooms.

The first room is centered around a large square table with two chairs on a raised section of the floor. There is a guard patrolling from the door on the other side of the room to the room on the left, past another guard who is eating a meal. The table holds some food, and there are two inactive Dwemer spheres opposite the entrance. The dining room to the left has four tables, each with two seats, placed by the faces of a square pillar. There is another room on the other side, with a random weapon in the rubble to the left, and a lootable skeleton with a potion and a large coin purse nearby just around the corner to the right.

Through the double doors to the east is the section blocked by the barred door. Aicantar and up to three guards can be found in this room. At the far end of the caged section overlooking the room is a valve that activates a Dwemer ballista, which is aimed directly in front of the valve. The valve also activates a spinning blade and several flame spouts in the room, with the latter aimed both across the room and in a V across the viewpoint from the caged section. Strangely, the flame spouts are situated above head height, meaning you can walk under them. If you wish to keep Aicantar alive, he will panic and run from the room when the valve is activated, opening the barred door. Otherwise, choose your moment to activate the valve to decimate the guards, then move quickly to prevent Aicantar from leaving.

By the Dwemer light source is the gate and the steps down into the room. Straight ahead is a stone table with two chairs. On the table are two soul gems and a copy of *Lost Legends*. To the right is the table where Aicantar was sitting. On this table is a copy of the ordinary version of *Chimarvamidium*, the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") skill book *[Twin Secrets](/wiki/Skyrim:Twin_Secrets "Skyrim:Twin Secrets")*, and a Dwemer chest. There is an arcane enchanter under the valve. Farther along are two tables shoved together into one L-shaped table, and to the south is the [Dwemer Puzzle Cube](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Puzzle_Cube "Skyrim:Dwemer Puzzle Cube"). To the north of the L-shaped table is the barred door, while the door to the east leads to Markarth Wizards' Balcony.

### Markarth Wizards' Balcony

The Markarth Wizards' Balcony is a very small outdoor area which connects the laboratory and the tower. It is actually part of the Markarth city map space, and can be accessed via persistent rock climbing. To the left is a dead-end next to a waterfall. To the right, there are two flights of stairs. After the first flight, the one in front leads directly to the door to the tower, while another flight to the northeast leads to a barred window with a view of the center crag of Markarth featuring the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella") and the [Guard Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Tower "Skyrim:Guard Tower").

There is a path between the rocks, just to the left of the first flight of stairs, that leads to the main waterfall in Markarth. It is possible to "ride" the waterfall down to ground level, or with a bit of luck, drop down to the deep section of the water below. You will find two skeletons of unsuccessful jumpers in the water at the base of the waterfall, near one of which are two loose gold coins.

### Calcelmo's Tower

The tablet written in Falmer and Dwemeris

The door opens to a short corridor, with four tattered flags hanging from the walls. At the end of the corridor is a room with a raised platform. To the right is a set of stairs leading up to an overhang at the same level as the platform. There is another overhang on the opposite side, and a narrow catwalk on either side of the corridor to the entrance. To reach these additional areas, you may stand on the empty Dwemer brazier on the left at the end of the first overhang, and jump. The second overhang has only a smattering of Dwemer items. It is possible to jump up to the platform from both the stairs to the right and the second overhang.

To the east of this area is the normal path, which leads up a set of stairs and through a door to Calcelmo's research area. The room contains many items that hint at how Hard Answers should be continued. To the right of the door is a small table, behind which is an inactive Dwemer centurion. Straight ahead from the door is a T-shaped table with ten rubbings of various Dwemer items, while there are two leveled potions on the other side of the table in the taller of the two shelves.

To the left is a compact area containing, in order from the left, a set of shelves, a dresser, an arcane enchanter, an alchemy lab, and two more shelves, all around a medium-sized stone table. On the table is a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") skill book *[Chimarvamidium](/wiki/Skyrim:Chimarvamidium "Skyrim:Chimarvamidium")*, and between the enchanter and the lab are two petty soul gems. There is a hefty number of Dwemer items, [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal"), and [rolls of paper](/wiki/Skyrim:Roll_of_Paper "Skyrim:Roll of Paper") lying on and around everything else in the room.

Just to the left of the door to the north is an expert-locked Dwemer chest. Through the door is the raised platform with the tablet inscribed in Falmer and Dwemer. When the guards appear, they will talk for a moment, then split up to look for you. To give them the slip, drop down to the stairs, now on the left, continue up the overhang, jump onto one of the catwalks, and finally drop down to the exit door.

## Notes

- Most of Understone Keep will respawn after 10 days. However, the Dwemer Museum and Calcelmo's Laboratory never respawn.
- The content from chests close to jarl's throne is labeled as owned, so taking it means stealing it, until completion of **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim. Then content of chests becomes freely available.
- There is a "Danger" [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the bottom right of the door leading to the Dwemer Museum. This is due to the high number of aggressive guards inside.
- Although it appears to be in the same zone as the city of Markarth, you cannot fast-travel from the Wizard's Balcony. You can, however, jump down from the narrow waterfall path below Calcelmo's Tower to the city proper and fast-travel from there.
- With 33 locks (gates, chests, and display cases), the Dwemer Museum is probably the best training place in Skyrim for practicing your Lockpicking skill.

## Bugs

- Fast travelling to Understone Keep can cause one of the guards outside to be flung up into the air, then plummet to his death. **?**
- Even though you should be able to enter the museum freely after you have been given the key, you might in fact still be considered trespassing.
- It is possible that a follower may refuse to talk to you while in Calcelmo's Laboratory, since they believe you are trespassing. This is problematic, as they will not follow you out of the room, and will remain "stuck" there. **?**
  - To fix this bug, draw a weapon and damage your follower until they leave your service. They will then leave the Laboratory on their own volition. Once they're outside, you can ask them to follow you once again.
  -  An alternate fix is to bring up the console while in the museum and click on your follower. Leave the museum, then reopen the console, type `moveto player`, and press enter.
- Ondolemar may become hostile to you on sight, which will also cause his two attendant Thalmor soldiers to attack, and may also cause the jarl and his court to turn hostile to you, even if you have no bounty in the Reach.
  - This may be caused by you attacking a random Thalmor party encountered in the wilderness (even if you kill all witnesses).
  - To fix this, reload a previous save and commit a minor crime, such as punching a Markarth guard, then clear the bounty using the usual methods.
- After escaping from Markarth Wizards' Balcony during Hard Answers, attempting to fast travel may cause the game to hang. This may be related to fast travel being disabled on Markarth Wizards' Balcony and not being properly enabled after escaping it. **?**
- The door that links the Dwemer Museum to Calcelmo's Laboratory is incorrectly tied to the Dwemer Museum Key, even though the laboratory is supposed to be off-limits.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, addresses this issue. The door is now properly tied to Calcelmo's Laboratory Key.
- The Thalmor Soldiers following Ondolemar will continue to respawn if Ondolemar dies or the Stormcloaks take Markarth.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
- Calcelmo's Tower is supposed to unlock during Hard Answers but doesn't.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- The guards in Calcelmo's Tower may accuse Aicantar of trespassing, even though he is Calcelmo's nephew.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, addresses this issue. They weren't assigned the proper factions.

# Skyrim:Unearthed

Ahzidal, the embittered destroyer

## Quick Walkthrough

1. *(Optional)* Read *[Ahzidal's Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Descent "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Descent")*.
2. Investigate [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow") and speak to [Ralis Sedarys](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralis_Sedarys "Skyrim:Ralis Sedarys").
3. Agree to help Ralis fund his excavation by donating 1,000 gold and wait for a message from him.
4. Visit Kolbjorn Barrow and defeat the [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr").
5. Find a way deeper into the barrow, and then speak to Ralis again.
6. Donate 2,000 gold to fund the excavation of Kolbjorn Barrow and wait for another message from Ralis.
7. Return to Kolbjorn Barrow, clear the draugr, and search for missing [miners](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner "Skyrim:Miner").
8. Speak to Ralis, fund 3,000 gold to his excavation, and await another message.
9. Return to Kolbjorn Barrow and clear the draugr.
10. Speak to Ralis, fund 5,000 gold to his excavation, and await another message.
11. Return to Kolbjorn Barrow and locate Ralis.
12. Defeat [Ahzidal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal_(creature) "Skyrim:Ahzidal (creature)") and confront Ralis; decide what to do with him.

### A Strange Partnership

Just northeast of the [Old Attius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Attius_Farm "Skyrim:Old Attius Farm") is [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow"). Outside Kolbjorn Barrow is a lone Dunmer named [Ralis Sedarys](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralis_Sedarys "Skyrim:Ralis Sedarys"). Go up and talk to him and he'll explain that he is a treasure hunter and has come with news that he has located a treasure in the barrow, but he cannot afford to excavate it alone and requests a donation of 1,000 gold, with a promise of a share of any treasure discovered.

### First Visit

A few days after you give him the money, a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") will give you [a note](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Ralis_Sedarys "Skyrim:Letter from Ralis Sedarys") about the barrow. Head off over to the barrow, and Ralis will explain that the [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") have been disturbed, and they have killed all the [miners](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner "Skyrim:Miner"). He asks you to go in and kill the draugr and then find a way further into the barrow. After you have killed the draugr, take the [Skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Skull (Dragonborn)") off the altar to open the next area, Go into the next room and pick up the [Ahzidal's Boots of Waterwalking](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Boots_of_Waterwalking "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Boots of Waterwalking"). (If the skull has been knocked off the pressure plate on the altar during the fight it must be lifted back onto the plinth and removed once more, or you can "walk" onto it and off by getting on the altar). Go back and talk to Ralis. He'll then ask for 2,000 gold to hire some more miners.

### Second Visit

Several days afterward you'll get [another note](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Ralis_Sedarys_2 "Skyrim:Letter from Ralis Sedarys 2") asking you to come back to the barrow. There are more draugr and two of the miners are missing. He asks that you locate the [missing](/wiki/Skyrim:Bradyn "Skyrim:Bradyn") [miners](/wiki/Skyrim:Mireli "Skyrim:Mireli") and to kill the remaining draugr. Before you get to Mireli, there is a gate with 4 handles arranged vertically to the right of the gate. Do not pull the third (from the top), as it releases a dart trap. Pull the switches in the following order: first, second, fourth, first. In the last section of the mine near the corpse of Mireli is a handle (near the floor on the other side of the wall with candles, a soul gem and coins) that can be turned to reveal a secret room where [Ahzidal's Ring of Necromancy](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Ring_of_Necromancy "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Ring of Necromancy") can be found. Note that although you will hear the sounds of a nearby [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"), it will not be accessible until a later visit.

Ralis now wants 3,000 gold to hire some mercenaries.

### Third Visit

You will receive a [third letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Ralis_Sedarys_3 "Skyrim:Letter from Ralis Sedarys 3") a few days later, asking you to return to the barrow. When the courier delivers the letter, he will tell you *"Another letter from Ralis. He's starting to scare me a little"*, a portent of things to come. Ralis will tell a similar story as last time: that there are yet more draugr, and that this time they have killed all the [mercenaries](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Guard "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Guard") that he hired. Enter the barrow and kill the draugr. To access [Ahzidal's Gauntlets of Warding](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Gauntlets_of_Warding "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Gauntlets of Warding"), pull the chain to the right of the iron doors that lead to the staircase into the newly excavated section, then backtrack around the corner where they will be sitting on a pedestal that was previously unavailable. Then, head down the stairs, avoiding the trap, and kill the new draugr. When you reach the open chamber, you must ensure all the pressure plates are lit for the gate to open and reach [Ahzidal's Ring of Arcana](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Ring_of_Arcana "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Ring of Arcana"). (The [Light Foot](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak#Light_Foot "Skyrim:Sneak") perk does not prevent you from lighting the pressure plates.) The timing is a bit tight; if you can't get it, using [Slow Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Slow_Time "Skyrim:Slow Time") seems to work, or you can run along the joint between two rows of tiles, depressing both rows at once, for a total of three runs across the grid. You can also circumvent the puzzle entirely with [Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis"). A pit filled with deep water surrounds the plinth that the ring is on. At the bottom you can find a coin purse, a burial urn and a leveled battleaxe. Once you're done here, head up the stairs and back out of the barrow to talk to Ralis who now wants 5,000 more gold. He will then send you [one last note](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Ralis_Sedarys_4 "Skyrim:Letter from Ralis Sedarys 4"), which simply reads "You're needed."

### A Poor Investment

When you get the final note, return to the barrow and look for clues at the camp, then head into the barrow and clear it out. You are finally able to reach the word wall which teaches a word for the [Cyclone](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyclone "Skyrim:Cyclone") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). On reaching the room with all the pressure plates on the floor, follow the passage to the left. A gate will close behind you will have to fight three draugr. The gate blocking access to [Ahzidal's Armor of Retribution](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Armor_of_Retribution "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Armor of Retribution") can be opened by rotating the two animal totem pillars until the whale symbols are facing you, then pulling the lever on the floor. Rotate the two animal totem pillars until the eagle symbols are facing you and pull the lever on the floor again to open the gate you came in, and the gate over the spiral staircase. At the bottom of the staircase, the gate blocking access to [Ahzidal's Helm of Vision](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Helm_of_Vision "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Helm of Vision") can be opened by rotating the two animal totem pillars until the snake symbols are facing you, then pulling the chain next to the door. There is a giant pool of oil encompassing almost the entire room, so it is recommended that you intentionally ignite it safely from the staircase as pulling the chain with an incorrect pillar arrangement will cause several [flame spout traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap") to blast the area in front of the gate. Removing the helm from its pedestal will activate another flame spout trap that is aimed back towards the gate. You may use Telekinesis again, but the flame jet will still travel far enough to ignite the oil. There is a [Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") source to the left of the helm chamber.

After battling several leveled draugr, you will eventually find Ralis completing the ritual to awaken a [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") named [Ahzidal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal_(creature) "Skyrim:Ahzidal (creature)"). Defeat Ahzidal, loot his eponymous [mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal_(item) "Skyrim:Ahzidal (item)"), then speak to Ralis, who will explain that he was under a spell. You can then choose to kill him or let him live, in which case he will become available as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"). If you kill him, you may loot [Hoarfrost](/wiki/Skyrim:Hoarfrost "Skyrim:Hoarfrost"), a unique ancient Nordic pickaxe, from his corpse. You can also take it from him if you spare him.

You can find the Black Book *[Filament and Filigree](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Filament_and_Filigree_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Filament and Filigree (book)")* at the end of the exit tunnel.

## Notes

- In total you will require 11,000 gold to complete the excavation.
- The time between each investment and the next courier message is three full days (72 hours).
- If you visit between messages, there will be miners and possibly guards working. They have generic dialogue reflecting the current state of the quest.
- Throughout the quest, a series of [journals](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Journal_of_Ralis_Sedarys "Skyrim:The Journal of Ralis Sedarys") can be found, giving insight into Ralis' state of mind. Take care when reading them as the disappearance of the camp will not occur if you take his journals from the camp prior to the final condition. They may also be stuck in your inventory permanently if you do so. The disappearance condition is *Filament and Filigree* is read and [Ahzidal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal_(item) "Skyrim:Ahzidal (item)") is got, the two actions' order doesn't matter.
- You can find Ahzidal's unique heavy armor set and rings:
  - [Ahzidal's Boots of Waterwalking](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Boots_of_Waterwalking "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Boots of Waterwalking") are available after the first phase of digging.
  - [Ahzidal's Ring of Necromancy](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Ring_of_Necromancy "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Ring of Necromancy") may be found after the second phase.
  - [Ahzidal's Gauntlets of Warding](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Gauntlets_of_Warding "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Gauntlets of Warding") and [Ahzidal's Ring of Arcana](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Ring_of_Arcana "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Ring of Arcana") can be acquired after the third phase.
  - [Ahzidal's Armor of Retribution](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Armor_of_Retribution "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Armor of Retribution") and [Ahzidal's Helm of Vision](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Helm_of_Vision "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Helm of Vision") become available after the fourth phase.
- The Ring of Arcana may not be on its plinth when you get to it—[shouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") from the draugr in the adjacent chamber can knock it into the pit of water. If this occurs, equipping the [Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis") spell can help you locate it (due to its longer range compared to the standard cursor).
- You may hear the chanting of the nearby word wall after the second phase has occurred, but you won't be able to access it until the fourth phase. You might be able to access it during the third phase if you stand close enough to the wall.
- The grate that opens to allow you to descend to meet Ahzidal on your final visit is controlled by the familiar pillars and is well-marked. The eagles on the opposite wall must be set on the corresponding pillars.
- The iron gate blocking the pedestal that holds Ahzidal's Armor of Retribution is not so obvious, however. As you enter the room, on the walls to either side there will be pull chains just to the right of an arch-way. If you pull the chains, this will activate rotating doors which will reveal that behind the arch-ways are two more pillars, each with the sign of the fish. The pillars behind the chairs need to be matched to these to open the gate and obtain the armor. Setting both pillars to the Eagle (and activating the lever) will open the door downstairs. The pillars here perform an uncharacteristic double-duty by opening two separate portals.
- The fastest way to complete this quest would be to commit a murder, and serve the jail time rather than pay a bounty. This will cause seven in game days to pass each time, allowing quick completion.

## Bugs

- Ralis may hire the miners, but never get anywhere with them - despite the passage of days (or even months), the courier never arrives, and when you check the dig site, they haven't reached the entrance.
  - Check the site once, talk to Ralis, then sleep in a bed on Solstheim for 24 or 48 hours. Repeat for each stage.
  - If the courier never arrives with Ralis' letters, you can bring him to you by bringing up the console, and typing and entering `prid 00039FB7` .
  - Then type and enter `moveto player`
  - Finally, you can talk to the courier to trigger his letter delivery dialogue.
- Upon entering [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow") for the second time, the door by [Mireli](/wiki/Skyrim:Mireli "Skyrim:Mireli") might drop down prematurely and lock you out of the room instead of locking down your retreat. Manually reopening the door will not help as it will just become an invisible barrier blocking your entrance. To reach Mireli and complete the quest, go back to the big hollow room and jump onto the platform. Alternatively, reload to a save before having entered the barrow for a second time.
- Upon entering [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow") for the fourth and final time, you are instructed to find [Ralis Sedarys](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralis_Sedarys "Skyrim:Ralis Sedarys") (stage 410). At some point before reaching the chamber with Ralis and [Ahzidal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal_(creature) "Skyrim:Ahzidal (creature)"), the quest may immediately progress to confronting Ralis (stage 475). It is possible that Ralis will be flagged as hostile towards the draugr and Ahzidal (or vice versa), and a brawl will ensue before you reach the chamber. Since Ralis is considered an essential NPC until you choose the dialogue option to kill him, upon reaching the chamber you will find Ralis chanting, as if to summon Ahzidal, but Ahzidal and the draugr are already dead. Approaching Ralis will trigger the normal dialogue (choose to kill or spare him). If he is spared, he will continue chanting as he runs away. He will still be chanting when approached at [The Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch").
- Once you finish the quest, the excavation site is supposed to clear up once you're far enough away. However, the script controlling this incorrectly polls the alias on Ralis when it should have been polling a static object at the site. This can result in the possibility that the registered update would fail to be renewed, leaving the quest open forever.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- Ralis' journals can be found on a table outside of the barrow excavation. Taking them after completion of the quest will permanently mark them as quest items, and it will be impossible to ever remove them from your inventory.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
  - You can remove the journals from your inventory by storing them in Ahzidal's ash pile, but they will still be marked as quest items.
  -  They may be removed via the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") by typing `Player.removeitem xx018108 1` and repeating for the IDs xx01810F, xx018110, xx018111, and xx0181CB. The *xx* on each ID will vary; see [this page](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID") for details.
- Ralis' journals can also be permanently marked as quest items if you complete the quest and leave the barrow without collecting the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Filament_and_Filigree_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Filament and Filigree (book)"). This glitch actually seems to depend on the passage of time. Completing the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Filament_and_Filigree_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Filament and Filigree (book)") quickly may cause the glitch to not be fixed. Waiting a few extra hours before leaving the dungeon should fix it. **?**
- Upon entering Kolbjorn Barrow for the third time, one of the draugr that you must kill may be outside of the map.
  - Leaving and reentering Kolbjorn should fix this issue.
- If you haven't picked up Ahzidal's Ring of Necromancy yet during the 2nd investment, it will disappear during the 3rd investment if you try to go back and grab it. It can be retrieved if you return to barrow after the third investment but before receiving the next letter. **?**
- If Ahzidal is killed as he rises from the ground, his corpse and ash pile may be below the ground and not lootable. **?**
- Upon entering Kolbjorn Barrow for the fourth time, the doorway leading to the lower section of the tomb may be blocked by rubble. Though this rubble can be walked through, as it has no collision, it can make it difficult to find where to go.
- At the second phase, you may find the third phase area accessible instead of being sealed off, allowing you to get Ahzidal's Gauntlets of Warding and the Ring of Arcana early.
- All of the generic miners present, both male and female, have "opposite gender animations" marked.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2dunKolbjornQST/DLC2dunKolbjornMiscQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2dunKolbjornQST/DLC2dunKolbjornMiscQST`.

# Skyrim:Unfathomable Depths

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Uncover the [memories](/wiki/Skyrim:Lexicon "Skyrim:Lexicon") of the Dwemer.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [From-Deepest-Fathoms](/wiki/Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms "Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms") |
| Location(s): | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") docks, [Avanchnzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanchnzel "Skyrim:Avanchnzel") |
| Reward: | [Ancient Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Knowledge "Skyrim:Ancient Knowledge") |
| ID: | MS04 |
| Required Level: | 14 |
| Suggested Level: | 16 |
| Difficulty: | Hard |

The Lexicon

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Accept the [Lexicon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lexicon "Skyrim:Lexicon") from [From-Deepest-Fathoms](/wiki/Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms "Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms").
2. Return the Lexicon to [Avanchnzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanchnzel "Skyrim:Avanchnzel").

### Memory Remains

From-Deepest-Fathoms wandering the Riften docks

Once you reach level 14, a female [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") named [From-Deepest-Fathoms](/wiki/Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms "Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms") will appear near [Riften Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery"), walking around in circles, manically talking to herself. When you approach her, she will tell you about a place called [Avanchnzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanchnzel "Skyrim:Avanchnzel") and an item she refers to as "the Lexicon": *"You. You must take the Lexicon. Free me of my burden."* When you respond, she merely continues: *"The memories. I cannot stand them. You must take them away, return them to Avanchnzel. You must take the Lexicon from me. Please... take it now."* She will not provide any explanations and will continue rambling until you accept. She then hands you a strange, ornately-decorated cube, and will walk away with the words: *"You must bring it to Avanchnzel, in the west. Return it to them. It must go back."*

### Four Thieves

[Avanchnzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanchnzel "Skyrim:Avanchnzel") is a large Dwemer ruin in southernmost Skyrim, in the [Jerall Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Jerall_Mountains "Skyrim:Jerall Mountains"), a long ways west of Riften and southwest of [Heartwood Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Heartwood_Mill "Skyrim:Heartwood Mill"). The exterior of the ruin is quite large, promising a lengthy journey within. The entrance itself is a cave-like opening in the cliff rather than a Dwemer-crafted stone door. Immediately upon entering, the hidden power of the Lexicon begins to awaken, and you will hear ghostly voices echoing through the tunnels. When you reach the first chamber, you will encounter four ghostly figures: [Drennen](/wiki/Skyrim:Drennen "Skyrim:Drennen"), [Breya](/wiki/Skyrim:Breya "Skyrim:Breya"), [Watches-The-Roots](/wiki/Skyrim:Watches-The-Roots "Skyrim:Watches-The-Roots") and [From-Deepest-Fathoms](/wiki/Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms "Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms"), the same Argonian who gave you the Lexicon back in Riften. The conversation between them reveals that Roots is the leader, while he and Fathoms have hired Breya and Drennen. Drennen is clearly the newcomer and is already worried about what lurks within Avanchnzel:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| ["It feels like we're being... watched."](/wiki/File:SR-quest-Unfathomable_Depths_03.jpg "\"It feels like we're being... watched.\"") | |  |  | | --- | --- | | **Drennen**: | *"I don't like this place. It feels like we're being... watched."* | | **Breya**: | *"It's a simple job, Drennen. We get in, we steal the Lexicon, we leave. Don't get jumpy."* | | **Fathoms**: | *"If you two cannot handle this, we can find others to hire."* | | **Roots**: | *"Enough. Their services will be more than adequate. Let us continue."* | |

The ghosts will then disappear without a trace. When you continue forward, you will notice a broken-down wall that leads into the actual ruin; clearly made by the ghostly adventurers. Inside the ruin, [dwarven spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") immediately attack, so dispose of them and proceed through the empty halls until you reach a door.

### Avanchnzel is Waiting

The next chamber is the central chamber, with multiple levels and bridges leading up to plateaus above. Two ghosts will be present on the bridge, the young [Drennen](/wiki/Skyrim:Drennen "Skyrim:Drennen") and the more experienced [Watches-The-Roots](/wiki/Skyrim:Watches-The-Roots "Skyrim:Watches-The-Roots"). Roots clearly did his homework and tells Drennen the purpose of Avanchnzel:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Drennen**: | *"This place is unbelievable."* |
| **Roots**: | *"Indeed. Avanchnzel is as much a library as it is a city. Built to hold the vast memories of the Dwemer."* |

*"Why are all these metal... things... ignoring us?"*

After this brief exchange the two ghosts will disappear, leaving you with two possible paths: east and south. Since the ghosts were heading south, pick that route and fight your way through numerous [dwarven spheres](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere") as the path twists and turns, leading down like a spiral. When you reach the large central chamber again, you will find yourself on the level below the bridge, and you will be attacked by four [dwarven spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider"). Make your way to the very bottom and check out the door to the south for a bit of treasure, then follow the map marker to the eastern door. Here, all four ghosts are present again, curiously staring at some buzzing [dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"):

|  |
| --- |
| **Breya**: *"Why are all these metal... things... ignoring us?"* |
| **Roots**: *"Anavchnzel*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *is waiting."* |
| **Breya**: *"Waiting for what?"* |
| **Roots**: *"No one seems to know. Perhaps the return of the Dwemer. Perhaps the end of the world."* |
| **Breya**: *"Best get rid of the ones we see. Just in case."* |

When the ghosts and the machinery are gone, proceed down the corridor. There is an unlocked chest with some minor loot near the shell of the left hand Dwemer sphere. Collect it if you wish and then enter the next zone, the [Avanchnzel Animoncultory](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanchnzel_Animoncultory "Skyrim:Avanchnzel Animoncultory").

### Accumulated Memories

*"I told you we should have hired a thief."*

*"Maybe we should turn back. I don't want to sleep here."*

In the first chamber of the Animoncultory, you will yet again encounter the ghosts, this time trying to break into one of the many hidden chambers of Avanchnzel. At this point, it is clear the place is starting to get to them:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Breya**: | *"I told you we should have hired a thief."* |
| **Fathoms**: | *"We are thieves, you fool. We're stealing the cube."* |
| **Breya**: | *"And yet none of us can pick a damned lock."* |

When the ghosts are gone, pick the lock for some minor loot, then proceed up the stairs and follow the tunnels to another large chamber with a tiny camp set up by the adventurers. Here, you will watch their growing frustrations with each other and the task at hand:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Drennen**: | *"This place is huge."* |
| **Roots**: | *"It is large, indeed. I did not anticipate Avanchnzel's size or the time needed to uncover the entrance. A few hours sleep and we should be ready to continue through."* |
| **Drennen**: | *"Maybe we should turn back. I don't want to sleep here."* |
| **Roots**: | *"Drennen, you do understand that the Lexicon at the bottom of this place holds the accumulated memories of centuries of Dwemer."* |
| **Breya**: | *"Not to mention our pay."* |
| **Drennen**: | *"So?"* |
| **Fathoms**: | *"So we're not turning back, you fool."* |
| **Breya**: | *"Besides, you're not scared of a few sleeping metal men. Are you, Drennen?"* |

Head east from the camping area and follow the tunnel as it turns north. Beware the booby-trapped door to the east, as the [spinning blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Blades "Skyrim:Spinning Blades") from the floor can kill you instantly. Turn around the corner and approach the northern side of the huge chamber with the camp. It contains a single dwarven spider, numerous dwemer artifacts on shelves, an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and some jewelry. From there, take the southern corridor, which leads one level down to another door. A dwarven spider and dwemer sphere guard the next room, and several locked doors lead to extra treasure. Keep moving in a western direction until you reach a chamber with yet another ghostly encounter:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Breya**: | *"I thought you said these things were "sleeping"?"* |
| **Roots**: | *"You said they were sleeping. I said they were waiting. It seems a few of them were "waiting" for someone to try and take the Lexicon."* |
| **Breya**: | *"Great."* |

Head down the southern corridor and open the door. A gigantic factory will appear before you, filled to the brink with dwarven spiders, as well as several dwarven centurions and spheres lying on tables, ready to attack if needed. With the exception of the spiders, none of them will attack, so locate the northern staircase and head down the slope to find the first evidence of what happened to the adventurers.

### The Lexicon

*"Drennen!"*

*"Soon the Lexicon's knowledge will be mine."*

At the foot of the slope, you will find the dead body of one of the ghosts: the young [Drennen](/wiki/Skyrim:Drennen "Skyrim:Drennen"). Around the corner, you will see the ghostly version of Drennen finally lose it and run towards you, disappearing exactly where his body lies. His final words—*"I can't do this. We shouldn't be here. I'm sorry."*—will be largely ignored by his companions, who, unaware that Drennen died just after turning the corner, will decide to move on:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Breya**: | *"Drennen!"* |
| **Fathoms**: | *"Let the field mouse run. Your pay will be double."* |
| **Breya**: | *"My pay will be nothing if we die in here!"* |
| **Roots**: | *"Calm yourself, Breya. We are closing in on the Lexicon. I can feel it calling. We'll continue without Drennen."* |

The three ghosts will then move on into the Avanchnzel Boilery, so follow them inside. There you will witness yet another conversation, where a seemingly-possessed Roots will claim he can hear the Lexicon calling:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Roots**: | *"We are close now. Can you hear the Lexicon calling out?"* |
| **Fathoms**: | *"Sure."* |
| **Breya**: | *"So we grab it and we get out, right?"* |
| **Roots**: | *"Once we have the Lexicon, we'll need to take it to its podium. I know what to do from there. Soon the Lexicon's knowledge will be mine."'* |
| **Fathoms**: | *"Ours. Soon the Lexicon's knowledge will be ours."* |
| **Roots**: | *"Of course."* |

### Unfathomable Depths

*"I can hear the Lexicon. Come on. Quickly!"*

The End of the Road

Walk down the pathway and through the steamy tunnel. A dwarven sphere will attack along the way, and you will encounter a dwarven spider sitting on a set of shelves, shivering. In the next room, you will see Roots, Breya, and Fathoms carefully approaching a door at the end of the room. The obsessed Roots will say:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Roots**: | *"We're almost there. I can hear the Lexicon. Come on. Quickly!"* |
| **Breya**: | *"Something doesn't feel right."* |

The three will then approach the door and Breya will shout, *"Wait!"* and Roots will cry out, *"Aaaaaaaaaaa...."* Behind the door, a set of [pressure plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") will transform the entire room into a deathtrap of nearly unavoidable spinning blades. At the bottom of the slope you will find [Watches-The-Roots](/wiki/Skyrim:Watches-The-Roots "Skyrim:Watches-The-Roots") dead, obviously killed by the blades. You can turn off the trap with the handle near his body, then open the nearby door for the final showdown.

In the last chamber, Breya's body can be found dead near the pedestal, killed by the dwarven centurion lying next to her. Impressively, she appears to have killed one of them before dying herself, no mean feat. Unfortunately, there was one more centurion in the room; it is likely responsible for her death. As soon as you approach the pedestal, it will activate, intent on making you its next kill. After the battle, locate the Lexicon Receptacle in the middle of the room and place the Lexicon on it. Once it is in place, behold the sight of power and memories as it opens. Your reward for following in the footsteps of some unfortunate adventurers is the passive effect [Ancient Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Knowledge "Skyrim:Ancient Knowledge").

To leave the ruin, open the western door; there is an unlocked boss chest in the darkness to your left as you approach the elevator, easily missed. Take the elevator up to the first zone, [Avanchnzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanchnzel "Skyrim:Avanchnzel"), and fight a few enemies. Locate the door with the wooden bar to the north and escape out onto the Avanchnzel Balcony, an exterior area that provides a breathtaking view over Skyrim. To the right is a locked Apprentice level chest containing minor loot.

## Notes

- Many leftovers show that in an earlier version of the quest, the Lexicon would not have been the important quest item. This honor would instead to go to the [Mnemic Egg](/wiki/Lore:Mnemic_Egg "Lore:Mnemic Egg") (an item that would later appear in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online")). There are two leftover activators; one is known as "Forge", with an internal name of `MS04Hearth`. The other is known as "Mnemic Egg", with an internal name of `MS04EggInForge`. These activators don't have unique models, and instead use random or placeholder ones for a floor sconce and a lever, respectively.
  - There is still a script known as `MS04HearthScript` used by the final game. Its name implies that this script would've made a specific animation available to put the Mnemic Egg in the forge, however, the final game repurposes it to hold the code for an animation for putting the Lexicon in its holder.
  - A line of script attached to stage 140 of the quest appears to reference this earlier storyline, it states `;Obsolete. The front gate scene was from a previous iteration of the story.`
  - There is a faction aligned with From-Deepest-Fathoms' personal faction, called "Agents of the Black Marsh", internally known as `MS04BlackMarshFaction`. The factions has two ranks, Agent and Assassin. At no point is this faction ever used for anything and no one ever becomes a part of it. It's unknown what its purpose was, but it may have been related to an earlier story iteration as well.
  - There is an empty dialogue view window known as `MS04GuardianGreet` still visible in the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), though it's unknown as to what "guardian" this refers to, as their dialogue doesn't exist.
  - Unused scripting in the quest would've given every member of the party a full set of Dwarven armor, although this never happens, and it's unknown what purpose this would've served.
- The cell `RiftenPlankside01` (where Fathoms usually wanders outside the Fishery), contains a multitude of markers that all refer to [Deeja](/wiki/Skyrim:Deeja "Skyrim:Deeja"): `MS04DeejaDocksWalk2`, `MS04DeejaDocksWander4`, and `DeejaDocksWalk`. These markers imply that either Deeja was at one point involved in the quest, possibly instead of Fathoms, or that Fathoms originally carried Deeja's name. Besides these markers, there's no evidence that shows that Deeja was in any way related to this quest.
- If you return the Lexicon before the Dwarven Centurion Master spots you, it will not attack you.
- You can pickpocket the Lexicon from Fathoms. The quest will activate as soon as it is in your possession even if you have not spoken with her, although your journal entries will state you having done so.
- If you return to From-Deepest-Fathoms in Riften after completion of this quest, you will find that she no longer has any unique dialogue. She doesn't react to your accomplishments in any way.
- At the very beginning of a flashback, ghosts are briefly visible like normal characters before turning into their intended, red spectral form. During this short interlude, they may react to your presence with generic NPC lines. They cannot be pickpocketed however, nor can they be harmed.
- You will need to level up via skill increases to or beyond the appropriate level for the quest to be eligible to start. You cannot be console-commanded to an arbitrarily high level and start the quest.

## Bugs

- A scene near the giant dwemer factory may be missing, since the trigger for it is located outside of the map: **?**

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Fathoms**: | *"The Lexicon had better be worth all this trouble."* |
| **Roots**: | *"I assure you, it is. The knowledge contained in the Lexicon created everything you see around you. Properly controlled, it has knowledge enough to turn paupers into kings."* |
| **Drennen**: | *"You sure that's power we're meant to have?"* |
| **Roots**: | *"Absolutely."* |

- Due to a spelling error in the game code, the final scene near the Centurion will never play as intended. **?** It describes the death of Breya and how Fathoms escaped:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Fathoms**: | *"I have the Lexicon! Where's the podium?"* |
| **Breya**: | *"I can't hold these things! We need to leave!"* |
| **Fathoms**: | *"I did not come all the way here just to walk out empty-handed."* |
| **Breya**: | *"The way out is right there! Run, damn it!"* |

- This scene was originally fixed by version 1.3.3. of the Unofficial Skyrim Patch, however, this was reverted by version 2.0.0., due to the changes actually breaking the scene further.
- Ancient Knowledge gives a 25% bonus while wearing *any* type of armor (not just Dwarven) and increases effective Smithing skill by 15% when tempering weapons and armor instead of giving a Smithing leveling bonus of 15%.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
  - This bug was supposed to be fixed with [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch") 1.9, but Bethesda erroneously required that the armor NOT be Dwarven, and didn't fix the Smithing error at all.

## Quest Stages

| Unfathomable Depths (MS04) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | A disturbed Argonian named From-Deepest-Fathoms was wandering the Riften docks. She wanted me to take something she referred to as a Lexicon back to Avanchnzel. |
| 100 |  | A disturbed Argonian named From-Deepest-Fathoms was wandering the Riften docks. She insisted I take the Lexicon she gave me back to Avanchnzel. *Objective 100:* Take the Lexicon to Avanchnzel |
| 900 |  | I've returned the Lexicon given to me by From-Deepest Fathoms *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* to Avanchnzel. |
| 1000 | ☑ |  |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 10:* Speak to From Deepest Fathoms *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 140, 150, 160, 190, 200, 210, 240, 250, 260, 290, 300, 310, 340, 350, 360, 390, 400, 410, 440, 450, 460, 490, 500, 510, 540, 550, 560, 590, 600, 610, 640, 650, 660, 690, 700, 710, 740, 750, 760, 800, 850.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MS04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MS04`.
